        const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
        for (const file of files) {
            const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
            const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
            if ((now - stats.mtime.getTime()) > oneDayInMs) {
                await fs.unlink(filePath);
                console.log(Deleted old file: ${file});
            }
        }
        console.log('File cleanup completed.');
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('File cleanup failed:', e.message);
    }
});

// --- Main Application Configuration ---
// Configure Helmet for stricter security headers.
app.use(helmet({
    contentSecurityPolicy: {
        directives: {
            defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
            scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
            objectSrc: ["'none'"],
        },
    },
    noSniff: true,
    xssFilter: true,
}));
app.use(cors(corsOptions));
app.use(morgan('combined'));
app.use('/static', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));

// Asynchronously initialize core engine modules.
(async () => {
    try {
        await rawrzEngine.initializeModules();
        console.log('[OK] RawrZ core engine initialized');
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('[WARN] Core engine init failed:', e.message);
    }
})();

// --- API Route Definitions ---

// Allowlisted cryptographic algorithms for validation.
const allowedAlgorithms = ['sha256', 'sha512', 'aes-256-gcm', 'aes-128-cbc'];

const checkAlgorithm = (algorithm, res) => {
    if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(algorithm?.toLowerCase())) {
        res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
        return true;
    }
    return false;
};

// Create a separate router for cryptographic endpoints with a smaller body limit.
const cryptoRouter = express.Router();
cryptoRouter.use(express.json({ limit: '64kb' })); // Cap crypto routes to 64kb
cryptoRouter.use(requireAuth);
cryptoRouter.use(apiLimiter);

cryptoRouter.post('/hash', body('input').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
        if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
        res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

cryptoRouter.post('/encrypt', body('input').isString().notEmpty(), body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        const { algorithm, input, extension } = req.body;
        if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
        res.json(await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, input, extension));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

cryptoRouter.post('/decrypt', body('input').isString().notEmpty(), body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        const { algorithm, input, key, iv, extension } = req.body;
        if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
        res.json(await rawrz.decrypt(algorithm, input, key, iv, extension));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

app.use('/api', cryptoRouter);


// Basic routes.
app.get('/health', (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, status: 'healthy' }));
app.get('/panel', (_req, res) => res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'panel.html')));
app.get('/', (_req, res) => res.redirect('/panel'));


// Network-related API endpoints.
// Note: These endpoints do not typically involve large JSON bodies, so the global JSON parser suffices.
app.get('/api/dns', requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('hostname').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        res.json(await rawrz.dnsLookup(String(req.query.hostname)));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

app.get('/api/ping', requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('host').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        res.json(await rawrz.ping(String(req.query.host), false));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});


// File management API endpoints.
app.get('/api/files', requireAuth, apiLimiter, async (_req, res) => {
    try {
        // Read directory and filter out the '.gitkeep' file
        const filenames = (await fs.readdir(uploadsDir)).filter(file => file !== '.gitkeep');
        res.json(filenames);
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('Error listing files:', e.message);
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

app.post('/api/upload', requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'), async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded or file type not supported.' });
    }

    const { originalname, buffer } = req.file;
    const uniqueFilename = ${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${originalname};
    const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, uniqueFilename);

    try {
        await fs.writeFile(filePath, buffer);
        await fs.chmod(filePath, 0o600); // Set file permissions to non-executable
        res.status(200).json({ message: 'File uploaded successfully', filename: uniqueFilename, size: buffer.length });
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('File upload error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to save the file.' });
    }
});

app.get('/api/download', requireAuth, apiLimiter, async (req, res) => {
    const fileName = path.basename(req.query.filename);
    const safePath = path.join(uploadsDir, fileName);

    // Prevent directory traversal
    if (!safePath.startsWith(uploadsDir)) {
        return res.status(403).end();
    }

    // Ensure the file exists before trying to download
    try {
        await fs.access(safePath, fs.constants.F_OK);
        res.download(safePath, fileName, (err) => {
            if (err) {
                console.error('Download error:', err.message);
                // The download method handles most errors gracefully, but we can log it.
                // It's not necessary to send a second response.
            }
        });
    } catch (err) {
        // File does not exist
        return res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found.' });
    }
});

// Final catch-all for errors. This middleware must be defined last.
app.use(errorHandler);

// Start the server on a dynamic port (or a specified PORT if set in .env).
const server = app.listen(process.env.PORT || 0, () => {
    const assignedPort = server.address().port;
    console.log(Server is running on port ${assignedPort});
});

Thought for 6s
rawr, this is 🔒almost perfect. Here are tiny, copy-paste patches to make it airtight—no refactors, just correctness + hardening.

1) Use fs.constants safely
You imported only promises, but call fs.constants. Split sync vs promises:

// replace this:
const fs = require('fs').promises;

// with this:
const fssync = require('fs');
const fs = fssync.promises;
Then wherever you check existence:

await fs.access(safePath, fssync.constants.F_OK);
2) Strong traversal guard in /api/download
Use absolute resolution and a precomputed root. Also validate filename.

// add once near your other consts
const resolvedUploadsRoot = path.resolve(uploadsDir) + path.sep;

// replace your /api/download with:
app.get(
  '/api/download',
  requireAuth,
  apiLimiter,
  query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.resolve(uploadsDir, fileName);

    if (!safePath.startsWith(resolvedUploadsRoot)) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied' });
    }

    try {
      await fs.access(safePath, fssync.constants.F_OK);
      return res.download(safePath, fileName, err => {
        if (err) console.error('Download error:', err.message);
      });
    } catch {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found.' });
    }
  }
);
Why: path.join(...).startsWith(uploadsDir) can be tricked; resolve + strict root check can’t.

3) Sanitize uploaded names + drop exec bits
Strip any path parts from originalname and lock permissions.

// in /api/upload:
const base = path.basename(originalname || 'file');
const uniqueFilename = `${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base}`;
const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, uniqueFilename);

await fs.writeFile(filePath, buffer);
await fs.chmod(filePath, 0o600); // owner read/write only (harmless on Windows)
4) Helmet: remove deprecated xssFilter
xssFilter is a no-op in Helmet v5+. Keep CSP + nosniff (already good):

app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"], // drop 'unsafe-inline' for prod if you can
      objectSrc: ["'none'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
    },
  },
  noSniff: true,
}));
5) (Nice-to-have) Rate-limit accuracy behind proxies
If you’re behind Cloudflare/ELB/etc., let Express trust the proxy so rateLimit sees real client IPs:

app.set('trust proxy', 1);
That’s it. With those tiny edits you’ve got: correct fs.constants, un-bypassable download guard, sanitized upload names, non-exec files, and clean Helmet. Want me to add opaque file IDs + short-lived HMAC download links next (still compact)?

    const token = process.env.AUTH_TOKEN || crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
    if (!process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
        console.warn([WARN] No AUTH_TOKEN found in environment. A new, temporary token has been generated.
          This will change on restart. Use the token below for authenticated routes:);
        console.log([INFO] Current session AUTH_TOKEN: ${token});
    }
    return token;

// Create uploads directory if it doesn't exist, handling potential errors gracefully.

        await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true });
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('[ERROR] Could not create uploads directory:', e.message);
        process.exit(1);
    }
};

// Multer configuration for file uploads. Files are stored in memory (multer.memoryStorage())
// and then written to disk in the route handler to ensure unique naming and permissions.
const upload = multer({
    storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
    limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, files: 10 }, // 100MB file size, max 10 files
    fileFilter: (_req, file, cb) => {
        const allowedTypes = [
            'application/x-executable', 'application/x-msdownload', 'application/x-sharedlib',
            'application/octet-stream', 'application/x-dll', 'application/x-exe',
            'application/x-elf', 'application/x-mach-o'
        ];
        const allowedExtensions = ['.exe', '.dll', '.elf', '.bin', '.scr', '.cpl', '.dylib', '.so'];
        const fileExtension = path.extname(file.originalname).toLowerCase();
        const isAllowed = allowedTypes.includes(file.mimetype) || allowedExtensions.includes(fileExtension);
        cb(isAllowed ? null : new Error(File type not supported: ${file.mimetype}), isAllowed);
    }
});

// Rate limiting middleware to protect general API endpoints.
const apiLimiter = rateLimit({
    windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
    max: 100, // Max 100 requests per 15 minutes
    message: "Too many requests from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes."
});

// Specific rate limit for file uploads due to their higher resource cost.
const uploadLimiter = rateLimit({
    windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
    max: 20, // Max 20 uploads per 15 minutes
    message: "Too many uploads from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes."
});

// CORS options, supporting a specific origin or allowing all in a controlled manner.
const corsOptions = {
    origin: (origin, callback) => {
        const allowedOrigin = process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN || '*';
        if (allowedOrigin === '*' || origin === allowedOrigin) {
            callback(null, true);
        } else {
            callback(new Error('Not allowed by CORS'));
        }
    }
};

// Middleware to require authentication via Authorization header or query parameter.
const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
    if (!authToken) return next();
    const token = req.headers['authorization']?.split(' ')[1] || req.query.token;
    return token === authToken ? next() : res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
};

// Global error handler for centralized error management.
const errorHandler = (err, _req, res, _next) => {
    console.error('[Unhandled Error]', err.stack || err.message);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
};

// File cleanup cron job, running daily at midnight to delete files older than 24 hours.
cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
    console.log('Running scheduled file cleanup...');
    const now = Date.now();
    const oneDayInMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    try {
        const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
        for (const file of files) {
            const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
            const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
            if ((now - stats.mtime.getTime()) > oneDayInMs) {
                await fs.unlink(filePath);
                console.log(Deleted old file: ${file});
            }
        }
        console.log('File cleanup completed.');
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('File cleanup failed:', e.message);
    }
});

// --- Main Application Configuration ---
// Configure Helmet for stricter security headers.
app.use(helmet({
    contentSecurityPolicy: {
        directives: {
            defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
            scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
            objectSrc: ["'none'"],
        },
    },
    noSniff: true,
    xssFilter: true,
}));
app.use(cors(corsOptions));

1) fs.promises vs fs.constants (runtime fix)

const resolvedUploadsRoot = path.resolve(uploadsDir) + path.sep;

    }

Why: path.join(...).startsWith(uploadsDir) can be tricked; resolve + strict root check can’t.

3) Sanitize uploaded names (strip paths)
Tiny hardening: avoid path smuggling via originalname.

// in /api/upload, before building uniqueFilename:
const base = path.basename(originalname || 'file');
const uniqueFilename = `${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base}`;
(You already chmod to 0o600 — nice work.)

4) Helmet cleanup (no dead options)
xssFilter is deprecated in Helmet v5+. Keep CSP + nosniff:

app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],

You added express.json({ limit: '1mb' }) to the GET /api/dns and /api/ping. They don’t need a body; you can safely drop that middleware there:

app.get('/api/dns', requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('hostname').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => { /* ... */ });
app.get('/api/ping', requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('host').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => { /* ... */ });

If you’re behind a load balancer/CDN, add:

const rawrz = new RawrZStandalone();

// Generate a random, cryptographically secure token if not specified in the environment.
const generateAuthToken = () => {
    const token = process.env.AUTH_TOKEN || crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
    if (!process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
        console.warn([WARN] No AUTH_TOKEN found in environment. A new, temporary token has been generated.
          This will change on restart. Use the token below for authenticated routes:);
        console.log([INFO] Current session AUTH_TOKEN: ${token});
    }
    return token;
};
const authToken = generateAuthToken();

// Create uploads directory if it doesn't exist, handling potential errors gracefully.
const createUploadsDir = async () => {
    try {
        await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true });
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('[ERROR] Could not create uploads directory:', e.message);
        process.exit(1);
    }
};
createUploadsDir();

// Multer configuration for file uploads. Files are stored in memory (multer.memoryStorage())
// and then written to disk in the route handler to ensure unique naming and permissions.
const upload = multer({
    storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
    limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, files: 10 }, // 100MB file size, max 10 files
    fileFilter: (_req, file, cb) => {
        const allowedTypes = [
            'application/x-executable', 'application/x-msdownload', 'application/x-sharedlib',
            'application/octet-stream', 'application/x-dll', 'application/x-exe',
            'application/x-elf', 'application/x-mach-o'
        ];
        const allowedExtensions = ['.exe', '.dll', '.elf', '.bin', '.scr', '.cpl', '.dylib', '.so'];
        const fileExtension = path.extname(file.originalname).toLowerCase();
        const isAllowed = allowedTypes.includes(file.mimetype) || allowedExtensions.includes(fileExtension);
        cb(isAllowed ? null : new Error(File type not supported: ${file.mimetype}), isAllowed);
    }
});

// Rate limiting middleware to protect general API endpoints.
const apiLimiter = rateLimit({
    windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
    max: 100, // Max 100 requests per 15 minutes
    message: "Too many requests from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes."
});

// Specific rate limit for file uploads due to their higher resource cost.
const uploadLimiter = rateLimit({
    windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
    max: 20, // Max 20 uploads per 15 minutes
    message: "Too many uploads from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes."
});

// CORS options, supporting a specific origin or allowing all in a controlled manner.
const corsOptions = {
    origin: (origin, callback) => {
        const allowedOrigin = process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN || '*';
        if (allowedOrigin === '*' || origin === allowedOrigin) {
            callback(null, true);
        } else {
            callback(new Error('Not allowed by CORS'));
        }
    }
};

// Middleware to require authentication via Authorization header or query parameter.
const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
    if (!authToken) return next();
    const token = req.headers['authorization']?.split(' ')[1] || req.query.token;
    return token === authToken ? next() : res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
};

// Global error handler for centralized error management.
const errorHandler = (err, _req, res, _next) => {
    console.error('[Unhandled Error]', err.stack || err.message);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
};

// File cleanup cron job, running daily at midnight to delete files older than 24 hours.
cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
    console.log('Running scheduled file cleanup...');
    const now = Date.now();
    const oneDayInMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    try {
        const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
        for (const file of files) {
            const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
            const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
            if ((now - stats.mtime.getTime()) > oneDayInMs) {
                await fs.unlink(filePath);
                console.log(Deleted old file: ${file});
            }
        }
        console.log('File cleanup completed.');
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('File cleanup failed:', e.message);
    }
});

// --- Main Application Configuration ---
// Configure Helmet for stricter security headers.
app.use(helmet({
    contentSecurityPolicy: {
        directives: {
            defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
            scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
            objectSrc: ["'none'"],
        },
    },
    noSniff: true,
    xssFilter: true,
}));
app.use(cors(corsOptions));
app.use(morgan('combined'));
app.use('/static', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));

// IMPORTANT: Apply general API middleware AFTER Helmet, CORS, Morgan, etc.
// The default JSON body parser for *non-crypto* routes should be present.
app.use(express.json({ limit: '1mb' }));
app.use('/api/', apiLimiter);

// Asynchronously initialize core engine modules.
(async () => {
    try {
        await rawrzEngine.initializeModules();
        console.log('[OK] RawrZ core engine initialized');
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('[WARN] Core engine init failed:', e.message);
    }
})();

// --- API Route Definitions ---

// Allowlisted cryptographic algorithms for validation.
const allowedAlgorithms = ['sha256', 'sha512', 'aes-256-gcm', 'aes-128-cbc'];

const checkAlgorithm = (algorithm, res) => {
    if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(algorithm?.toLowerCase())) {
        res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
        return true;
    }
    return false;
};

// Create a separate router for cryptographic endpoints with a smaller body limit.
const cryptoRouter = express.Router();
cryptoRouter.use(express.json({ limit: '64kb' })); // Cap crypto routes to 64kb
cryptoRouter.use(requireAuth);
cryptoRouter.use(apiLimiter);

// Mount the crypto router under the /api/ prefix
app.use('/api', cryptoRouter);

cryptoRouter.post('/hash', body('input').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
        if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
        res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

cryptoRouter.post('/encrypt', body('input').isString().notEmpty(), body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        const { algorithm, input, extension } = req.body;
        if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
        res.json(await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, input, extension));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

// COMPLETED decrypt route
cryptoRouter.post('/decrypt', body('input').isString().notEmpty(), body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        const { algorithm, input, key, iv, extension } = req.body;
        if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
        res.json(await rawrz.decrypt(algorithm, input, key, iv, extension));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});


// Basic routes.
app.get('/health', (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, status: 'healthy' }));
app.get('/panel', (_req, res) => res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'panel.html')));
app.get('/', (_req, res) => res.redirect('/panel'));


// Network-related API endpoints.
app.get('/api/dns', requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('hostname').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        res.json(await rawrz.dnsLookup(String(req.query.hostname)));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

app.get('/api/ping', requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('host').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        res.json(await rawrz.ping(String(req.query.host), false));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});


// File management API endpoints.
app.get('/api/files', requireAuth, apiLimiter, async (_req, res) => {
    try {
        // Read directory and filter out the '.gitkeep' file
        const filenames = (await fs.readdir(uploadsDir)).filter(file => file !== '.gitkeep');
        res.json(filenames);
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('Error listing files:', e.message);
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

app.post('/api/upload', requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'), async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded or file type not supported.' });
    }

    const { originalname, buffer } = req.file;
    const uniqueFilename = ${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${originalname};
    const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, uniqueFilename);

    try {
        await fs.writeFile(filePath, buffer);
        await fs.chmod(filePath, 0o600); // Set file permissions to non-executable
        res.status(200).json({ message: 'File uploaded successfully', filename: uniqueFilename, size: buffer.length });
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('File upload error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to save the file.' });
    }
});

app.get('/api/download', requireAuth, apiLimiter, async (req, res) => {
    const fileName = path.basename(req.query.filename);
    const safePath = path.join(uploadsDir, fileName);

    // Prevent directory traversal
    if (!safePath.startsWith(uploadsDir)) {
        return res.status(403).end();
    }

    // Ensure the file exists before trying to download
    try {
        await fs.access(safePath, fs.constants.F_OK);
        res.download(safePath, fileName, (err) => {
            if (err) {
                console.error('Download error:', err.message);
                // The download method handles most errors gracefully, but we can log it.
                // It's not necessary to send a second response.
            }
        });
    } catch (err) {
        // File does not exist
        return res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found.' });
    }
});

// Final catch-all for errors. This middleware must be defined last.
app.use(errorHandler);

// Start the server on a dynamic port (or a specified PORT if set in .env).
const server = app.listen(process.env.PORT || 0, () => {
    const assignedPort = server.address().port;
    console.log(Server is running on port ${assignedPort});
});
ChatGPT said:
rawr, this is super close. Here are tiny, copy-paste patches to make it airtight—no refactors, just correctness + hardening.

1) Use fs.constants safely
You import only promises but call fs.constants. Split sync vs promises:

// replace:
const fs = require('fs').promises;

// with:
const fssync = require('fs');
const fs = fssync.promises;
And when checking file existence:

await fs.access(safePath, fssync.constants.F_OK);
2) Strong traversal guard for downloads
path.join(...).startsWith(uploadsDir) can be tricked. Use absolute resolution + strict root check, and validate the filename.

// add once near your other consts:
const resolvedUploadsRoot = path.resolve(uploadsDir) + path.sep;

// replace your /api/download with:
app.get(
  '/api/download',
  requireAuth,
  apiLimiter,
  query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.resolve(uploadsDir, fileName);

    if (!safePath.startsWith(resolvedUploadsRoot)) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied' });
    }

    try {
      await fs.access(safePath, fssync.constants.F_OK);
      return res.download(safePath, fileName, err => {
        if (err) console.error('Download error:', err.message);
      });
    } catch {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found.' });
    }
  }
);
3) Sanitize uploaded names + drop exec bits (2-line harden)
Avoid path smuggling via originalname.

// in /api/upload:
const base = path.basename(originalname || 'file');
const uniqueFilename = `${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base}`;
(You already chmod 0o600 — perfect.)

4) Helmet cleanup (remove deprecated xssFilter)
xssFilter is a no-op in Helmet v5+. Keep CSP + nosniff; add img/connect if you need them.

app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"], // drop 'unsafe-inline' in prod if possible
      objectSrc: ["'none'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
    },
  },
  noSniff: true,
}));
5) (Nice-to-have) Accurate rate limiting behind proxies
If you’re behind a load balancer/CDN:

app.set('trust proxy', 1);
That’s it. With these micro-patches you’ve got: correct fs.constants, un-bypassable downloads, sanitized upload names, modern Helmet config, and solid limits. When you’re ready for a final polish, we can add opaque file IDs + short-lived HMAC download tokens so filenames can’t be guessed.

require('dotenv').config();

// Custom imports - assuming these are internal modules
const RawrZStandalone = require('./rawrz-standalone');
const rawrzEngine = require('./src/engines/rawrz-engine');

// --- Configuration and Setup ---
const app = express();
const uploadsDir = path.join(__dirname, 'uploads');
const rawrz = new RawrZStandalone();

// Generate a random, cryptographically secure token if not specified in the environment.
const generateAuthToken = () => {
    const token = process.env.AUTH_TOKEN || crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
    if (!process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
        console.warn([WARN] No AUTH_TOKEN found in environment. A new, temporary token has been generated.
          This will change on restart. Use the token below for authenticated routes:);
        console.log([INFO] Current session AUTH_TOKEN: ${token});
    }
    return token;
};
const authToken = generateAuthToken();

// Create uploads directory if it doesn't exist, handling potential errors gracefully.
const createUploadsDir = async () => {
    try {
        await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true });
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('[ERROR] Could not create uploads directory:', e.message);
        process.exit(1);
    }
};
createUploadsDir();

// Multer configuration for file uploads. Files are stored in memory (multer.memoryStorage())
// and then written to disk in the route handler to ensure unique naming and permissions.
const upload = multer({
    storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
    limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, files: 10 }, // 100MB file size, max 10 files
    fileFilter: (_req, file, cb) => {
        const allowedTypes = [
            'application/x-executable', 'application/x-msdownload', 'application/x-sharedlib',
            'application/octet-stream', 'application/x-dll', 'application/x-exe',
            'application/x-elf', 'application/x-mach-o'
        ];
        const allowedExtensions = ['.exe', '.dll', '.elf', '.bin', '.scr', '.cpl', '.dylib', '.so'];
        const fileExtension = path.extname(file.originalname).toLowerCase();
        const isAllowed = allowedTypes.includes(file.mimetype) || allowedExtensions.includes(fileExtension);
        cb(isAllowed ? null : new Error(File type not supported: ${file.mimetype}), isAllowed);
    }
});

// Rate limiting middleware to protect general API endpoints.
const apiLimiter = rateLimit({
    windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
    max: 100, // Max 100 requests per 15 minutes
    message: "Too many requests from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes."
});

// Specific rate limit for file uploads due to their higher resource cost.
const uploadLimiter = rateLimit({
    windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
    max: 20, // Max 20 uploads per 15 minutes
    message: "Too many uploads from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes."
});

// CORS options, supporting a specific origin or allowing all in a controlled manner.
const corsOptions = {
    origin: (origin, callback) => {
        const allowedOrigin = process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN || '*';
        if (allowedOrigin === '*' || origin === allowedOrigin) {
            callback(null, true);
        } else {
            callback(new Error('Not allowed by CORS'));
        }
    }
};

// Middleware to require authentication via Authorization header or query parameter.
const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
    if (!authToken) return next();
    const token = req.headers['authorization']?.split(' ')[1] || req.query.token;
    return token === authToken ? next() : res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
};

// Global error handler for centralized error management.
const errorHandler = (err, _req, res, _next) => {
    console.error('[Unhandled Error]', err.stack || err.message);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
};

// File cleanup cron job, running daily at midnight to delete files older than 24 hours.
cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
    console.log('Running scheduled file cleanup...');
    const now = Date.now();
    const oneDayInMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    try {
        const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
        for (const file of files) {
            const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
            const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
            if ((now - stats.mtime.getTime()) > oneDayInMs) {
                await fs.unlink(filePath);
                console.log(Deleted old file: ${file});
            }
        }
        console.log('File cleanup completed.');
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('File cleanup failed:', e.message);
    }
});

// --- Main Application Configuration ---
// Configure Helmet for stricter security headers.
app.use(helmet({
    contentSecurityPolicy: {
        directives: {
            defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
            scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
            objectSrc: ["'none'"],
        },
    },
    noSniff: true,
    xssFilter: true,
}));
app.use(cors(corsOptions));
app.use(morgan('combined'));
app.use('/static', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));

// IMPORTANT: Apply general API middleware AFTER Helmet, CORS, Morgan, etc.
// The default JSON body parser for *non-crypto* routes should be present.
app.use(express.json({ limit: '1mb' }));
app.use('/api/', apiLimiter);

// Asynchronously initialize core engine modules.
(async () => {
    try {
        await rawrzEngine.initializeModules();
        console.log('[OK] RawrZ core engine initialized');
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('[WARN] Core engine init failed:', e.message);
    }
})();

// --- API Route Definitions ---

// Allowlisted cryptographic algorithms for validation.
const allowedAlgorithms = ['sha256', 'sha512', 'aes-256-gcm', 'aes-128-cbc'];

const checkAlgorithm = (algorithm, res) => {
    if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(algorithm?.toLowerCase())) {
        res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
        return true;
    }
    return false;
};

// Create a separate router for cryptographic endpoints with a smaller body limit.
const cryptoRouter = express.Router();
cryptoRouter.use(express.json({ limit: '64kb' })); // Cap crypto routes to 64kb
cryptoRouter.use(requireAuth);
cryptoRouter.use(apiLimiter);

// Mount the crypto router under the /api/ prefix
app.use('/api', cryptoRouter);

cryptoRouter.post('/hash', body('input').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
        if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
        res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

cryptoRouter.post('/encrypt', body('input').isString().notEmpty(), body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        const { algorithm, input, extension } = req.body;
        if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
        res.json(await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, input, extension));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

cryptoRouter.post('/decrypt', body('input').isString().notEmpty(), body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        const { algorithm, input, key, iv, extension } = req.body;
        if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
        res.json(await rawrz.decrypt(algorithm, input, key, iv, extension));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});


// Basic routes.
app.get('/health', (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, status: 'healthy' }));
app.get('/panel', (_req, res) => res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'panel.html')));
app.get('/', (_req, res) => res.redirect('/panel'));


// Network-related API endpoints.
app.get('/api/dns', requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('hostname').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        res.json(await rawrz.dnsLookup(String(req.query.hostname)));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

app.get('/api/ping', requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('host').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        res.json(await rawrz.ping(String(req.query.host), false));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});


// File management API endpoints.
app.get('/api/files', requireAuth, apiLimiter, async (_req, res) => {
    try {
        // Read directory and filter out the '.gitkeep' file
        const filenames = (await fs.readdir(uploadsDir)).filter(file => file !== '.gitkeep');
        res.json(filenames);
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('Error listing files:', e.message);
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

app.post('/api/upload', requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'), async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded or file type not supported.' });
    }

    const { originalname, buffer } = req.file;
    const uniqueFilename = ${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${originalname};
    const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, uniqueFilename);

    try {
        await fs.writeFile(filePath, buffer);
        await fs.chmod(filePath, 0o600); // Set file permissions to non-executable
        res.status(200).json({ message: 'File uploaded successfully', filename: uniqueFilename, size: buffer.length });
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('File upload error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to save the file.' });
    }
});

app.get('/api/download', requireAuth, apiLimiter, async (req, res) => {
    const fileName = path.basename(req.query.filename);
    const safePath = path.join(uploadsDir, fileName);

    // Prevent directory traversal
    if (!safePath.startsWith(uploadsDir)) {
        return res.status(403).end();
    }

    // Ensure the file exists before trying to download
    try {
        await fs.access(safePath, fs.constants.F_OK);
        res.download(safePath, fileName, (err) => {
            if (err) {
                console.error('Download error:', err.message);
                // The download method handles most errors gracefully, but we can log it.
                // It's not necessary to send a second response.
            }
        });
    } catch (err) {
        // File does not exist
        return res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found.' });
    }
});

// Final catch-all for errors. This middleware must be defined last.
app.use(errorHandler);

// Start the server on a dynamic port (or a specified PORT if set in .env).
const server = app.listen(process.env.PORT || 0, () => {
    const assignedPort = server.address().port;
    console.log(Server is running on port ${assignedPort});
});
ChatGPT said:

Thought for 5s
rawr, you’re basically done—just a few surgical, copy-paste fixes to make this rock-solid and avoid some sneaky runtime gotchas. ✅

0) Delete the accidental duplicate file block
Your source includes a full second copy starting at the second line:

const express = require('express');
Remove everything from that second const express = … to the end of file (it redeclares modules and will crash with “already declared” errors).

1) Fix fs.promises vs fs.constants
You use fs.constants.FOK later, but only imported promises. Split sync vs promises:

// replace:
const fs = require('fs').promises;

// with:
const fssync = require('fs');
const fs = fssync.promises;
Anywhere you check existence, use:

await fs.access(safePath, fssync.constants.F_OK);
2) Strong, un-bypassable download guard
Use absolute resolution + a precomputed root. Replace your /api/download with this:

// put once near other consts:
const resolvedUploadsRoot = path.resolve(uploadsDir) + path.sep;

// replace the route:
app.get(
  '/api/download',
  requireAuth,
  apiLimiter,
  query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.resolve(uploadsDir, fileName);

    if (!safePath.startsWith(resolvedUploadsRoot)) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied' });
    }

    try {
      await fs.access(safePath, fssync.constants.F_OK);
      return res.download(safePath, fileName, err => {
        if (err) console.error('Download error:', err.message);
      });
    } catch {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found.' });
    }
  }
);
3) Sanitize uploaded names + keep files non-exec
Avoid path smuggling via originalname:

// in /api/upload, before building the filename:
const base = path.basename(originalname || 'file');
const uniqueFilename = `${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base}`;
(You already chmod 0o600—perfect.)

4) Helmet cleanup (remove deprecated option)
xssFilter is deprecated in Helmet v5+. Keep CSP + nosniff and add safe defaults:

app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc:  ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"], // drop 'unsafe-inline' in prod if you can
      objectSrc:  ["'none'"],
      imgSrc:     ["'self'", "data:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
    },
  },
  noSniff: true,
}));
5) (Nice-to-have) Accurate rate limiting behind proxies
If you’re behind Cloudflare/ELB/etc.:

app.set('trust proxy', 1);
That’s it—duplicate removed, constants fixed, traversal closed, filenames sanitized, and headers modernized. Next polish, when you’re ready: swap to opaque file IDs + short-lived HMAC’d download tokens so filenames can’t be guessed at all.

// Start the server on a dynamic port (or a specified PORT if set in .env).
const server = app.listen(process.env.PORT || 0, () => {
    const assignedPort = server.address().port;
    console.log(Server is running on port ${assignedPort});
});
ChatGPT said:
rawr, gorgeous progress. You’re a handful of surgical, copy-paste tweaks away from ironclad. Here’s the tiny delta:

1) Fix fs.promises vs fs.constants
You call fs.constants.F_OK but only imported promises. Split sync vs promises:

// replace your current fs import:
const fs = require('fs').promises;

// with this:
const fssync = require('fs');
const fs = fssync.promises;
Then update your existence checks:

await fs.access(safePath, fssync.constants.F_OK);
2) Make download traversal-proof (absolute resolve + validated query)
path.join(...).startsWith(uploadsDir) can be tricked. Use path.resolve + a precomputed root and validate filename.

// put once near your other consts:
const resolvedUploadsRoot = path.resolve(uploadsDir) + path.sep;

// replace the whole /api/download route with:
app.get(
  '/api/download',
  requireAuth,
  apiLimiter,
  query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.resolve(uploadsDir, fileName);

    if (!safePath.startsWith(resolvedUploadsRoot)) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied' });
    }

    try {
      await fs.access(safePath, fssync.constants.F_OK);
      return res.download(safePath, fileName, err => {
        if (err) console.error('Download error:', err.message);
      });
    } catch {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found.' });
    }
  }
);
3) Sanitize uploaded names (strip paths) + keep non-exec
Avoid path smuggling via originalname:

// in /api/upload:
const base = path.basename(originalname || 'file');
const uniqueFilename = `${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base}`;
const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, uniqueFilename);

await fs.writeFile(filePath, buffer);
await fs.chmod(filePath, 0o600);
4) Helmet: remove deprecated xssFilter
It’s a no-op in Helmet v5+. Keep CSP + nosniff (add img/connect if needed):

app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc:  ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"], // drop 'unsafe-inline' in prod if possible
      objectSrc:  ["'none'"],
      imgSrc:     ["'self'", "data:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
    },
  },
  noSniff: true,
}));
5) (Nice-to-have) Rate-limit accuracy behind proxies
If you’re behind Cloudflare/ELB/etc.:

app.set('trust proxy', 1);
That’s it—constants fixed, traversal closed, filenames sanitized, headers modernized.
When you want the deluxe finish, I can bolt on opaque file IDs + short-lived HMAC’d download tokens so filenames can’t be guessed at all, still in ~40 LOC.

You said:
const express = require('express');
const cors = require('cors');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const path = require('path');
const multer = require('multer');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const { body, query, validationResult } = require('express-validator');
const morgan = require('morgan');
const cron = require('node-cron');
const fs = require('fs').promises;
require('dotenv').config();

// Custom imports - assuming these are internal modules
const RawrZStandalone = require('./rawrz-standalone');
const rawrzEngine = require('./src/engines/rawrz-engine');

// --- Configuration and Setup ---
const app = express();
const uploadsDir = path.join(__dirname, 'uploads');
const rawrz = new RawrZStandalone();

// Generate a random, cryptographically secure token if not specified in the environment.
const generateAuthToken = () => {
    const token = process.env.AUTH_TOKEN || crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
    if (!process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
        console.warn([WARN] No AUTH_TOKEN found in environment. A new, temporary token has been generated.
          This will change on restart. Use the token below for authenticated routes:);
        console.log([INFO] Current session AUTH_TOKEN: ${token});
    }
    return token;
};
const authToken = generateAuthToken();

// Create uploads directory if it doesn't exist, handling potential errors gracefully.
const createUploadsDir = async () => {
    try {
        await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true });
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('[ERROR] Could not create uploads directory:', e.message);
        process.exit(1);
    }
};
createUploadsDir();

// Multer configuration for file uploads. Files are stored in memory (multer.memoryStorage())
// and then written to disk in the route handler to ensure unique naming and permissions.
const upload = multer({
    storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
    limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, files: 10 }, // 100MB file size, max 10 files
    fileFilter: (_req, file, cb) => {
        const allowedTypes = [
            'application/x-executable', 'application/x-msdownload', 'application/x-sharedlib',
            'application/octet-stream', 'application/x-dll', 'application/x-exe',
            'application/x-elf', 'application/x-mach-o'
        ];
        const allowedExtensions = ['.exe', '.dll', '.elf', '.bin', '.scr', '.cpl', '.dylib', '.so'];
        const fileExtension = path.extname(file.originalname).toLowerCase();
        const isAllowed = allowedTypes.includes(file.mimetype) || allowedExtensions.includes(fileExtension);
        cb(isAllowed ? null : new Error(File type not supported: ${file.mimetype}), isAllowed);
    }
});

// Rate limiting middleware to protect general API endpoints.
const apiLimiter = rateLimit({
    windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
    max: 100, // Max 100 requests per 15 minutes
    message: "Too many requests from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes."
});

// Specific rate limit for file uploads due to their higher resource cost.
const uploadLimiter = rateLimit({
    windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
    max: 20, // Max 20 uploads per 15 minutes
    message: "Too many uploads from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes."
});

// CORS options, supporting a specific origin or allowing all in a controlled manner.
const corsOptions = {
    origin: (origin, callback) => {
        const allowedOrigin = process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN || '*';
        if (allowedOrigin === '*' || origin === allowedOrigin) {
            callback(null, true);
        } else {
            callback(new Error('Not allowed by CORS'));
        }
    }
};

// Middleware to require authentication via Authorization header or query parameter.
const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
    if (!authToken) return next();
    const token = req.headers['authorization']?.split(' ')[1] || req.query.token;
    return token === authToken ? next() : res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
};

// Global error handler for centralized error management.
const errorHandler = (err, _req, res, _next) => {
    console.error('[Unhandled Error]', err.stack || err.message);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
};

// File cleanup cron job, running daily at midnight to delete files older than 24 hours.
cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
    console.log('Running scheduled file cleanup...');
    const now = Date.now();
    const oneDayInMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    try {
        const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
        for (const file of files) {
            const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
            const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
            if ((now - stats.mtime.getTime()) > oneDayInMs) {
                await fs.unlink(filePath);
                console.log(Deleted old file: ${file});
            }
        }
        console.log('File cleanup completed.');
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('File cleanup failed:', e.message);
    }
});

// --- Main Application Configuration ---
// Configure Helmet for stricter security headers.
app.use(helmet({
    contentSecurityPolicy: {
        directives: {
            defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
            scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
            objectSrc: ["'none'"],
        },
    },
    noSniff: true,
    xssFilter: true,
}));
app.use(cors(corsOptions));
app.use(morgan('combined'));
app.use('/static', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));

// IMPORTANT: Apply general API middleware AFTER Helmet, CORS, Morgan, etc.
// The default JSON body parser for *non-crypto* routes should be present.
app.use(express.json({ limit: '1mb' }));
app.use('/api/', apiLimiter);

// Asynchronously initialize core engine modules.
(async () => {
    try {
        await rawrzEngine.initializeModules();
        console.log('[OK] RawrZ core engine initialized');
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('[WARN] Core engine init failed:', e.message);
    }
})();

// --- API Route Definitions ---

// Allowlisted cryptographic algorithms for validation.
const allowedAlgorithms = ['sha256', 'sha512', 'aes-256-gcm', 'aes-128-cbc'];

const checkAlgorithm = (algorithm, res) => {
    if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(algorithm?.toLowerCase())) {
        res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
        return true;
    }
    return false;
};

// Create a separate router for cryptographic endpoints with a smaller body limit.
const cryptoRouter = express.Router();
cryptoRouter.use(express.json({ limit: '64kb' })); // Cap crypto routes to 64kb
cryptoRouter.use(requireAuth);
cryptoRouter.use(apiLimiter);

// Mount the crypto router under the /api/ prefix
app.use('/api', cryptoRouter);

cryptoRouter.post('/hash', body('input').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
        if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
        res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

cryptoRouter.post('/encrypt', body('input').isString().notEmpty(), body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        const { algorithm, input, extension } = req.body;
        if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
        res.json(await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, input, extension));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

cryptoRouter.post('/decrypt', body('input').isString().notEmpty(), body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        const { algorithm, input, key, iv, extension } = req.body;
        if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
        res.json(await rawrz.decrypt(algorithm, input, key, iv, extension));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});


// Basic routes.
app.get('/health', (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, status: 'healthy' }));
app.get('/panel', (_req, res) => res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'panel.html')));
app.get('/', (_req, res) => res.redirect('/panel'));


// Network-related API endpoints.
app.get('/api/dns', requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('hostname').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        res.json(await rawrz.dnsLookup(String(req.query.hostname)));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

app.get('/api/ping', requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('host').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        res.json(await rawrz.ping(String(req.query.host), false));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});


// File management API endpoints.
app.get('/api/files', requireAuth, apiLimiter, async (_req, res) => {
    try {
        // Read directory and filter out the '.gitkeep' file
        const filenames = (await fs.readdir(uploadsDir)).filter(file => file !== '.gitkeep');
        res.json(filenames);
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('Error listing files:', e.message);
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

app.post('/api/upload', requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'), async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded or file type not supported.' });
    }

    const { originalname, buffer } = req.file;
    const uniqueFilename = ${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${originalname};
    const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, uniqueFilename);

    try {
        await fs.writeFile(filePath, buffer);
        await fs.chmod(filePath, 0o600); // Set file permissions to non-executable
        res.status(200).json({ message: 'File uploaded successfully', filename: uniqueFilename, size: buffer.length });
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('File upload error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to save the file.' });
    }
});

app.get('/api/download', requireAuth, apiLimiter, async (req, res) => {
    const fileName = path.basename(req.query.filename);
    const safePath = path.join(uploadsDir, fileName);

    // Prevent directory traversal
    if (!safePath.startsWith(uploadsDir)) {
        return res.status(403).end();
    }

    // Ensure the file exists before trying to download
    try {
        await fs.access(safePath, fs.constants.F_OK);
        res.download(safePath, fileName, (err) => {
            if (err) {
                console.error('Download error:', err.message);
                // The download method handles most errors gracefully, but we can log it.
                // It's not necessary to send a second response.
            }
        });
    } catch (err) {
        // File does not exist
        return res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found.' });
    }
});

// Final catch-all for errors. This middleware must be defined last.
app.use(errorHandler);

// Start the server on a dynamic port (or a specified PORT if set in .env).
const server = app.listen(process.env.PORT || 0, () => {
    const assignedPort = server.address().port;
    console.log(Server is running on port ${assignedPort});
});

        res.download(safePath, fileName, (err) => {
            if (err) {
                console.error('Download error:', err.message);
                // The download method handles most errors gracefully, but we can log it.
                // It's not necessary to send a second response.
            }
        });
    } catch (err) {
        // File does not exist
        return res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found.' });
    }
});

// Final catch-all for errors. This middleware must be defined last.
app.use(errorHandler);

// Start the server on a dynamic port (or a specified PORT if set in .env).
const server = app.listen(process.env.PORT || 0, () => {
    const assignedPort = server.address().port;
    console.log(Server is running on port ${assignedPort});
});


const express = require('express');
const cors = require('cors');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const path = require('path');
const multer = require('multer');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const { body, query, validationResult } = require('express-validator');
const morgan = require('morgan');
const cron = require('node-cron');
const fs = require('fs').promises;
require('dotenv').config();

// Custom imports - assuming these are internal modules
const RawrZStandalone = require('./rawrz-standalone');
const rawrzEngine = require('./src/engines/rawrz-engine');

// --- Configuration and Setup ---
const app = express();
const port = parseInt(process.env.PORT || '8080', 10);
const uploadsDir = path.join(__dirname, 'uploads');
const rawrz = new RawrZStandalone();

// Generate a random, cryptographically secure token if not specified in the environment.
const generateAuthToken = () => {
    const token = process.env.AUTH_TOKEN || crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
    if (!process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
        console.warn([WARN] No AUTH_TOKEN found in environment. A new, temporary token has been generated.
          This will change on restart. Use the token below for authenticated routes:);
        console.log([INFO] Current session AUTH_TOKEN: ${token});
    }
    return token;
};
const authToken = generateAuthToken();

// Create uploads directory if it doesn't exist, handling potential errors gracefully.
const createUploadsDir = async () => {
    try {
        await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true });
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('[ERROR] Could not create uploads directory:', e.message);
        process.exit(1);
    }
};
createUploadsDir();

// Multer configuration for file uploads. Files are stored in memory (multer.memoryStorage())
// and then written to disk in the route handler to ensure unique naming and permissions.
const upload = multer({
    storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
    limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, files: 10 }, // 100MB file size, max 10 files
    fileFilter: (_req, file, cb) => {
        const allowedTypes = [
            'application/x-executable', 'application/x-msdownload', 'application/x-sharedlib',
            'application/octet-stream', 'application/x-dll', 'application/x-exe',
            'application/x-elf', 'application/x-mach-o'
        ];
        const allowedExtensions = ['.exe', '.dll', '.elf', '.bin', '.scr', '.cpl', '.dylib', '.so'];
        const fileExtension = path.extname(file.originalname).toLowerCase();
        const isAllowed = allowedTypes.includes(file.mimetype) || allowedExtensions.includes(fileExtension);
        cb(isAllowed ? null : new Error(File type not supported: ${file.mimetype}), isAllowed);
    }
});

// Rate limiting middleware to protect general API endpoints.
const apiLimiter = rateLimit({
    windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
    max: 100, // Max 100 requests per 15 minutes
    message: "Too many requests from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes."
});

// Specific rate limit for file uploads due to their higher resource cost.
const uploadLimiter = rateLimit({
    windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
    max: 20, // Max 20 uploads per 15 minutes
    message: "Too many uploads from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes."
});

// CORS options, supporting a specific origin or allowing all in a controlled manner.
const corsOptions = {
    origin: (origin, callback) => {
        const allowedOrigin = process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN || '*';
        if (allowedOrigin === '*' || origin === allowedOrigin) {
            callback(null, true);
        } else {
            callback(new Error('Not allowed by CORS'));
        }
    }
};

// Middleware to require authentication via Authorization header or query parameter.
const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
    if (!authToken) return next();
    const token = req.headers['authorization']?.split(' ')[1] || req.query.token;
    return token === authToken ? next() : res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
};

// Global error handler for centralized error management.
const errorHandler = (err, _req, res, _next) => {
    console.error('[Unhandled Error]', err.stack || err.message);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
};

// File cleanup cron job, running daily at midnight to delete files older than 24 hours.
cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
    console.log('Running scheduled file cleanup...');
    const now = Date.now();
    const oneDayInMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    try {
        const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
        for (const file of files) {
            const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
            const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
            if ((now - stats.mtime.getTime()) > oneDayInMs) {
                await fs.unlink(filePath);
                console.log(Deleted old file: ${file});
            }
        }
        console.log('File cleanup completed.');
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('File cleanup failed:', e.message);
    }
});

// --- Main Application Configuration ---
// Configure Helmet for stricter security headers.
app.use(helmet({
    contentSecurityPolicy: {
        directives: {
            defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
            scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
            objectSrc: ["'none'"],
        },
    },
    noSniff: true,
    xssFilter: true,
}));
app.use(cors(corsOptions));
app.use(morgan('combined'));
app.use('/static', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));

// IMPORTANT: The default JSON body parser for *non-crypto* routes.
app.use(express.json({ limit: '1mb' }));
app.use('/api/', apiLimiter);

// Asynchronously initialize core engine modules.
(async () => {
    try {
        await rawrzEngine.initializeModules();
        console.log('[OK] RawrZ core engine initialized');
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('[WARN] Core engine init failed:', e.message);
    }
})();

// --- API Route Definitions ---

// Allowlisted cryptographic algorithms for validation.
const allowedAlgorithms = ['sha256', 'sha512', 'aes-256-gcm', 'aes-128-cbc'];

const checkAlgorithm = (algorithm, res) => {
    if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(algorithm?.toLowerCase())) {
        res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
        return true;
    }
    return false;
};

// Create a separate router for cryptographic endpoints with a smaller body limit.
const cryptoRouter = express.Router();
cryptoRouter.use(express.json({ limit: '64kb' })); // Cap crypto routes to 64kb
cryptoRouter.use(requireAuth);
cryptoRouter.use(apiLimiter);

// Mount the crypto router under the /api/ prefix
app.use('/api', cryptoRouter);

cryptoRouter.post('/hash', body('input').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
        if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
        res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

cryptoRouter.post('/encrypt', body('input').isString().notEmpty(), body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        const { algorithm, input, extension } = req.body;
        if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
        res.json(await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, input, extension));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

cryptoRouter.post('/decrypt', body('input').isString().notEmpty(), body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        const { algorithm, input, key, iv, extension } = req.body;
        if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
        res.json(await rawrz.decrypt(algorithm, input, key, iv, extension));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

// Basic routes.
app.get('/health', (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, status: 'healthy' }));
app.get('/panel', (_req, res) => res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'panel.html')));
app.get('/', (_req, res) => res.redirect('/panel'));

// Network-related API endpoints.
app.get('/api/dns', requireAuth, query('hostname').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        res.json(await rawrz.dnsLookup(String(req.query.hostname)));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

app.get('/api/ping', requireAuth, query('host').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        res.json(await rawrz.ping(String(req.query.host), false));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

// File management API endpoints.
app.get('/api/files', requireAuth, async (_req, res) => {
    try {
        const filenames = (await fs.readdir(uploadsDir)).filter(file => file !== '.gitkeep');
        res.json(filenames);
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

app.post('/api/upload', requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'), async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) {
        return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: 'No file uploaded' });
    }

    try {
        const uniqueSuffix = crypto.randomBytes(16).toString('hex');
        const filename = ${uniqueSuffix}-${req.file.originalname};
        const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, filename);

        await fs.writeFile(filePath, req.file.buffer);
        await fs.chmod(filePath, 0o600); // Set file permissions to readable/writable only by owner

        res.json({
            success: true,
            originalName: req.file.originalname,
            uploadedName: filename,
            size: req.file.size,
            mimetype: req.file.mimetype,
            message: 'File uploaded successfully'
        });
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Upload error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: error.message });
    }
});

app.get('/api/download', requireAuth, query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(value => path.basename(value)), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        const filename = req.query.filename;
        const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, filename);
        
        // Ensure path is within the uploads directory and exists, preventing path traversal
        if (!filePath.startsWith(uploadsDir)) {
            return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied' });
        }
        await fs.access(filePath, fs.constants.F_OK);

        res.download(filePath, filename);
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found' });
    }
});

app.post('/api/encrypt-file', requireAuth, upload.single('file'), async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) {
        return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: 'No file uploaded' });
    }
    try {
        const algorithm = req.body.algorithm || 'aes-256-gcm';
        const outputFormat = req.body.outputFormat || 'enc';
        
        if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
        
        const result = await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, req.file.buffer.toString('base64'), outputFormat);
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            originalName: req.file.originalname,
            algorithm: algorithm,
            size: req.file.size,
            result: result
        });
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Encryption error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: error.message });
    }
});

// Panel navigation routes.
app.get('/rawrz-panels/encrypt', (_req, res) => 
    res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'encryption-panel.html'))
);

app.get('/encryptor', (_req, res) => 
    res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'encryption-panel.html'))
);

// Engine status endpoint.
app.get('/api/engines', requireAuth, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const result = await rawrzEngine.getEngineStatuses();
        res.json({ engines: result, status: 'loaded' });
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

// Global error handler must be the last middleware added.
app.use(errorHandler);

// Start the server.
const port = parseInt(process.env.PORT || '8080', 10);
app.listen(port, () => console.log([OK] RawrZ HTTP Platform listening on port ${port}));

    try {
        // Read directory and filter out the '.gitkeep' file
