        res.json(filenames);
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('Error listing files:', e.message);
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

app.post('/api/upload', requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'), async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded or file type not supported.' });
    }

    const { originalname, buffer } = req.file;
    const uniqueFilename = ${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${originalname};
    const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, uniqueFilename);

    try {
        await fs.writeFile(filePath, buffer);
        await fs.chmod(filePath, 0o600); // Set file permissions to non-executable
        res.status(200).json({ message: 'File uploaded successfully', filename: uniqueFilename, size: buffer.length });
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('File upload error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to save the file.' });
    }
});

app.get('/api/download', requireAuth, apiLimiter, async (req, res) => {
    const fileName = path.basename(req.query.filename);
    const safePath = path.join(uploadsDir, fileName);

    // Prevent directory traversal
    if (!safePath.startsWith(uploadsDir)) {
        return res.status(403).end();
    }

    // Ensure the file exists before trying to download
    try {
        await fs.access(safePath, fs.constants.F_OK);
        res.download(safePath, fileName, (err) => {
            if (err) {
                console.error('Download error:', err.message);
                // The download method handles most errors gracefully, but we can log it.
                // It's not necessary to send a second response.
            }
        });
    } catch (err) {
        // File does not exist
        return res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found.' });
    }
});

// Final catch-all for errors. This middleware must be defined last.
app.use(errorHandler);

// Start the server on a dynamic port (or a specified PORT if set in .env).
const server = app.listen(process.env.PORT || 0, () => {
    const assignedPort = server.address().port;
    console.log(Server is running on port ${assignedPort});
});



const express = require('express');
const cors = require('cors');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const path = require('path');
const multer = require('multer');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const { body, query, validationResult } = require('express-validator');
const morgan = require('morgan');
const cron = require('node-cron');
const fs = require('fs').promises;
require('dotenv').config();

// Custom imports - assuming these are internal modules
const RawrZStandalone = require('./rawrz-standalone');
const rawrzEngine = require('./src/engines/rawrz-engine');

// --- Configuration and Setup ---
const app = express();
const uploadsDir = path.join(__dirname, 'uploads');
const rawrz = new RawrZStandalone();

// Generate a random, cryptographically secure token if not specified in the environment.
const generateAuthToken = () => {
    const token = process.env.AUTH_TOKEN || crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
    if (!process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
        console.warn([WARN] No AUTH_TOKEN found in environment. A new, temporary token has been generated.
          This will change on restart. Use the token below for authenticated routes:);
        console.log([INFO] Current session AUTH_TOKEN: ${token});
    }
    return token;
};
const authToken = generateAuthToken();

// Create uploads directory if it doesn't exist, handling potential errors gracefully.
const createUploadsDir = async () => {
    try {
        await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true });
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('[ERROR] Could not create uploads directory:', e.message);
        process.exit(1);
    }
};
createUploadsDir();

// Multer configuration for file uploads. Files are stored in memory (multer.memoryStorage())
// and then written to disk in the route handler to ensure unique naming and permissions.
const upload = multer({
    storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
    limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, files: 10 }, // 100MB file size, max 10 files
    fileFilter: (_req, file, cb) => {
        const allowedTypes = [
            'application/x-executable', 'application/x-msdownload', 'application/x-sharedlib',
            'application/octet-stream', 'application/x-dll', 'application/x-exe',
            'application/x-elf', 'application/x-mach-o'
        ];
        const allowedExtensions = ['.exe', '.dll', '.elf', '.bin', '.scr', '.cpl', '.dylib', '.so'];
        const fileExtension = path.extname(file.originalname).toLowerCase();
        const isAllowed = allowedTypes.includes(file.mimetype) || allowedExtensions.includes(fileExtension);
        cb(isAllowed ? null : new Error(File type not supported: ${file.mimetype}), isAllowed);
    }
});

// Rate limiting middleware to protect general API endpoints.
const apiLimiter = rateLimit({
    windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
    max: 100, // Max 100 requests per 15 minutes
    message: "Too many requests from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes."
});

// Specific rate limit for file uploads due to their higher resource cost.
const uploadLimiter = rateLimit({
    windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
    max: 20, // Max 20 uploads per 15 minutes
    message: "Too many uploads from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes."
});

// CORS options, supporting a specific origin or allowing all in a controlled manner.
const corsOptions = {
    origin: (origin, callback) => {
        const allowedOrigin = process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN || '*';
        if (allowedOrigin === '*' || origin === allowedOrigin) {
            callback(null, true);
        } else {
            callback(new Error('Not allowed by CORS'));
        }
    }
};

// Middleware to require authentication via Authorization header or query parameter.
const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
    if (!authToken) return next();
    const token = req.headers['authorization']?.split(' ')[1] || req.query.token;
    return token === authToken ? next() : res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
};

// Global error handler for centralized error management.
const errorHandler = (err, _req, res, _next) => {
    console.error('[Unhandled Error]', err.stack || err.message);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
};

// File cleanup cron job, running daily at midnight to delete files older than 24 hours.
cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
    console.log('Running scheduled file cleanup...');
    const now = Date.now();
    const oneDayInMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    try {
        const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
        for (const file of files) {
            const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
            const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
            if ((now - stats.mtime.getTime()) > oneDayInMs) {
                await fs.unlink(filePath);
                console.log(Deleted old file: ${file});
            }
        }
        console.log('File cleanup completed.');
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('File cleanup failed:', e.message);
    }
});

// --- Main Application Configuration ---
// Configure Helmet for stricter security headers.
app.use(helmet({
    contentSecurityPolicy: {
        directives: {
            defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
            scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
            objectSrc: ["'none'"],
        },
    },
    noSniff: true,
    xssFilter: true,
}));
app.use(cors(corsOptions));
app.use(morgan('combined'));
app.use('/static', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));

// IMPORTANT: Apply general API middleware AFTER Helmet, CORS, Morgan, etc.
// The default JSON body parser for *non-crypto* routes should be present.
app.use(express.json({ limit: '1mb' }));
app.use('/api/', apiLimiter);

// Asynchronously initialize core engine modules.
(async () => {
    try {
        await rawrzEngine.initializeModules();
        console.log('[OK] RawrZ core engine initialized');
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('[WARN] Core engine init failed:', e.message);
    }
})();

// --- API Route Definitions ---

// Allowlisted cryptographic algorithms for validation.
const allowedAlgorithms = ['sha256', 'sha512', 'aes-256-gcm', 'aes-128-cbc'];

const checkAlgorithm = (algorithm, res) => {
    if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(algorithm?.toLowerCase())) {
        res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
        return true;
    }
    return false;
};

// Create a separate router for cryptographic endpoints with a smaller body limit.
const cryptoRouter = express.Router();
cryptoRouter.use(express.json({ limit: '64kb' })); // Cap crypto routes to 64kb
cryptoRouter.use(requireAuth);
cryptoRouter.use(apiLimiter);

// Mount the crypto router under the /api/ prefix
app.use('/api', cryptoRouter);

cryptoRouter.post('/hash', body('input').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
        if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
        res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('[Crypto Error]', e.stack || e.message); // keep in logs
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' }); // generic to client
    }
});

cryptoRouter.post('/encrypt', body('input').isString().notEmpty(), body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        const { algorithm, input, extension } = req.body;
        if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
        res.json(await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, input, extension));
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('[Crypto Error]', e.stack || e.message); // keep in logs
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' }); // generic to client
    }
});

cryptoRouter.post('/decrypt', body('input').isString().notEmpty(), body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        const { algorithm, input, key, iv, extension } = req.body;
        if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
        res.json(await rawrz.decrypt(algorithm, input, key, iv, extension));
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('[Crypto Error]', e.stack || e.message); // keep in logs
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' }); // generic to client
    }
});


// Basic routes.
app.get('/health', (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, status: 'healthy' }));
app.get('/panel', (_req, res) => res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'panel.html')));
app.get('/', (_req, res) => res.redirect('/panel'));


// Network-related API endpoints.
app.get('/api/dns', requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('hostname').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        res.json(await rawrz.dnsLookup(String(req.query.hostname)));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

app.get('/api/ping', requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('host').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        res.json(await rawrz.ping(String(req.query.host), false));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});


// File management API endpoints.
app.get('/api/files', requireAuth, apiLimiter, async (_req, res) => {
    try {
        // Read directory and filter out the '.gitkeep' file
        const filenames = (await fs.readdir(uploadsDir)).filter(file => file !== '.gitkeep');
        res.json(filenames);
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('Error listing files:', e.message);
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

app.post('/api/upload', requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'), async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded or file type not supported.' });
    }

    const { originalname, buffer } = req.file;
    const uniqueFilename = ${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${originalname};
    const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, uniqueFilename);

    try {
        await fs.writeFile(filePath, buffer);
        await fs.chmod(filePath, 0o600); // Set file permissions to non-executable
        res.status(200).json({ message: 'File uploaded successfully', filename: uniqueFilename, size: buffer.length });
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('File upload error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to save the file.' });
    }
});

app.get('/api/download', requireAuth, apiLimiter, async (req, res) => {
    const fileName = path.basename(req.query.filename);
    const safePath = path.join(uploadsDir, fileName);

    // Prevent directory traversal
    if (!safePath.startsWith(uploadsDir)) {
        return res.status(403).end();
    }

    // Ensure the file exists before trying to download
    try {
        await fs.access(safePath, fs.constants.F_OK);
        res.download(safePath, fileName, (err) => {
            if (err) {
                console.error('Download error:', err.message);
                // The download method handles most errors gracefully, but we can log it.
                // It's not necessary to send a second response.
            }
        });
    } catch (err) {
        // File does not exist
        return res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found.' });
    }
});

// Final catch-all for errors. This middleware must be defined last.
app.use(errorHandler);

// Start the server on a dynamic port (or a specified PORT if set in .env).
const server = app.listen(process.env.PORT || 0, () => {
    const assignedPort = server.address().port;
    console.log(Server is running on port ${assignedPort});
});

        return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: 'No file uploaded' });
    }

    try {
        const uniqueSuffix = crypto.randomBytes(16).toString('hex');
        const filename = ${uniqueSuffix}-${req.file.originalname};
        const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, filename);

        await fs.writeFile(filePath, req.file.buffer);
        await fs.chmod(filePath, 0o600); // Set file permissions to readable/writable only by owner

        res.json({
            success: true,
            originalName: req.file.originalname,
            uploadedName: filename,
            size: req.file.size,
            mimetype: req.file.mimetype,
            message: 'File uploaded successfully'
        });
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Upload error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: error.message });
    }
});

app.get('/api/download', requireAuth, query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(value => path.basename(value)), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
        const filename = req.query.filename;
        const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, filename);
        
        // Ensure path is within the uploads directory and exists, preventing path traversal
        if (!filePath.startsWith(uploadsDir)) {
            return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied' });
        }
        await fs.access(filePath, fs.constants.F_OK);

        res.download(filePath, filename);
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found' });
    }
});

app.post('/api/encrypt-file', requireAuth, upload.single('file'), async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) {
        return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: 'No file uploaded' });
    }
    try {
        const algorithm = req.body.algorithm || 'aes-256-gcm';
        const outputFormat = req.body.outputFormat || 'enc';
        
        if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
        
        const result = await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, req.file.buffer.toString('base64'), outputFormat);
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            originalName: req.file.originalname,
            algorithm: algorithm,
            size: req.file.size,
            result: result
        });
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Encryption error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: error.message });
    }
});

ChatGPT said:

Thought for 7s
You’re super close. A few surgical fixes (and one copy-paste oops) to make this airtight:

0) Deduplicate the file
You’ve pasted the whole server multiple times in one file (several const app = express() blocks). Keep one complete copy and delete the rest, or Node will crash/rebind and linting will explode.

1) fs.constants bug (you imported only promises)
You call fs.constants.FOK/F_OK but fs is promises. Split sync + promises:

// replace:
const fs = require('fs').promises;

// with:
const fssync = require('fs');
const fs = fssync.promises;
Then update existence checks:

await fs.access(safePath, fssync.constants.F_OK);
2) Auth header parsing bug
One block has:

const token = req.headers['authorization']?.split(' ') || req.query.token;
This returns an array, not the bearer token. Fix everywhere to:

const authHeader = req.headers['authorization'] || '';
const headerToken = authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ') ? authHeader.slice(7) : null;
const token = headerToken || req.query.token;
return token === authToken ? next() : res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
3) Path-traversal on download (use resolve, validate)
path.join(...).startsWith(uploadsDir) is fragile. Do this:

// near your other consts:
const uploadsRoot = path.resolve(uploadsDir) + path.sep;

// route:
app.get(
  '/api/download',
  requireAuth,
  apiLimiter,
  query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.resolve(uploadsDir, fileName);

    if (!safePath.startsWith(uploadsRoot)) return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied' });

    try {
      await fs.access(safePath, fssync.constants.F_OK);
      return res.download(safePath, fileName, err => {
        if (err) console.error('Download error:', err.message);
      });
    } catch {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found.' });
    }
  }
);
4) Sanitize uploaded filenames (and keep non-exec)
A few places build uniqueFilename with the raw originalname. Strip paths first:

const base = path.basename(req.file.originalname || 'file');
const uniqueFilename = `${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base}`;
const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, uniqueFilename);

await fs.writeFile(filePath, req.file.buffer);
await fs.chmod(filePath, 0o600);
(Apply this in every /api/upload variant you kept.)

5) Helmet: remove deprecated xssFilter
xssFilter is a no-op in Helmet v5+. Keep CSP + nosniff, and add imgSrc/connectSrc as needed:

app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc:  ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"], // drop 'unsafe-inline' in prod if you can
      objectSrc:  ["'none'"],
      imgSrc:     ["'self'", "data:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
    },
  },
  noSniff: true,
}));
6) Trust proxy (for accurate rate-limit IPs)
If you’re behind a proxy/load balancer:

app.set('trust proxy', 1);
7) Crypto DoS guard (looks good—keep it)
You correctly moved crypto endpoints under a router with express.json({ limit: '64kb' }). ✅

Thought for 11s
Nice cleanup—this version is in good shape. A few final nits + hardening ideas:

Must-fix / should-fix
Double rate-limit on crypto routes
You apply apiLimiter at app.use('/api/', apiLimiter) and inside cryptoRouter. That will double count requests. Keep one:

// EITHER keep this global one:
app.use('/api/', apiLimiter);

// ...and remove this:
cryptoRouter.use(apiLimiter);

// OR remove the global and keep a custom limiter per router.
Leaking tokens via URL (optional but recommended)
Query-param auth (?token=...) can end up in logs/proxies. Consider header-only:

const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
  if (!authToken) return next();
  const authHeader = req.headers['authorization'] || '';
  const token = authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ') ? authHeader.slice(7).trim() : null;
  if (token !== authToken) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
  next();
};
Don’t print the live token in prod
Keep the helpful console log in dev only:

if (!process.env.AUTH_TOKEN && process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
  console.warn('[WARN] No AUTH_TOKEN ...');
  console.log(`[INFO] Current session AUTH_TOKEN: ${token}`);
}
Upload size field
You can report req.file.size (multer already computed it) instead of req.file.buffer.length.

res.status(200).json({ message: 'File uploaded successfully', filename: uniqueFilename, size: req.file.size });
Nice-to-have hardening
Multer error handler: catch LIMIT_FILE_SIZE etc. and return 413 instead of 500.

Strict CORS in prod: replace '*' with your real origin.

Helmet CSP: drop 'unsafe-inline' in prod (or use a nonce) if your frontend allows it.

Opaque file IDs: avoid filename enumeration by storing {id: uuid, name, path} and downloading via /api/download?id=... with a short-lived signed token.

If you want, I can drop in a tiny Multer error middleware + a signed download token helper.

/*  RawrZ HTTP Platform – baseline-secure edition  */

const helmet        = require('helmet');

const multer        = require('multer');
const crypto        = require('crypto');

  console.warn('[WARN] AUTH_TOKEN not set; using ephemeral token:', authToken);

  if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(algorithm?.toLowerCase())) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
    return true;
  }
  return false;
};

(async () => {

  const header = req.headers.authorization || '';
  const headerToken = header.startsWith('Bearer ') ? header.slice(7).trim() : null;

  if (!authToken) return next();                  // dev-mode bypass
  return token === authToken ? next() : res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
};

  storage: multer.memoryStorage(),

  fileFilter: (_req, file, cb) => {
    const allowedTypes = ['application/x-executable', 'application/x-msdownload',
      'application/x-sharedlib', 'application/octet-stream', 'application/x-dll',
      'application/x-exe', 'application/x-elf', 'application/x-mach-o'];
    const allowedExtensions = ['.exe', '.dll', '.elf', '.bin', '.scr', '.cpl', '.dylib', '.so'];
    const ext = path.extname(file.originalname).toLowerCase();

    res.json(files.filter(f => f !== '.gitkeep'));
  } catch { res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' }); }

app.post('/api/upload',
  requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'),
  async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded' });
    try {
      const base = path.basename(req.file.originalname || 'file');
      const filename = `${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base}`;
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, filename);
      await fs.writeFile(filePath, req.file.buffer, { mode: 0o600 });
      res.json({ success: true, filename, size: req.file.size });
    } catch {
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Upload failed' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/download',
  requireAuth, apiLimiter,
  query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.resolve(uploadsDir, fileName);

    if (!safePath.startsWith(uploadsRoot)) return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied' });

    try {
      await fs.access(safePath, fssync.constants.F_OK);
      return res.download(safePath, fileName, err => err && console.error('Download error:', err.message));
    } catch {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found' });
    }
  });

/* ---------- cron: delete 24 h+ files ---------- */
cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
  console.log('[Cron] Cleaning old uploads...');
  const cutoff = Date.now() - 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
  try {
    const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    await Promise.all(
      files.map(async f => {
        const p = path.join(uploadsDir, f);
        const stat = await fs.stat(p).catch(() => null);
        if (stat && stat.mtime.getTime() < cutoff) await fs.unlink(p);
      })
    );
    console.log('[Cron] Cleanup finished');
  } catch (e) { console.error('[Cron] Cleanup error:', e.message); }
});

/* ---------- error handler (last) ---------- */
app.use((err, _req, res, _next) => {
  console.error('[Express Error]', err.stack || err.message);
  res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
});

/* ---------- listen ---------- */
app.listen(port, () => console.log(`[OK] RawrZ HTTP Platform listening on port ${port}`));

const express = require('express');
const cors = require('cors');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const path = require('path');
const multer = require('multer');
require('dotenv').config();

const RawrZStandalone = require('./rawrz-standalone');
const rawrzEngine = require('./src/engines/rawrz-engine');

const app = express();
const port = parseInt(process.env.PORT || '8080', 10);
const authToken = process.env.AUTH_TOKEN || '';

const rawrz = new RawrZStandalone();

// Configure multer for file uploads
const upload = multer({
    storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
    limits: {
        fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, // 100MB limit
        files: 10 // Max 10 files at once
    },
    fileFilter: (req, file, cb) => {
        const allowedTypes = [
            'application/x-executable', 'application/x-msdownload', 'application/x-sharedlib',
            'application/octet-stream', 'application/x-dll', 'application/x-exe',
            'application/x-elf', 'application/x-mach-o'
        ];
        const allowedExtensions = [
            '.exe', '.dll', '.elf', '.bin', '.scr', '.cpl',
            '.dylib', '.so', '.o', '.obj', '.a', '.lib'
        ];
        const fileExtension = path.extname(file.originalname).toLowerCase();

        if (allowedTypes.includes(file.mimetype) || allowedExtensions.includes(fileExtension)) {
            cb(null, true);
        } else {
            cb(new Error(File type not supported: ${file.mimetype}), false);
        }
    }
});

// Middleware
function requireAuth(req, res, next) {
    if (!authToken) return next();
    
    const header = req.headers['authorization'] || '';
    const query = req.query.token;
    
    if (header.startsWith('Bearer ')) {
        const token = header.slice(7).trim();
        if (token === authToken) return next();
    }
    
    if (query && query === authToken) return next();
    
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
}

app.use(helmet());
app.use(cors());
app.use(express.json({ limit: '5mb' }));
app.use('/static', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));

// Initialize engines
(async () => {
    try {
        await rawrzEngine.initializeModules();
        console.log('[OK] RawrZ core engine initialized');
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('[WARN] Core engine init failed:', e.message);
    }
})();

// Basic routes
app.get('/health', (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, status: 'healthy' }));
app.get('/panel', (_req, res) => res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'panel.html')));
app.get('/', (_req, res) => res.redirect('/panel'));

// Core RawrZ API endpoints

    try {
        const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body || {};
        if (!input) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'input is required' });
        res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

        res.json(await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, input, extension));
    } catch (e) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
    }
});

        if (!algorithm || !input) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'algorithm and input required' });

Got it—your “Original” is functional, but it’s missing several hardening pieces (auth parsing edge cases, traversal-safe downloads, rate limits, CSP, input validation, upload perms, and algorithm allow-listing). Here’s a drop-in hardened server you can paste over server.js. It preserves your API shape where safe and moves crypto/file ops under /api/* with validation.

/*  RawrZ HTTP Platform – hardened drop-in  */
const express       = require('express');
const cors          = require('cors');
const helmet        = require('helmet');
const path          = require('path');
const multer        = require('multer');
const crypto        = require('crypto');
const rateLimit     = require('express-rate-limit');
const { body, query, validationResult } = require('express-validator');
const morgan        = require('morgan');
const fs            = require('fs').promises;
const fssync        = require('fs'); // for constants only
require('dotenv').config();

const RawrZStandalone = require('./rawrz-standalone');
const rawrzEngine     = require('./src/engines/rawrz-engine');

/* ---------- config ---------- */
const app         = express();
const port        = parseInt(process.env.PORT || '8080', 10);
const uploadsDir  = path.resolve(__dirname, 'uploads');
const uploadsRoot = uploadsDir + path.sep; // for traversal guard
const rawrz       = new RawrZStandalone();

/* ---------- security: trust proxy & logging ---------- */
app.set('trust proxy', 1);
app.use(morgan('combined'));

/* ---------- helmet & cors ---------- */
app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"], // remove 'unsafe-inline' in prod if possible
      objectSrc: ["'none'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"]
    }
  },
  noSniff: true,
}));
app.use(cors({
  origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN || '*',
  credentials: true
}));

/* ---------- auth token ---------- */
const authToken = process.env.AUTH_TOKEN || '';
const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
  if (!authToken) return next(); // dev mode
  const header = req.headers.authorization || '';
  const headerToken = header.startsWith('Bearer ') ? header.slice(7).trim() : null;
  const token = headerToken || req.query.token;
  return token === authToken ? next() : res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
};

/* ---------- body limits & rate limits ---------- */
app.use(express.json({ limit: '1mb' }));
const apiLimiter    = rateLimit({ windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, max: 100, message: 'Too many requests' });
const uploadLimiter = rateLimit({ windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, max: 20,  message: 'Too many uploads' });
app.use('/api', apiLimiter);

/* ---------- mkdir uploads ---------- */
(async () => { await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true }).catch(() => {}); })();

/* ---------- multer ---------- */
const upload = multer({
  storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
  limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, files: 10 },
  fileFilter: (_req, file, cb) => {
    const allowedTypes = [
      'application/x-executable','application/x-msdownload','application/x-sharedlib',
      'application/octet-stream','application/x-dll','application/x-exe',
      'application/x-elf','application/x-mach-o'
    ];
    const allowedExtensions = ['.exe','.dll','.elf','.bin','.scr','.cpl','.dylib','.so','.o','.obj','.a','.lib'];
    const extOK  = allowedExtensions.includes(path.extname(file.originalname).toLowerCase());
    const typeOK = allowedTypes.includes(file.mimetype);
    cb(null, extOK || typeOK);
  }
});

/* ---------- initialize engines ---------- */
(async () => {
  try {
    await rawrzEngine.initializeModules();
    console.log('[OK] RawrZ core engine initialized');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[WARN] Core engine init failed:', e.message);
  }
})();

/* ---------- static & panel ---------- */
app.use('/static', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));
app.get('/health', (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, status: 'healthy' }));
app.get('/panel', (_req, res) => res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'panel.html')));
app.get('/', (_req, res) => res.redirect('/panel'));

/* ---------- crypto routes (validated, small body) ---------- */
const allowedAlgorithms = ['sha256', 'sha512', 'aes-256-gcm', 'aes-128-cbc'];
const cryptoRouter = express.Router();
cryptoRouter.use(express.json({ limit: '64kb' }));
cryptoRouter.use(requireAuth);

const checkAlgorithm = (algo, res) => {
  if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(String(algo || '').toLowerCase())) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
    return true;
  }
  return false;
};

cryptoRouter.post('/hash',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty(),
  body('algorithm').optional().isString(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req); if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch (e) { res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' }); }
  }
);

cryptoRouter.post('/encrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty(),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req); if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, input, extension));
    } catch { res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' }); }
  }
);

cryptoRouter.post('/decrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty(),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req); if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, key, iv, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.decrypt(algorithm, input, key, iv, extension));
    } catch { res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' }); }
  }
);

app.use('/api', cryptoRouter);

/* ---------- network endpoints ---------- */
app.get('/dns',
  requireAuth,
  query('hostname').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req); if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.dnsLookup(String(req.query.hostname))); }
    catch (e) { res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' }); }
  }
);

app.get('/ping',
  requireAuth,
  query('host').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req); if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.ping(String(req.query.host), false)); }
    catch (e) { res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' }); }
  }
);

/* ---------- files: list/upload/download ---------- */
app.get('/files', requireAuth, async (_req, res) => {
  try {
    const list = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    res.json(list.filter(f => f !== '.gitkeep'));
  } catch { res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' }); }
});

app.post('/upload',
  requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'),
  async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded' });
    try {
      const base = path.basename(req.file.originalname || 'file');
      const name = `${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base}`;
      const p = path.join(uploadsDir, name);
      await fs.writeFile(p, req.file.buffer, { mode: 0o600 });
      res.json({ success: true, filename: name, size: req.file.size });
    } catch { res.status(500).json({ error: 'Upload failed' }); }
  }
);

// keep your JSON-based upload for API parity (sanitizes filename)
app.post('/upload-json',
  requireAuth,
  body('filename').isString().notEmpty(),
  body('base64').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req); if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const base = path.basename(req.body.filename);
      const name = `${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base}`;
      const buf  = Buffer.from(req.body.base64, 'base64');
      await fs.writeFile(path.join(uploadsDir, name), buf, { mode: 0o600 });
      res.json({ success: true, filename: name, size: buf.length });
    } catch { res.status(500).json({ error: 'Upload failed' }); }
  }
);

app.get('/download',
  requireAuth,
  query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req); if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.resolve(uploadsDir, fileName);
    if (!safePath.startsWith(uploadsRoot)) return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied' });
    try {
      await fs.access(safePath, fssync.constants.F_OK);
      res.download(safePath, fileName, err => err && console.error('Download error:', err.message));
    } catch { res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found' }); }
  }
);

/* ---------- encryptor API (file upload → encrypt) ---------- */
app.post('/api/upload', upload.single('file'), (req, res) => {
  try {
    if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: 'No file uploaded' });
    res.json({
      success: true,
      originalName: req.file.originalname,
      size: req.file.size,
      mimetype: req.file.mimetype,
      message: 'File uploaded successfully'
    });
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('Upload error:', e);
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: 'Internal Server Error' });
  }
});

app.post('/api/encrypt', upload.single('file'), async (req, res) => {
  try {
    if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: 'No file uploaded' });
    const algorithm   = (req.body.algorithm || 'aes-256-gcm').toLowerCase();
    const outputFormat= req.body.outputFormat || 'enc';
    if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(algorithm)) return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
    const result = await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, req.file.buffer.toString('base64'), outputFormat);
    res.json({ success: true, originalName: req.file.originalname, algorithm, size: req.file.size, result });
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('Encryption error:', e);
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: 'Internal Server Error' });
  }
});

/* ---------- optional: CLI (disabled by default) ---------- */
const ENABLE_CLI = /^true$/i.test(process.env.RAWRZ_ENABLE_CLI || '');
if (ENABLE_CLI) {
  app.post('/cli', requireAuth, body('command').isString().notEmpty(), async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req); if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

      const { command, args = [] } = req.body;
      const cli = new RawrZStandalone();
      const output = await cli.processCommand([command, ...args]);
      res.json({ success: true, result: output });
    } catch (e) { res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' }); }
  });
}

  try {
    const result = await rawrzEngine.getEngineStatuses();
    res.json({ engines: result, status: 'loaded' });
  } catch (e) { res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' }); }
});

/* ---------- listen ---------- */
app.listen(port, () => console.log(`[OK] RawrZ HTTP Platform listening on port ${port}`));
What changed (in brief)
Proper Bearer parsing + optional ?token fallback.

Helmet CSP, CORS origin via ALLOWED_ORIGIN, trust proxy, logging.

Rate limits for /api + separate upload limiter.

Stronger validators via express-validator.

Uploads stored with 0600 perms; sanitized filenames; traversal-safe downloads using path.resolve + uploadsRoot check.

Crypto endpoints moved to /api/*, 64 KB JSON cap, and algorithm allow-list.

Kept your /api/encrypt (file → encrypt) but aligned algorithm names to lower-case and validated.

CLI endpoint disabled by default; enable with RAWRZ_ENABLE_CLI=true.

If you want me to align the routes back to your exact original paths (e.g., keep /hash at root), I can produce that variant too—same hardening, just different mount points.

/*  RawrZ HTTP Platform – baseline-secure edition  */
const express       = require('express');
const cors          = require('cors');
const helmet        = require('helmet');
const path          = require('path');
const multer        = require('multer');
const crypto        = require('crypto');
const rateLimit     = require('express-rate-limit');
const { body, query, validationResult } = require('express-validator');
const morgan        = require('morgan');
const cron          = require('node-cron');
const fs            = require('fs').promises;
const fssync        = require('fs');                // ← sync constants only
require('dotenv').config();

const RawrZStandalone = require('./rawrz-standalone');
const rawrzEngine     = require('./src/engines/rawrz-engine');

/* ---------- config ---------- */
const app         = express();
const port        = parseInt(process.env.PORT || '8080', 10);
const uploadsDir  = path.resolve(__dirname, 'uploads');
const uploadsRoot = uploadsDir + path.sep;          // ← for traversal guard
const rawrz       = new RawrZStandalone();

/* ---------- auth token ---------- */
const authToken = process.env.AUTH_TOKEN || crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
if (!process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
  console.warn('[WARN] AUTH_TOKEN not set; using ephemeral token:', authToken);
}

/* ---------- helpers ---------- */
const allowedAlgorithms = ['sha256', 'sha512', 'aes-256-gcm', 'aes-128-cbc'];
const checkAlgorithm = (algorithm, res) => {
  if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(algorithm?.toLowerCase())) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
    return true;
  }
  return false;
};

/* ---------- mkdir ---------- */
(async () => {
  try { await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true }); }
  catch { process.exit(1); }
})();

/* ---------- middleware ---------- */
app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc:  ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],   // drop unsafe-inline in prod if possible
      objectSrc:  ["'none'"],
      imgSrc:     ["'self'", "data:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
    },
  },
  noSniff: true,
}));
app.use(cors({
  origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN || '*',
  credentials: true
}));
app.use(morgan('combined'));
app.set('trust proxy', 1);                        // ← accurate client IP behind proxy
app.use('/static', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));

/* ---------- body parsers ---------- */
const apiLimiter = rateLimit({ windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, max: 100, message: 'Too many requests' });
const uploadLimiter = rateLimit({ windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, max: 20, message: 'Too many uploads' });

app.use(express.json({ limit: '1mb' }));
app.use('/api', apiLimiter);

/* ---------- auth ---------- */
const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
  const header = req.headers.authorization || '';
  const headerToken = header.startsWith('Bearer ') ? header.slice(7).trim() : null;
  const token = headerToken || req.query.token;
  if (!authToken) return next();                  // dev-mode bypass
  return token === authToken ? next() : res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
};

/* ---------- crypto router (64 kB) ---------- */
const cryptoRouter = express.Router();
cryptoRouter.use(express.json({ limit: '64kb' }));
cryptoRouter.use(requireAuth);
cryptoRouter.use(apiLimiter);

cryptoRouter.post('/hash',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch {
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/encrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty(),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, input, extension));
    } catch {
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/decrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty(),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, key, iv, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.decrypt(algorithm, input, key, iv, extension));
    } catch {
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.use('/api', cryptoRouter);

/* ---------- multer ---------- */
const upload = multer({
  storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
  limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, files: 10 },
  fileFilter: (_req, file, cb) => {
    const allowedTypes = ['application/x-executable', 'application/x-msdownload',
      'application/x-sharedlib', 'application/octet-stream', 'application/x-dll',
      'application/x-exe', 'application/x-elf', 'application/x-mach-o'];
    const allowedExtensions = ['.exe', '.dll', '.elf', '.bin', '.scr', '.cpl', '.dylib', '.so'];
    const ext = path.extname(file.originalname).toLowerCase();
    cb(null, allowedTypes.includes(file.mimetype) || allowedExtensions.includes(ext));
  }
});

/*  RawrZ HTTP Platform – baseline-secure edition  */
const express       = require('express');
const cors          = require('cors');
const helmet        = require('helmet');
const path          = require('path');
const multer        = require('multer');
const crypto        = require('crypto');
const rateLimit     = require('express-rate-limit');
const { body, query, validationResult } = require('express-validator');
const morgan        = require('morgan');
const cron          = require('node-cron');
const fs            = require('fs').promises;
const fssync        = require('fs');                // ← sync constants only
require('dotenv').config();

const RawrZStandalone = require('./rawrz-standalone');
const rawrzEngine     = require('./src/engines/rawrz-engine');

/* ---------- config ---------- */
const app         = express();
const port        = parseInt(process.env.PORT || '8080', 10);
const uploadsDir  = path.resolve(__dirname, 'uploads');
const uploadsRoot = uploadsDir + path.sep;          // ← for traversal guard
const rawrz       = new RawrZStandalone();

/* ---------- auth token ---------- */
const authToken = process.env.AUTH_TOKEN || crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
if (!process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
  console.warn('[WARN] AUTH_TOKEN not set; using ephemeral token:', authToken);
}

/* ---------- helpers ---------- */
const allowedAlgorithms = ['sha256', 'sha512', 'aes-256-gcm', 'aes-128-cbc'];
const checkAlgorithm = (algorithm, res) => {
  if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(algorithm?.toLowerCase())) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
    return true;
  }
  return false;
};

/* ---------- mkdir ---------- */
(async () => {
  try { await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true }); }
  catch { process.exit(1); }
})();

/* ---------- middleware ---------- */
app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc:  ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],   // drop unsafe-inline in prod if possible
      objectSrc:  ["'none'"],
      imgSrc:     ["'self'", "data:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
    },
  },
  noSniff: true,
}));
app.use(cors({
  origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN || '*',
  credentials: true
}));
app.use(morgan('combined'));
app.set('trust proxy', 1);                        // ← accurate client IP behind proxy
app.use('/static', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));

/* ---------- body parsers ---------- */
const apiLimiter = rateLimit({ windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, max: 100, message: 'Too many requests' });
const uploadLimiter = rateLimit({ windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, max: 20, message: 'Too many uploads' });

app.use(express.json({ limit: '1mb' }));
app.use('/api', apiLimiter);

/* ---------- auth ---------- */
const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
  const header = req.headers.authorization || '';
  const headerToken = header.startsWith('Bearer ') ? header.slice(7).trim() : null;
  const token = headerToken || req.query.token;
  if (!authToken) return next();                  // dev-mode bypass
  return token === authToken ? next() : res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
};

/* ---------- crypto router (64 kB) ---------- */
const cryptoRouter = express.Router();
cryptoRouter.use(express.json({ limit: '64kb' }));
cryptoRouter.use(requireAuth);
cryptoRouter.use(apiLimiter);

cryptoRouter.post('/hash',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch {
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/encrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty(),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, input, extension));
    } catch {
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/decrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty(),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, key, iv, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.decrypt(algorithm, input, key, iv, extension));
    } catch {
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.use('/api', cryptoRouter);

/* ---------- multer ---------- */
const upload = multer({
  storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
  limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, files: 10 },
  fileFilter: (_req, file, cb) => {
    const allowedTypes = ['application/x-executable', 'application/x-msdownload',
      'application/x-sharedlib', 'application/octet-stream', 'application/x-dll',
      'application/x-exe', 'application/x-elf', 'application/x-mach-o'];
    const allowedExtensions = ['.exe', '.dll', '.elf', '.bin', '.scr', '.cpl', '.dylib', '.so'];
    const ext = path.extname(file.originalname).toLowerCase();
    cb(null, allowedTypes.includes(file.mimetype) || allowedExtensions.includes(ext));
  }
});

/* ---------- routes ---------- */
app.get('/health', (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, status: 'healthy' }));
app.get('/panel', (_req, res) => res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'panel.html')));
app.get('/', (_req, res) => res.redirect('/panel'));

app.get('/api/dns',
  requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('hostname').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.dnsLookup(String(req.query.hostname))); }
    catch { res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' }); }
  });

app.get('/api/ping',
  requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('host').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.ping(String(req.query.host), false)); }
    catch { res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' }); }
  });

app.get('/api/files', requireAuth, apiLimiter, async (_req, res) => {
  try {
    const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    res.json(files.filter(f => f !== '.gitkeep'));
  } catch { res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' }); }
});

app.post('/api/upload',
  requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'),
  async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded' });
    try {
      const base = path.basename(req.file.originalname || 'file');
      const filename = `${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base}`;
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, filename);
      await fs.writeFile(filePath, req.file.buffer, { mode: 0o600 });
      res.json({ success: true, filename, size: req.file.size });
    } catch {
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Upload failed' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/download',
  requireAuth, apiLimiter,
  query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.resolve(uploadsDir, fileName);

    if (!safePath.startsWith(uploadsRoot)) return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied' });

    try {
      await fs.access(safePath, fssync.constants.F_OK);
      return res.download(safePath, fileName, err => err && console.error('Download error:', err.message));
    } catch {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found' });
    }
  });

/* ---------- cron: delete 24 h+ files ---------- */
cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
  console.log('[Cron] Cleaning old uploads...');
  const cutoff = Date.now() - 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
  try {
    const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    await Promise.all(
      files.map(async f => {
        const p = path.join(uploadsDir, f);
        const stat = await fs.stat(p).catch(() => null);
        if (stat && stat.mtime.getTime() < cutoff) await fs.unlink(p);
      })
    );
    console.log('[Cron] Cleanup finished');
  } catch (e) { console.error('[Cron] Cleanup error:', e.message); }
});

/* ---------- error handler (last) ---------- */
app.use((err, _req, res, _next) => {
  console.error('[Express Error]', err.stack || err.message);
  res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
});

/* ---------- engine boot & listen ---------- */
(async () => {
  try {
    await rawrzEngine.initializeModules();
    console.log('[OK] RawrZ core engine initialized');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[WARN] Core engine init failed:', e.message);
  }
})();

app.listen(port, () => console.log(`[OK] RawrZ HTTP Platform listening on port ${port}`));

ChatGPT said:
That snippet is a good secure pattern for a download route. Let’s break down what’s happening and why it matters:

if (!safePath.startsWith(uploadsRoot)) {
  return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });
}
// Continue with file download...
res.download(safePath, fileName, (err) => {
    if (err) {
        console.error('Download error:', err);
        res.status(500).send('Internal Server Error');
    }
});
Why this is safe
Traversal guard
By checking safePath.startsWith(uploadsRoot), you make sure the resolved path is still under your uploads/ directory. That blocks directory-traversal tricks like ?filename=../../etc/passwd.

Consistent error handling
Returning 403 with { error: 'Forbidden' } when validation fails ensures attackers don’t get hints about your folder structure.

Controlled fallback
Using the res.download callback lets you catch filesystem errors (like “file missing” or “permission denied”) and respond with a consistent 500. In production, you might want to distinguish between:

404 for “file not found”

500 for actual internal errors
so clients don’t get misled.

Optional refinements
404 for missing files
Before calling res.download, run await fs.access(safePath) so you can send 404 instead of always 500.

Logging only server-side
Avoid sending raw error messages back to the client. Right now you’re doing res.status(500).send('Internal Server Error'), which is good. Just make sure stack traces stay in logs only.

Rate-limiting downloads
If downloads could be abused (e.g., DoS), consider applying the same apiLimiter or a separate limiter just for /api/download.

Token check
Wrap this in your requireAuth middleware so only authorized users can trigger downloads.

So: your snippet is already sound. With the refinements above (especially distinguishing 404 vs 500), it’s a production-ready download route.

Want me to slot this into your cleaned-up server file so you have a fully integrated /api/download with 404 handling instead of blanket 500?

const cors          = require('cors');
const helmet        = require('helmet');
const path          = require('path');
const multer        = require('multer');
const crypto        = require('crypto');
const rateLimit     = require('express-rate-limit');

const morgan        = require('morgan');
const cron          = require('node-cron');
const fs            = require('fs').promises;
const fssync        = require('fs');  // for constants only

const uploadsRoot = uploadsDir + path.sep;

  console.warn('[WARN] AUTH_TOKEN not set; using ephemeral token for this run:', authToken);
}

  try { await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true }); }
  catch (e) {
    console.error('[FATAL] Could not ensure uploads directory:', e.message);
    process.exit(1);
  }
  try {
    await rawrzEngine.initializeModules();

  contentSecurityPolicy: {

      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],

      objectSrc:  ["'none'"],
      imgSrc:     ["'self'", "data:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
      styleSrc:   ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"], // if inline styles required by panel
    },
  },

      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, filename);
      await fs.writeFile(filePath, req.file.buffer, { mode: 0o600 });
      res.json({ success: true, filename, size: req.file.size, mimetype: req.file.mimetype });
    } catch {
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Upload failed' });
    }
  });

/* ---------- download (robust traversal & 404) ---------- */
app.get('/api/download',
  requireAuth, apiLimiter,
  query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.resolve(uploadsDir, fileName);
    if (!safePath.startsWith(uploadsRoot)) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });
    }

    try {
      await fs.access(safePath, fssync.constants.F_OK);
    } catch {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found' });
    }

    res.download(safePath, fileName, (err) => {
      if (err) {
        console.error('Download error:', err?.message || err);
        if (!res.headersSent) res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
      }
    });
  });

/* ---------- encrypt file (buffer → base64 → encrypt) ---------- */
app.post('/api/encrypt-file',
  requireAuth, upload.single('file'),
  async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded' });
    try {
      const algorithm    = (req.body.algorithm || 'aes-256-gcm').toLowerCase();
      const outputFormat = req.body.outputFormat || 'enc';
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;

      const base64 = req.file.buffer.toString('base64');
      const result = await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, base64, outputFormat);
      res.json({
        success: true,
        originalName: req.file.originalname,
        algorithm,
        size: req.file.size,
        result
      });
    } catch {
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

/* ---------- panel shortcuts & engine status ---------- */
app.get('/rawrz-panels/encrypt', (_req, res) =>
  res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'encryption-panel.html'))
);
app.get('/encryptor', (_req, res) =>
  res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'encryption-panel.html'))
);

app.get('/api/engines', requireAuth, async (_req, res) => {
  try {
    const statuses = await rawrzEngine.getEngineStatuses();
    res.json({ engines: statuses, status: 'loaded' });
  } catch {
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
  }
});

/* ---------- daily cleanup of 24h+ files ---------- */
cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
  console.log('[Cron] Cleaning old uploads…');
  const cutoff = Date.now() - 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
  try {
    const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    await Promise.all(files.map(async f => {
      const p = path.join(uploadsDir, f);
      try {
        const st = await fs.stat(p);
        if (st.mtime.getTime() < cutoff) await fs.unlink(p);
      } catch { /* ignore missing/locked */ }
    }));
    console.log('[Cron] Cleanup complete');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[Cron] Cleanup error:', e.message);
  }
});

/* ---------- final error handler ---------- */
app.use((err, _req, res, _next) => {
  console.error('[Express Error]', err?.stack || err?.message || err);
  res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
});

/* ---------- listen ---------- */
app.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(`[OK] RawrZ HTTP Platform listening on port ${port}`);
});
Notes

Uses strict CSP, rate limits, auth, sanitized filenames, traversal guard, and generic error messages.

AUTH_TOKEN can be provided via env; otherwise it generates an ephemeral one and logs it.

/api/encrypt-file validates the algorithm against a tight allowlist.

Downloads return 403 on traversal, 404 when missing, 500 on unexpected errors.

Daily cron removes uploads older than 24h.

  const header = req.headers.authorization || '';
  const token = header.startsWith('Bearer ') ? header.slice(7).trim() : null;
  if (!authToken && process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
    console.warn('[DEV] Auth bypass enabled. Not for production use.');
    return next();
  }
  if (!token || token !== authToken) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });

  next();

const checkAlgorithm = (algorithm, res) => {
  if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(algorithm?.toLowerCase())) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
    return true;
  }
  return false;

  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

      const { algorithm, input, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;

// --- Multer (Memory Storage with Robust File Filter) ---
const upload = multer({
  storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
  limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, files: 10 },
  fileFilter: async (_req, file, cb) => {
    const allowedTypes = [
      'application/x-executable', 'application/x-msdownload', 'application/x-sharedlib',
      'application/octet-stream', 'application/x-dll', 'application/x-exe',
      'application/x-elf', 'application/x-mach-o'
    ];
    const buffer = file.buffer;
    const type = await fileType.fromBuffer(buffer);

    // Fallback to extension check if magic number detection fails
    const ext = path.extname(file.originalname || '').toLowerCase();
    const isAllowed = (type && allowedTypes.includes(type.mime)) || allowedTypes.includes(file.mimetype) || allowedExtensions.includes(ext);

    if (isAllowed) {
      cb(null, true);
    } else {
      cb(new Error(File type not supported: ${type ? type.mime : file.mimetype}), false);
    }
  }
});

// --- Routes ---
app.get('/health', (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, status: 'healthy' }));

  } catch (err) {
    console.error('[Files Error]', err.stack || err.message);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
  }
});

app.post('/api/upload',
  requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'),
  async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded or file type not supported' });
    try {
      const base = path.basename(req.file.originalname || 'file');
      const filename = ${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base};
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, filename);
      await fs.writeFile(filePath, req.file.buffer, { mode: 0o600 });
      res.json({ success: true, filename, size: req.file.size });
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Upload Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Upload failed' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/download',
  requireAuth, apiLimiter,
  query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.join(uploadsDir, fileName);

    // Path traversal check
    if (!safePath.startsWith(uploadsRoot)) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });
    }

    try {
      await fs.access(safePath, fs.constants.R_OK);
      res.download(safePath, fileName, (err) => {
        if (err) {
          console.error('[Download Error]', err.stack || err.message);
          res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
        }
      });
    } catch (err) {
      if (err.code === 'ENOENT') {
        res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found' });
      } else {
        console.error('[Download Access Error]', err.stack || err.message);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
      }
    }
  });

// --- File Cleanup Cron Job ---
cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
    console.log('Running scheduled file cleanup...');
    const now = Date.now();
    const oneDayInMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    try {
        const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
        for (const file of files) {
            const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
            const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
            if (stats.isFile() && (now - stats.mtime.getTime()) > oneDayInMs) {
                await fs.unlink(filePath);
                console.log(Deleted old file: ${file});
            }
        }
        console.log('File cleanup completed.');
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('File cleanup failed:', e.message);
    }
});

// --- Global Error Handler ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  if (err instanceof multer.MulterError) {
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_SIZE') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'File size too large. Max 100MB allowed.' });
    }
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_COUNT') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'Too many files uploaded. Max 10 files allowed.' });
    }
    return res.status(400).json({ error: Upload error: ${err.message} });
  } else if (err) {
    if (err.message.includes('File type not supported')) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: err.message });
    }
    console.error('[Unhandled Error]', err.stack || err.message);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
  }
  next();
});

app.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(Server is running securely on port ${port});
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
    console.log('[INFO] Remember to run npm audit regularly to check for vulnerable dependencies.');
  }
});
ChatGPT said:

Thought for 15s
Nice start! I spot a few issues that will bite you in prod (and a couple that will throw immediately):

multer.fileFilter can’t be async, and you can’t read file.buffer there (it doesn’t exist yet). Do content-sniffing after upload.single() using file-type.

allowedExtensions is referenced but never defined.

fs.constants is used via fs (the promises API) — that’s undefined. Use require('fs').constants.

Path traversal guard should use path.resolve(...) before startsWith.

helmet({ xssFilter: true }) is deprecated; drop it.

CORS: origin: '*' with credentials: true is invalid in browsers. Use a specific origin or set credentials: false.

Here’s a fixed, clean version you can paste over your file:

/*  RawrZ HTTP Platform – secure-from-scratch edition  */
'use strict';

// --- Dependencies ---
const express       = require('express');
const cors          = require('cors');
const helmet        = require('helmet');
const path          = require('path');
const multer        = require('multer');
const crypto        = require('crypto');
const rateLimit     = require('express-rate-limit');
const { body, query, validationResult } = require('express-validator');
const morgan        = require('morgan');
const cron          = require('node-cron');
const fs            = require('fs').promises;
const fssync        = require('fs'); // for constants
const { fileTypeFromBuffer } = require('file-type');
require('dotenv').config();

// --- Internal Modules ---
const RawrZStandalone = require('./rawrz-standalone');
const rawrzEngine     = require('./src/engines/rawrz-engine');

// --- Configuration ---
const app         = express();
const port        = parseInt(process.env.PORT || '8080', 10);

const uploadsRoot = uploadsDir + path.sep; // For path traversal checks

if (!process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
  console.warn('[WARN] AUTH_TOKEN not set in environment. Using ephemeral token for this session:', authToken);
}

// --- Boot ---
(async () => {
  try {
    await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true });
    console.log('[OK] Ensured uploads directory exists.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[FATAL] Could not create uploads directory:', e.message);
    process.exit(1);
  }

  try {
    await rawrzEngine.initializeModules();
    console.log('[OK] RawrZ core engine initialized.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[WARN] Core engine init failed:', e.message);
  }
})();

// --- Security Middleware: Helmet & CORS ---

  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc:  ["'self'"],            // avoid 'unsafe-inline'
      objectSrc:  ["'none'"],
      imgSrc:     ["'self'", "data:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
      styleSrc:   ["'self'"],            // avoid 'unsafe-inline'
    },
  },
  noSniff: true,
}));

app.use(cors({
  // If you truly need credentials, set a specific origin instead of '*'
  origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN || '*',
  credentials: Boolean(process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN && process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN !== '*'),
}));

// --- Logging & Proxy Settings ---
app.use(morgan('combined'));
app.set('trust proxy', 1);

// --- Rate Limiting & Body Parsers ---

  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
  max: 100,
  message: 'Too many requests from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes.',
});

  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
  max: 20,
  message: 'Too many uploads from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes.',
});

const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
  const header = req.headers.authorization || '';
  const token = header.startsWith('Bearer ') ? header.slice(7).trim() : null;

  // In this build, authToken is always truthy (ephemeral if not provided),
  // so we just compare it.
  if (!token || token !== authToken) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
  }
  next();
};

// --- Helpers ---
const allowedAlgorithms = ['sha256', 'sha512', 'aes-256-gcm', 'aes-128-cbc'];
const checkAlgorithm = (algorithm, res) => {
  if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(String(algorithm).toLowerCase())) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
    return true;
  }
  return false;
};

  'application/x-executable', 'application/x-msdownload', 'application/x-sharedlib',
  'application/octet-stream', 'application/x-dll', 'application/x-exe',
  'application/x-elf', 'application/x-mach-o'
];
const allowedExtensions = ['.exe', '.dll', '.elf', '.bin', '.scr', '.cpl', '.dylib', '.so'];

// --- Static File Serving ---
app.use('/static', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));

cryptoRouter.use(apiLimiter);

  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),

    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, input, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });
