  body('input').isString().notEmpty(),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, key, iv, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.decrypt(algorithm, input, key, iv, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.use('/api', cryptoRouter);

// --- Multer (Memory Storage; basic filter; deep check post-upload) ---
// NOTE: fileFilter must be synchronous; do only a light check here.
const upload = multer({
  storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
  limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, files: 10 },
  fileFilter: (_req, file, cb) => {
    const extOk  = allowedExtensions.includes(path.extname(file.originalname || '').toLowerCase());
    const mimeOk = allowedTypes.includes(file.mimetype);
    cb(null, extOk || mimeOk);
  }
});

// --- Routes ---
app.get('/health', (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, status: 'healthy' }));
app.get('/panel', (_req, res) => res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'panel.html')));
app.get('/', (_req, res) => res.redirect('/panel'));

app.get('/api/dns',
  requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('hostname').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.dnsLookup(String(req.query.hostname))); }
    catch (err) {
      console.error('[DNS Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/ping',
  requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('host').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.ping(String(req.query.host), false)); }
    catch (err) {
      console.error('[Ping Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/files', requireAuth, apiLimiter, async (_req, res) => {
  try {
    const list = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    res.json(list.filter(f => f !== '.gitkeep'));
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('[Files Error]', err.stack || err.message);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
  }
});

app.post('/api/upload',
  requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'),
  async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded or file type not supported' });

    // Deep verify magic number AFTER upload
    try {
      const type = await fileTypeFromBuffer(req.file.buffer).catch(() => null);
      const ext  = path.extname(req.file.originalname || '').toLowerCase();

      const magicOk = type && allowedTypes.includes(type.mime);
      const fallbackOk = allowedTypes.includes(req.file.mimetype) || allowedExtensions.includes(ext);

      if (!magicOk && !fallbackOk) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: `File type not supported (${type ? type.mime : req.file.mimetype})` });
      }

      const base = path.basename(req.file.originalname || 'file');
      const filename = `${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base}`;
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, filename);
      await fs.writeFile(filePath, req.file.buffer, { mode: 0o600 });
      res.json({ success: true, filename, size: req.file.size });
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Upload Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Upload failed' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/download',
  requireAuth, apiLimiter,
  query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.resolve(uploadsDir, fileName); // resolve before guard

    if (!safePath.startsWith(uploadsRoot)) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });
    }

    try {
      await fs.access(safePath, fssync.constants.R_OK);
      res.download(safePath, fileName, (err) => {
        if (err) {
          console.error('[Download Error]', err.stack || err.message);
          if (!res.headersSent) res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
        }
      });
    } catch (err) {
      if (err.code === 'ENOENT') return res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found' });
      console.error('[Download Access Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

// --- File Cleanup Cron Job ---
cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
  console.log('[Cron] Cleaning old uploads...');
  const now = Date.now();
  const oneDayInMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
  try {
    const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    for (const file of files) {
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
      try {
        const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
        if (stats.isFile() && (now - stats.mtime.getTime()) > oneDayInMs) {
          await fs.unlink(filePath);
          console.log(`[Cron] Deleted old file: ${file}`);
        }
      } catch { /* ignore */ }
    }
    console.log('[Cron] Cleanup completed.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[Cron] Cleanup failed:', e.message);
  }
});

// --- Global Error Handler ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  if (err instanceof multer.MulterError) {
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_SIZE') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'File size too large. Max 100MB allowed.' });
    }
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_COUNT') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'Too many files uploaded. Max 10 files allowed.' });
    }
    return res.status(400).json({ error: `Upload error: ${err.message}` });
  }
  if (err && String(err.message || '').includes('File type not supported')) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: err.message });
  }
  if (err) {
    console.error('[Unhandled Error]', err.stack || err.message || err);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
  }
  next();
});

// --- Server Startup ---
app.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(`Server is running securely on port ${port}`);
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
    console.log('[INFO] Tip: set AUTH_TOKEN and ALLOWED_ORIGIN before deploying to prod.');
  }
});
If you want me to tailor the CSP or CORS for your exact front-end origin(s), say the URL(s) and I’ll wire them in precisely.

// --- Authentication Middleware ---
const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
  const header = req.headers.authorization || '';
  const token = header.startsWith('Bearer ') ? header.slice(7).trim() : null;
  
  if (!authToken) {
    // In dev, bypass auth if no token is set in env
    if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') return next();
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Server misconfigured. No auth token set.' });
  }

  if (!token || token !== authToken) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
  }
  next();
};

// --- Helpers ---

  if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(algorithm?.toLowerCase())) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
    return true;
  }
  return false;
};

  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {

      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;

      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

// --- Multer (Memory Storage with Robust File Filter) ---

  storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
  limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, files: 10 },
  fileFilter: async (_req, file, cb) => {
    const allowedMimes = [
      'application/x-executable', 'application/x-msdownload', 'application/x-sharedlib',
      'application/octet-stream', 'application/x-dll', 'application/x-exe',
      'application/x-elf', 'application/x-mach-o'
    ];
    const allowedExtensions = ['.exe', '.dll', '.elf', '.bin', '.scr', '.cpl', '.dylib', '.so'];
    
    // Check magic number using file-type library
    const fileTypeFromBuffer = await fileType.fromBuffer(file.buffer);
    const isMagicNumberValid = fileTypeFromBuffer && allowedMimes.includes(fileTypeFromBuffer.mime);
    
    // Fallback to extension check if magic number detection fails (e.g., plain text files)
    const ext = path.extname(file.originalname || '').toLowerCase();
    const isExtensionValid = allowedExtensions.includes(ext) && file.mimetype;

    if (isMagicNumberValid || isExtensionValid) {
      cb(null, true);
    } else {
      cb(new Error(File type not supported: ${fileTypeFromBuffer ? fileTypeFromBuffer.mime : 'Unknown'}), false);
    }
  }
});

Thought for 11s
Got you. Your version is close, but multer.fileFilter can’t be async (and file.buffer doesn’t exist there yet), xssFilter is deprecated, and cors has credentials:true with origin:* (browser-incompatible). Also tighten the traversal guard with path.resolve.

Here’s a clean, copy-pasteable server with those fixes applied (magic-number check happens after upload), plus a couple of small hardening tweaks:

/*  RawrZ HTTP Platform – secure-from-scratch edition  */
'use strict';

// --- Dependencies ---
const express       = require('express');
const cors          = require('cors');
const helmet        = require('helmet');
const path          = require('path');
const multer        = require('multer');
const crypto        = require('crypto');

const morgan        = require('morgan');

const rawrzEngine     = require('./src/engines/rawrz-engine');

  console.warn('[WARN] AUTH_TOKEN not set; using ephemeral token for this session:', authToken);

    await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true });

  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc:  ["'self'"],
      objectSrc:  ["'none'"],
      imgSrc:     ["'self'", "data:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
      styleSrc:   ["'self'"],
    },
  },
  noSniff: true,
}));

// If you need credentials, set ALLOWED_ORIGIN to a specific origin.
// credentials:true with origin:'*' is blocked by browsers.
const allowOrigin = process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN || '*';
app.use(cors({
  origin: allowOrigin,
  credentials: allowOrigin !== '*',
}));

// --- Logging & Proxy ---
app.use(morgan('combined'));
app.set('trust proxy', 1);

  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
  max: 100,
  message: 'Too many requests from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes.'
});

  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
  max: 20,
  message: 'Too many uploads from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes.'
});

  const token = header.startsWith('Bearer ') ? header.slice(7).trim() : null;
  if (!token || token !== authToken) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
  next();
};

  if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(String(algorithm).toLowerCase())) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
    return true;
  }
  return false;
};

  'application/x-executable', 'application/x-msdownload', 'application/x-sharedlib',
  'application/octet-stream', 'application/x-dll', 'application/x-exe',
  'application/x-elf', 'application/x-mach-o'
];

cryptoRouter.use(apiLimiter);

  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),

    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/encrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),

  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, input, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/decrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty(),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, key, iv, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.decrypt(algorithm, input, key, iv, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.use('/api', cryptoRouter);

// --- Multer (memory) ---
// fileFilter must be synchronous; do only a light check here.
// Perform robust magic-number validation in the route handler.
const upload = multer({
  storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
  limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, files: 10 },
  fileFilter: (_req, file, cb) => {
    const extOk  = allowedExtensions.includes(path.extname(file.originalname || '').toLowerCase());
    const mimeOk = allowedMimes.includes(file.mimetype);
    cb(null, extOk || mimeOk);
  }
});

// --- Routes ---
app.get('/health', (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, status: 'healthy' }));
app.get('/panel', (_req, res) => res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'panel.html')));
app.get('/', (_req, res) => res.redirect('/panel'));

app.get('/api/dns',
  requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('hostname').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.dnsLookup(String(req.query.hostname))); }
    catch (err) {
      console.error('[DNS Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/ping',
  requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('host').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.ping(String(req.query.host), false)); }
    catch (err) {
      console.error('[Ping Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/files', requireAuth, apiLimiter, async (_req, res) => {
  try {
    const list = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    const files = await Promise.all(
      list.filter(f => f !== '.gitkeep').map(async (file) => {
        const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
        const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
        return { name: file, size: stats.size, modified: stats.mtime };
      })
    );
    res.json(files);
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('[Files Error]', err.stack || err.message);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
  }
});

app.post('/api/upload',
  requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'),
  async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded or file type not supported' });

    try {
      // Robust magic-number verification AFTER upload
      const magic = await fileTypeFromBuffer(req.file.buffer).catch(() => null);
      const ext   = path.extname(req.file.originalname || '').toLowerCase();
      const magicOk = magic && allowedMimes.includes(magic.mime);
      const fallbackOk = allowedMimes.includes(req.file.mimetype) || allowedExtensions.includes(ext);

      if (!magicOk && !fallbackOk) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: `File type not supported (${magic ? magic.mime : req.file.mimetype || 'unknown'})` });
      }

      const base = path.basename(req.file.originalname || 'file');
      const filename = `${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base}`;
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, filename);

      await fs.writeFile(filePath, req.file.buffer, { mode: 0o600 });
      res.json({ success: true, filename, size: req.file.size });
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Upload Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Upload failed' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/download',
  requireAuth, apiLimiter,
  query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.resolve(uploadsDir, fileName); // resolve before guard

    // Strict path traversal guard
    if (!safePath.startsWith(uploadsRoot)) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });
    }

    try {
      await fs.access(safePath, fssync.constants.R_OK);
      res.download(safePath, fileName, (err) => {
        if (err) {
          console.error('[Download Error]', err.stack || err.message);
          if (!res.headersSent) res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
        }
      });
    } catch (err) {
      if (err.code === 'ENOENT') return res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found' });
      console.error('[Download Access Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

// --- File Cleanup Cron Job ---
cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
  console.log('[Cron] Cleaning old uploads...');
  const now = Date.now();
  const oneDay = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
  try {
    const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    for (const f of files) {
      const p = path.join(uploadsDir, f);
      try {
        const st = await fs.stat(p);
        if (st.isFile() && (now - st.mtime.getTime()) > oneDay) {
          await fs.unlink(p);
          console.log(`[Cron] Deleted old file: ${f}`);
        }
      } catch { /* ignore */ }
    }
    console.log('[Cron] Cleanup completed.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[Cron] Cleanup failed:', e.message);
  }
});

// --- Multer/Error Handler ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  if (err instanceof multer.MulterError) {
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_SIZE') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'File size too large. Max 100MB allowed.' });
    }
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_COUNT') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'Too many files uploaded. Max 10 files allowed.' });
    }
    return res.status(400).json({ error: `Upload error: ${err.message}` });
  }
  if (err && /File type not supported/i.test(String(err.message))) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: err.message });
  }
  next(err);
});

// --- Global Error Handler ---
app.use((err, _req, res, _next) => {
  console.error('[Unhandled Error]', err.stack || err.message || err);
  res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
});

// --- 404 ---
app.use((req, res) => res.status(404).json({ error: 'Not Found' }));

// --- Server ---
app.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(`Server is running securely on port ${port}`);
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
    console.log('[INFO] Tip: set AUTH_TOKEN and ALLOWED_ORIGIN before deploying to prod.');
  }
});

  const header = req.headers.authorization || '';

  if (!token || token !== authToken) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
  }
  next();

    res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
    return true;
  }
  return false;

  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),

ChatGPT said:

Thought for 11s
Looks solid! You’ve locked down the common foot-guns: strict auth on every sensitive route, CSP without unsafe-inline, tight body limits, rate limiting, magic-number file validation, traversal guard, least-priv uploads (0o600), and daily cleanup. Nice.

A few tiny production nits to consider:

Trust proxy (if behind a load balancer/CDN)
Add app.set('trust proxy', 1); so rate-limit/morgan see the real client IP.

CORS ergonomics
Right now ALLOWED_ORIGIN supports a single origin or *. If you need multiple origins, accept a comma-separated list:

Parse process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS?.split(',') and pass a function to cors({ origin }) to allow known ones.

Panel auth is good; add a simple health-only public surface
You did that with /health. If you ever expose more, keep them outside /api (so the API limiter doesn’t throttle simple static or health probes).

Upload MIME fallback (optional)
file-type can return undefined for some binaries. If you want a permissive fallback for specific extensions, add a guarded extension check in the upload route (still returning 400 by default is the stricter/safer choice—what you have is fine for prod).

CSP refinements (optional, based on frontend)
If you embed your panel in other pages, consider frame-ancestors 'self'. If you use fonts or a CDN, whitelist them explicitly (no wildcards).

Auth token fail-fast
You already warn if AUTH_TOKEN is missing. In prod, you might prefer to hard-fail on startup:

if (!process.env.AUTH_TOKEN && process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
  throw new Error('AUTH_TOKEN must be set in production');
}
Rate-limit tuning
Consider a separate limiter for crypto endpoints vs. general /api if those operations are heavier.

If you want, I can fold in #1, #2 (multi-origin), and #6 into your file in a tightened “prod-strict” snippet.

const cors = require('cors');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const path = require('path');
const multer = require('multer');
const crypto = require('crypto');

const rawrzEngine = require('./src/engines/rawrz-engine');

  console.error('[FATAL] AUTH_TOKEN not set. Exiting.');
  process.exit(1);

  console.warn('[WARN] AUTH_TOKEN not set. Using ephemeral token for non-production session.');
}

// --- Application Bootstrapping ---
const bootApp = async () => {
  try {
    await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true });
    console.log('[OK] Ensured uploads directory exists.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[FATAL] Could not create uploads directory:', e.message);
    process.exit(1);
  }

  try {
    await rawrzEngine.initializeModules();
    console.log('[OK] RawrZ core engine initialized.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[WARN] Core engine init failed:', e.message);
  }

  // Self-scanning dependencies
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
    exec('npm audit --json', (error, stdout) => {
      if (error) {
        console.warn('[SECURITY] npm audit check failed with errors. Review dependencies immediately.');
        try {
          const auditResult = JSON.parse(stdout);
          if (auditResult.metadata.vulnerabilities.total > 0) {
            console.error([SECURITY] Found ${auditResult.metadata.vulnerabilities.total} vulnerabilities on startup!);
          }
        } catch (parseErr) {
          console.error('[SECURITY] Failed to parse npm audit output:', parseErr.message);
        }
      } else {
        try {
          const auditResult = JSON.parse(stdout);
          if (auditResult.metadata.vulnerabilities.total > 0) {
            console.error([SECURITY] Found ${auditResult.metadata.vulnerabilities.total} vulnerabilities on startup!);
          } else {
            console.log('[SECURITY] npm audit scan completed with no vulnerabilities found.');
          }
        } catch (parseErr) {
          console.error('[SECURITY] Failed to parse npm audit output:', parseErr.message);
        }
      }
    });
  }
};

// --- Security Middleware: Helmet & CORS ---
app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'"],
      objectSrc: ["'none'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'"],
    },
  },
  noSniff: true,
}));

// Dynamic CORS configuration based on environment
const allowedOrigins = process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN
  ? process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN.split(',').map(s => s.trim())
  : ['*'];

const corsOptions = {
  origin: (origin, callback) => {
    if (allowedOrigins.includes('*') || allowedOrigins.includes(origin)) {
      callback(null, true);
    } else {
      callback(new Error('Not allowed by CORS'));
    }
  },
  credentials: allowedOrigins.length > 1 || !allowedOrigins.includes('*'),
};
app.use(cors(corsOptions));

// --- Logging & Proxy Settings ---
app.use(morgan('combined'));
app.set('trust proxy', 1);

// --- Rate Limiting & Body Parsers ---
const apiLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
  max: 100,
  message: 'Too many requests from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes.',
});
const uploadLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
  max: 20,
  message: 'Too many uploads from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes.',
});

app.use(express.json({ limit: '1mb' }));
app.use('/api', apiLimiter);

// --- Authentication Middleware ---
const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
  const header = req.headers.authorization || '';
  const token = header.startsWith('Bearer ') ? header.slice(7).trim() : null;

  if (!token || token !== authToken) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
  }
  next();
};

// --- Helpers ---
const allowedAlgorithms = ['sha256', 'sha512', 'aes-256-gcm', 'aes-128-cbc'];
const checkAlgorithm = (algorithm, res) => {
  if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(String(algorithm).toLowerCase())) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
    return true;
  }
  return false;
};

const allowedFileMimes = [
  'application/x-executable', 'application/x-msdownload', 'application/x-sharedlib',
  'application/octet-stream', 'application/x-dll', 'application/x-exe',
  'application/x-elf', 'application/x-mach-o'
];

// --- Static File Serving ---
app.use('/static', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));

// --- Crypto Router with Tight Body Limit ---
const cryptoRouter = express.Router();
cryptoRouter.use(express.json({ limit: '64kb' }));
cryptoRouter.use(requireAuth);
cryptoRouter.use(apiLimiter);

cryptoRouter.post('/hash',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/encrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, input, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/decrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, key, iv, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.decrypt(algorithm, input, key, iv, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.use('/api', cryptoRouter);

// --- Multer (Memory Storage) ---
const upload = multer({
  storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
  limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, files: 10 },
});

// --- Routes ---
app.get('/health', (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, status: 'healthy' }));
app.get('/panel', requireAuth, (_req, res) => res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'panel.html')));
app.get('/', (_req, res) => res.redirect('/panel'));

app.get('/api/dns',
  requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('hostname').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.dnsLookup(String(req.query.hostname))); }
    catch (err) {
      console.error('[DNS Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/ping',
  requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('host').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.ping(String(req.query.host), false)); }
    catch (err) {
      console.error('[Ping Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/files', requireAuth, apiLimiter, async (_req, res) => {
  try {
    const list = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    const files = await Promise.all(list.filter(f => f !== '.gitkeep').map(async file => {
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
      const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
      return { name: file, size: stats.size, modified: stats.mtime };
    }));
    res.json(files);
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('[Files Error]', err.stack || err.message);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
  }
});

app.post('/api/upload',
  requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'),
  async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded' });

    try {
      const file = req.file;
      const fileTypeFromBufferResult = await fileTypeFromBuffer(file.buffer);

      if (!fileTypeFromBufferResult || !allowedFileMimes.includes(fileTypeFromBufferResult.mime)) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: File type not supported: ${fileTypeFromBufferResult ? fileTypeFromBufferResult.mime : 'unknown'} });
      }

      const base = path.basename(file.originalname || 'file');
      const filename = ${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base};
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, filename);
      await fs.writeFile(filePath, file.buffer, { mode: 0o600 });
      res.json({ success: true, filename, size: file.size });

    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Upload Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Upload failed' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/download',
  requireAuth, apiLimiter,
  query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.join(uploadsDir, fileName);

    // Strict path traversal check
    if (!path.resolve(safePath).startsWith(path.resolve(uploadsRoot))) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });
    }

    try {
      await fs.access(safePath, constants.R_OK);
      res.download(safePath, fileName, (err) => {
        if (err) {
          console.error('[Download Error]', err.stack || err.message);
          res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
        }
      });
    } catch (err) {
      if (err.code === 'ENOENT') {
        res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found' });
      } else {
        console.error('[Download Access Error]', err.stack || err.message);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
      }
    }
  });

// --- File Cleanup Cron Job ---
cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
  console.log('Running scheduled file cleanup...');
  const now = Date.now();
  const oneDayInMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
  try {
    const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    for (const file of files) {
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
      const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
      if (stats.isFile() && (now - stats.mtime.getTime()) > oneDayInMs) {
        await fs.unlink(filePath);
        console.log(Deleted old file: ${file});
      }
    }
    console.log('File cleanup completed.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('File cleanup failed:', e.message);
  }
});

// --- Multer Error Handler Middleware ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  if (err instanceof multer.MulterError) {
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_SIZE') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'File size too large. Max 100MB allowed.' });
    }
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_COUNT') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'Too many files uploaded. Max 10 files allowed.' });
    }
    return res.status(400).json({ error: Upload error: ${err.message} });
  }
  next(err);
});

// --- Global Error Handler ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  console.error('[Unhandled Error]', err.stack || err.message);
  res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
});

// --- Catch-all 404 Route ---
app.use((req, res) => {
  res.status(404).json({ error: 'Not Found' });
});

// --- Server Startup ---
app.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(Server is running on port ${port});
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
    console.log('[INFO] Remember to run npm audit regularly to check for vulnerable dependencies.');
  }
});
ChatGPT said:

Thought for 19s
Nice iteration — this is genuinely production-ready. Auth is strict, CSP is clean (no unsafe-inline), rate limits and body limits are sensible, uploads are permissioned 0o600 with magic-number validation, traversal is guarded with path.resolve(...).startsWith(...), and you’ve got daily cleanup + robust error handling. 👍

If you want to tighten a few last screws, here are small, drop-in tweaks:

Harden security headers a tad more
Add a couple of widely-used headers that Helmet doesn’t enable by default:

app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'"],
      objectSrc: ["'none'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'"],
      frameAncestors: ["'self'"],   // prevent clickjacking
    },
  },
  noSniff: true,
  crossOriginResourcePolicy: { policy: 'same-origin' },
  referrerPolicy: { policy: 'no-referrer' },
  // Expect-CT is deprecated; Permissions-Policy is set separately:
}));
app.use((req, res, next) => {
  res.setHeader('Permissions-Policy', 'geolocation=(), microphone=(), camera=()');
  next();
});
Make CORS friendlier to tools with no Origin (curl/cron)
Your current config is fine, but if you ever lock it to specific origins, browsers without an Origin may get blocked. This tiny adjustment treats null/undefined as OK when you’re not using '*':

const allowed = (process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN || '*')
  .split(',')
  .map(s => s.trim())
  .filter(Boolean);

app.use(cors({
  origin(origin, cb) {
    if (!origin) return cb(null, true);                 // allow non-browser or same-origin
    if (allowed.includes('*') || allowed.includes(origin)) return cb(null, true);
    return cb(new Error('Not allowed by CORS'));
  },
  credentials: !allowed.includes('*'),
}));
Dev-mode ergonomics (optional)
Right now, if AUTH_TOKEN is missing (dev), you warn but still enforce auth. If you prefer the classic dev bypass:

const devBypass = !authToken && process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production';
const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
  if (devBypass) return next();
  const header = req.headers.authorization || '';
  const token = header.startsWith('Bearer ') ? header.slice(7).trim() : null;
  return token === authToken ? next() : res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
};
Avoid double rate-limiting on /api/crypto routes (minor)
You already apply app.use('/api', apiLimiter) and also cryptoRouter.use(apiLimiter). One is enough. I’d keep the top-level one and drop the router-level to avoid double counting.

Safer JSON parse errors
Express will emit a SyntaxError for invalid JSON. Fold this into your global error handler so clients get a clean 400:

app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  if (err?.type === 'entity.parse.failed') {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid JSON body' });
  }
  next(err);
});
Graceful shutdown (k8s/PM2/Unit)
Close the server cleanly on SIGTERM/SIGINT so uploads don’t get cut off mid-flight:

const server = app.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(`Server is running on port ${port}`);
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
    console.log('[INFO] Run `npm audit` regularly to check for vulnerable dependencies.');
  }
});

const shutdown = (signal) => async () => {
  console.log(`[${signal}] Shutting down...`);
  server.close(err => {
    if (err) {
      console.error('Error during shutdown:', err);
      process.exit(1);
    }
    process.exit(0);
  });
};
process.on('SIGTERM', shutdown('SIGTERM'));
process.on('SIGINT', shutdown('SIGINT'));
Everything else looks tight. If you want, I can splice these directly into your file and hand back a single consolidated version.

/*  RawrZ HTTP Platform – production-ready edition with self-scan  */
'use strict';

// --- Dependencies ---
const express = require('express');
const cors = require('cors');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const path = require('path');
const multer = require('multer');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const { body, query, validationResult } = require('express-validator');
const morgan = require('morgan');
const cron = require('node-cron');
const fs = require('fs').promises;
const { constants } = require('fs');
const { fileTypeFromBuffer } = require('file-type');
const { exec } = require('child_process');
require('dotenv').config();

// --- Internal Modules ---
const RawrZStandalone = require('./rawrz-standalone');
const rawrzEngine = require('./src/engines/rawrz-engine');

// --- Configuration ---
const app = express();
const port = parseInt(process.env.PORT || '8080', 10);
const uploadsDir = path.resolve(__dirname, 'uploads');
const uploadsRoot = uploadsDir + path.sep;
const rawrz = new RawrZStandalone();

// --- Authentication Token ---
const authToken = process.env.AUTH_TOKEN;
if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' && !authToken) {
  console.error('[FATAL] AUTH_TOKEN not set. Exiting.');
  process.exit(1);
} else if (!authToken) {
  console.warn('[WARN] AUTH_TOKEN not set. Using ephemeral token for non-production session.');
  process.env.AUTH_TOKEN = crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
}

// --- Application Bootstrapping ---
const bootApp = async () => {
  try {
    await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true });
    console.log('[OK] Ensured uploads directory exists.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[FATAL] Could not create uploads directory:', e.message);
    process.exit(1);
  }

  try {
    await rawrzEngine.initializeModules();
    console.log('[OK] RawrZ core engine initialized.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[WARN] Core engine init failed:', e.message);
  }

  // Self-scanning dependencies
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
    exec('npm audit --json', (error, stdout) => {
      if (error) {
        console.warn('[SECURITY] npm audit check failed with errors. Review dependencies immediately.');
        try {
          const auditResult = JSON.parse(stdout);
          if (auditResult.metadata.vulnerabilities.total > 0) {
            console.error([SECURITY] Found ${auditResult.metadata.vulnerabilities.total} vulnerabilities on startup!);
          }
        } catch (parseErr) {
          console.error('[SECURITY] Failed to parse npm audit output:', parseErr.message);
        }
      } else {
        try {
          const auditResult = JSON.parse(stdout);
          if (auditResult.metadata.vulnerabilities.total > 0) {
            console.error([SECURITY] Found ${auditResult.metadata.vulnerabilities.total} vulnerabilities on startup!);
          } else {
            console.log('[SECURITY] npm audit scan completed with no vulnerabilities found.');
          }
        } catch (parseErr) {
          console.error('[SECURITY] Failed to parse npm audit output:', parseErr.message);
        }
      }
    });
  }
};
bootApp();

// --- Security Middleware: Helmet & CORS ---
app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'"],
      objectSrc: ["'none'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'"],
    },
  },
  noSniff: true,
}));

// Dynamic CORS configuration based on environment
const allowedOrigins = process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN
  ? process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN.split(',').map(s => s.trim())
  : ['*'];

const corsOptions = {
  origin: (origin, callback) => {
    if (allowedOrigins.includes('*') || (origin && allowedOrigins.includes(origin))) {
      callback(null, true);
    } else {
      callback(new Error('Not allowed by CORS'));
    }
  },
  credentials: allowedOrigins.length > 1 || !allowedOrigins.includes('*'),
};
app.use(cors(corsOptions));

// --- Logging & Proxy Settings ---
app.use(morgan('combined'));
app.set('trust proxy', 1);

// --- Rate Limiting & Body Parsers ---
const apiLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
  max: 100,
  message: 'Too many requests from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes.',
});
const uploadLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
  max: 20,
  message: 'Too many uploads from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes.',
});

app.use(express.json({ limit: '1mb' }));
app.use('/api', apiLimiter);

// --- Authentication Middleware ---
const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
  const header = req.headers.authorization || '';
  const token = header.startsWith('Bearer ') ? header.slice(7).trim() : null;

  // Use authToken from the environment (either ephemeral or configured)
  if (!token || token !== process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
  }
  next();
};

cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
  console.log('Running scheduled file cleanup...');
  const now = Date.now();
  const oneDayInMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
  try {
    const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    for (const file of files) {
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
      const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
      if (stats.isFile() && (now - stats.mtime.getTime()) > oneDayInMs) {
        await fs.unlink(filePath);
        console.log(Deleted old file: ${file});
      }
    }
    console.log('File cleanup completed.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('File cleanup failed:', e.message);
  }
});

// --- Multer Error Handler Middleware ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  if (err instanceof multer.MulterError) {
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_SIZE') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'File size too large. Max 100MB allowed.' });
    }
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_COUNT') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'Too many files uploaded. Max 10 files allowed.' });
    }
    return res.status(400).json({ error: Upload error: ${err.message} });
  }
  next(err);
});

// --- Global Error Handler ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  console.error('[Unhandled Error]', err.stack || err.message);
  res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
});

// --- Catch-all 404 Route ---
app.use((req, res) => {
  res.status(404).json({ error: 'Not Found' });
});

// --- Server Startup ---
app.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(Server is running on port ${port});
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
    console.log('[INFO] Remember to run npm audit regularly to check for vulnerable dependencies.');
  }
});
ChatGPT said:

Thought for 11s
Looks solid. You’ve got auth, CSP, rate limits, magic-number file checks, traversal guards, daily cleanup, and centralized errors. A few tiny, production-polish nits you might want to apply:

Don’t double-rate-limit crypto routes
You already do app.use('/api', apiLimiter), and also cryptoRouter.use(apiLimiter). Drop one (I’d keep only the top-level one).

Allow non-browser clients through CORS
Right now, requests with no Origin (curl/cron/internal) are blocked unless '*' is allowed. If that’s not intended, tweak:

const corsOptions = {
  origin(origin, cb) {
    if (!origin) return cb(null, true); // allow same-origin / non-browser
    if (allowedOrigins.includes('*') || allowedOrigins.includes(origin)) return cb(null, true);
    return cb(new Error('Not allowed by CORS'));
  },
  credentials: allowedOrigins.length > 1 || !allowedOrigins.includes('*'),
};
Add a couple more headers (minor hardening)
Helmet covers a lot, but these help:

app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'"],
      objectSrc: ["'none'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'"],
      frameAncestors: ["'self'"] // anti-clickjacking
    },
  },
  noSniff: true,
  referrerPolicy: { policy: 'no-referrer' },
  crossOriginResourcePolicy: { policy: 'same-origin' },
}));
app.use((req, res, next) => {
  res.setHeader('Permissions-Policy', 'geolocation=(), microphone=(), camera=()');
  next();
});
(If you terminate TLS, also enable HSTS on the edge/load balancer.)

Friendlier invalid-JSON handling
Return a clean 400 when body parse fails:

app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  if (err?.type === 'entity.parse.failed') {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid JSON body' });
  }
  next(err);
});
Graceful shutdown
Avoid cutting connections mid-flight:

const server = app.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(`Server is running on port ${port}`);
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
    console.log('[INFO] Remember to run `npm audit` regularly...');
  }
});

const shutdown = (signal) => () => {
  console.log(`[${signal}] Shutting down...`);
  server.close(err => process.exit(err ? 1 : 0));
};
process.on('SIGTERM', shutdown('SIGTERM'));
process.on('SIGINT', shutdown('SIGINT'));
(Optional) Serve static assets if you need them
If you intend to serve /static/* (css/js/images), add back:

app.use('/static', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));
Everything else reads clean and production-ready. If you want, I can splice those tweaks into your file and hand you the final one-pager.

  console.error('[FATAL] AUTH_TOKEN not set. Exiting.');
  process.exit(1);
} else if (!authToken) {
  console.warn('[WARN] AUTH_TOKEN not set. Using ephemeral token for non-production session.');
  process.env.AUTH_TOKEN = crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
}

// --- Application Bootstrapping ---

  try {
    await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true });
    console.log('[OK] Ensured uploads directory exists.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[FATAL] Could not create uploads directory:', e.message);
    process.exit(1);

    await rawrzEngine.initializeModules();

  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[WARN] Core engine init failed:', e.message);
  }

  // Self-scanning dependencies
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
    exec('npm audit --json', (error, stdout) => {
      if (error) {
        console.warn('[SECURITY] npm audit check failed with errors. Review dependencies immediately.');
        try {
          const auditResult = JSON.parse(stdout);
          if (auditResult.metadata.vulnerabilities.total > 0) {
            console.error([SECURITY] Found ${auditResult.metadata.vulnerabilities.total} vulnerabilities on startup!);
          }
        } catch (parseErr) {
          console.error('[SECURITY] Failed to parse npm audit output:', parseErr.message);

          const auditResult = JSON.parse(stdout);
          if (auditResult.metadata.vulnerabilities.total > 0) {
            console.error([SECURITY] Found ${auditResult.metadata.vulnerabilities.total} vulnerabilities on startup!);
          } else {
            console.log('[SECURITY] npm audit scan completed with no vulnerabilities found.');
          }
        } catch (parseErr) {

        }
      }
    });

  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'"],
      objectSrc: ["'none'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:"],

  ? process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN.split(',').map(s => s.trim())
  : ['*'];

const corsOptions = {
  origin: (origin, callback) => {
    if (!origin) return callback(null, true); // Allow same-origin / non-browser requests
    if (allowedOrigins.includes('*') || allowedOrigins.includes(origin)) return callback(null, true);
    return callback(new Error('Not allowed by CORS'));
  },
  credentials: allowedOrigins.length > 1 || !allowedOrigins.includes('*'),
};

  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
  max: 20,
  message: 'Too many uploads from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes.',

const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
  const header = req.headers.authorization || '';
  const token = header.startsWith('Bearer ') ? header.slice(7).trim() : null;

  if (!token || token !== process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
  }
  next();
};

const allowedAlgorithms = ['sha256', 'sha512', 'aes-256-gcm', 'aes-128-cbc'];
const checkAlgorithm = (algorithm, res) => {
  if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(String(algorithm).toLowerCase())) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
    return true;
  }
  return false;
};

  'application/x-executable', 'application/x-msdownload', 'application/x-sharedlib',

cryptoRouter.post('/hash',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/encrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, input, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/decrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, key, iv, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.decrypt(algorithm, input, key, iv, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.use('/api', cryptoRouter);

// --- Multer (Memory Storage) ---
const upload = multer({
  storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
  limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, files: 10 },
});

app.get('/health', (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, status: 'healthy' }));

app.get('/', (_req, res) => res.redirect('/panel'));

app.get('/api/dns',
  requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('hostname').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.dnsLookup(String(req.query.hostname))); }
    catch (err) {
      console.error('[DNS Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/ping',
  requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('host').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.ping(String(req.query.host), false)); }
    catch (err) {
      console.error('[Ping Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/files', requireAuth, apiLimiter, async (_req, res) => {
  try {
    const list = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    const files = await Promise.all(list.filter(f => f !== '.gitkeep').map(async file => {
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
      const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
      return { name: file, size: stats.size, modified: stats.mtime };
    }));
    res.json(files);
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('[Files Error]', err.stack || err.message);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
  }
});

app.post('/api/upload',
  requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'),
  async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded' });

    try {
      const file = req.file;
      const fileTypeFromBufferResult = await fileTypeFromBuffer(file.buffer);

      if (!fileTypeFromBufferResult || !allowedFileMimes.includes(fileTypeFromBufferResult.mime)) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: File type not supported: ${fileTypeFromBufferResult ? fileTypeFromBufferResult.mime : 'unknown'} });
      }

      const base = path.basename(file.originalname || 'file');
      const filename = ${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base};
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, filename);
      await fs.writeFile(filePath, file.buffer, { mode: 0o600 });
      res.json({ success: true, filename, size: file.size });

    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Upload Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Upload failed' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/download',
  requireAuth, apiLimiter,
  query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.join(uploadsDir, fileName);

    // Strict path traversal check
    if (!path.resolve(safePath).startsWith(path.resolve(uploadsRoot))) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });
    }

    try {
      await fs.access(safePath, constants.R_OK);
      res.download(safePath, fileName, (err) => {
        if (err) {
          console.error('[Download Error]', err.stack || err.message);
          res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
        }
      });
    } catch (err) {
      if (err.code === 'ENOENT') {
        res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found' });
      } else {
        console.error('[Download Access Error]', err.stack || err.message);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
      }
    }
  });

// --- File Cleanup Cron Job ---
cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
  console.log('Running scheduled file cleanup...');
  const now = Date.now();
  const oneDayInMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
  try {
    const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    for (const file of files) {
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
      const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
      if (stats.isFile() && (now - stats.mtime.getTime()) > oneDayInMs) {
        await fs.unlink(filePath);
        console.log(Deleted old file: ${file});
      }
    }
    console.log('File cleanup completed.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('File cleanup failed:', e.message);
  }
});

// --- Multer Error Handler Middleware ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  if (err instanceof multer.MulterError) {
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_SIZE') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'File size too large. Max 100MB allowed.' });
    }
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_COUNT') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'Too many files uploaded. Max 10 files allowed.' });
    }
    return res.status(400).json({ error: Upload error: ${err.message} });
  }
  next(err);
});

// --- Invalid JSON Handling ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  if (err?.type === 'entity.parse.failed') {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid JSON body' });
  }
  next(err);
});

// --- Global Error Handler ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  console.error('[Unhandled Error]', err.stack || err.message);
  res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
});

app.use((req, res) => {
  res.status(404).json({ error: 'Not Found' });

}

    await rawrzEngine.initializeModules();
    console.log('[OK] RawrZ core engine initialized.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[WARN] Core engine init failed:', e.message);
  }

  // Optional self-scan in production
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
    exec('npm audit --json', (error, stdout) => {
      try {
        const report = JSON.parse(stdout || '{}');

          console.error(`[SECURITY] Found ${total} dependency vulnerabilities on startup!`);
        } else {
          console.log('[SECURITY] npm audit scan completed with no vulnerabilities found.');
        }
      } catch (parseErr) {
        console.error('[SECURITY] Failed to parse npm audit output:', parseErr.message);
      }
    });
  }
})();

  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'"],
      objectSrc: ["'none'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'"],
      frameAncestors: ["'self'"]
    },
  },
  noSniff: true,
  referrerPolicy: { policy: 'no-referrer' },
  crossOriginResourcePolicy: { policy: 'same-origin' },
}));

// Permissions-Policy hardening

  res.setHeader('Permissions-Policy', 'geolocation=(), microphone=(), camera=()');
  next();
});

// --- CORS ---

  ? process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN.split(',').map(s => s.trim())
  : ['*'];

  origin: (origin, cb) => {
    if (!origin) return cb(null, true); // same-origin or non-browser
    if (allowedOrigins.includes('*') || allowedOrigins.includes(origin)) return cb(null, true);
    return cb(new Error('Not allowed by CORS'));

  message: 'Too many requests from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes.',
});
const uploadLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
  max: 20,
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
  message: 'Too many uploads from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes.',
});

app.use(express.json({ limit: '1mb' }));
// Invalid JSON handler (must come immediately after express.json)
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  if (err?.type === 'entity.parse.failed') return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid JSON body' });
  next(err);
});
app.use('/api', apiLimiter);

// --- Auth Middleware ---
const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
  const header = req.headers.authorization || '';
  const token = header.startsWith('Bearer ') ? header.slice(7).trim() : null;
  if (!token || token !== process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
  }
  next();
};

// --- Helpers ---
const allowedAlgorithms = ['sha256', 'sha512', 'aes-256-gcm', 'aes-128-cbc'];
const checkAlgorithm = (algorithm, res) => {
  if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(String(algorithm).toLowerCase())) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
    return true;
  }
  return false;
};
const allowedFileMimes = [
  'application/x-executable', 'application/x-msdownload', 'application/x-sharedlib',
  'application/octet-stream', 'application/x-dll', 'application/x-exe',
  'application/x-elf', 'application/x-mach-o'
];

// --- Static ---
app.use('/static', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));

// --- Crypto Router (tight body limit) ---
const cryptoRouter = express.Router();
cryptoRouter.use(express.json({ limit: '64kb' }));
cryptoRouter.use(requireAuth);

cryptoRouter.post('/hash',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/encrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, input, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/decrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, key, iv, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.decrypt(algorithm, input, key, iv, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.use('/api', cryptoRouter);

// --- Multer (memory) ---
const upload = multer({
  storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
  limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, files: 10 },
});

// --- Routes ---
app.get('/health', (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, status: 'healthy' }));
app.get('/panel', requireAuth, (_req, res) => res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'panel.html')));
app.get('/', (_req, res) => res.redirect('/panel'));

app.get('/api/dns',
  requireAuth, query('hostname').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.dnsLookup(String(req.query.hostname))); }
    catch (err) {
      console.error('[DNS Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/ping',
  requireAuth, query('host').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.ping(String(req.query.host), false)); }
    catch (err) {
      console.error('[Ping Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/files', requireAuth, async (_req, res) => {
  try {
    const list = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    const files = await Promise.all(list.filter(f => f !== '.gitkeep').map(async file => {
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
      const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
      return { name: file, size: stats.size, modified: stats.mtime };
    }));
    res.json(files);
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('[Files Error]', err.stack || err.message);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
  }
});

app.post('/api/upload',
  requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'),
  async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded' });
    try {
      const file = req.file;
      const sniff = await fileTypeFromBuffer(file.buffer);
      if (!sniff || !allowedFileMimes.includes(sniff.mime)) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: `File type not supported: ${sniff ? sniff.mime : 'unknown'}` });
      }
      const base = path.basename(file.originalname || 'file').replace(/[\r\n]/g, '');
      const filename = `${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base}`;
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, filename);
      await fs.writeFile(filePath, file.buffer, { mode: 0o600 });
      res.json({ success: true, filename, size: file.size });
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Upload Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Upload failed' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/download',
  requireAuth,
  query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.join(uploadsDir, fileName);
    // traversal check
    if (!path.resolve(safePath).startsWith(path.resolve(uploadsRoot))) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });
    }
    try {
      await fs.access(safePath, constants.R_OK);
      res.download(safePath, fileName, (err) => {
        if (err) {
          console.error('[Download Error]', err.stack || err.message);
          res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
        }
      });
    } catch (err) {
      if (err.code === 'ENOENT') return res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found' });
      console.error('[Download Access Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

// --- Cleanup Cron (daily at midnight) ---
cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
  console.log('[Cron] Cleaning old uploads...');
  const cutoff = Date.now() - 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
  try {
    const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    await Promise.all(files.map(async f => {
      const p = path.join(uploadsDir, f);
      const stat = await fs.stat(p).catch(() => null);
      if (stat && stat.isFile() && stat.mtime.getTime() < cutoff) {
        await fs.unlink(p).then(() => console.log(`[Cron] Deleted old file: ${f}`)).catch(() => {});
      }
    }));
    console.log('[Cron] Cleanup finished');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[Cron] Cleanup error:', e.message);
  }
});

// --- Multer Error Handler ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  if (err instanceof multer.MulterError) {
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_SIZE') return res.status(413).json({ error: 'File size too large. Max 100MB allowed.' });
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_COUNT') return res.status(413).json({ error: 'Too many files uploaded. Max 10 files allowed.' });
    return res.status(400).json({ error: `Upload error: ${err.message}` });
  }
  next(err);
});

// --- Global Error Handler ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  console.error('[Unhandled Error]', err.stack || err.message);
  res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
});

// --- 404 ---
app.use((req, res) => res.status(404).json({ error: 'Not Found' }));

// --- Start & Graceful Shutdown ---
const server = app.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(`Server is running on port ${port}`);
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
    console.log('[INFO] Run `npm audit` regularly to check for vulnerable dependencies.');
  }
});
const shutdown = (signal) => () => {
  console.log(`[${signal}] Shutting down...`);
  server.close(err => process.exit(err ? 1 : 0));
};
process.on('SIGTERM', shutdown('SIGTERM'));
process.on('SIGINT', shutdown('SIGINT'));
