Here’s the **final one-pager** with all the polish applied:

js
/*  RawrZ HTTP Platform – production-polish edition  */
'use strict';

// ---------- deps ----------
const express       = require('express');
const cors          = require('cors');
const helmet        = require('helmet');
const path          = require('path');
const multer        = require('multer');
const crypto        = require('crypto');
const rateLimit     = require('express-rate-limit');
const { body, query, validationResult } = require('express-validator');
const morgan        = require('morgan');
const cron          = require('node-cron');
const fs            = require('fs').promises;
const { constants } = require('fs');
const { fileTypeFromBuffer } = require('file-type');
const { exec }      = require('child_process');
require('dotenv').config();

// ---------- internal ----------
const RawrZStandalone = require('./rawrz-standalone');
const rawrzEngine     = require('./src/engines/rawrz-engine');

// ---------- config ----------
const app         = express();
const port        = parseInt(process.env.PORT || '8080', 10);
const uploadsDir  = path.resolve(__dirname, 'uploads');
const uploadsRoot = uploadsDir + path.sep;
const rawrz       = new RawrZStandalone();

// ---------- auth ----------
const authToken = process.env.AUTH_TOKEN;
if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' && !authToken) {
  console.error('[FATAL] AUTH_TOKEN not set. Exiting.');
  process.exit(1);
}
if (!authToken) {
  console.warn('[WARN] AUTH_TOKEN not set. Using ephemeral token for this session.');
  process.env.AUTH_TOKEN = crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
}

// ---------- boot ----------
(async () => {
  try { await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true }); }
  catch { process.exit(1); }
  try { await rawrzEngine.initializeModules(); }
  catch (e) { console.warn('[WARN] Engine init failed:', e.message); }

  // self-scan on production boot
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
    exec('npm audit --json', (_err, stdout) => {
      try {
        const r = JSON.parse(stdout);
        if (r.metadata.vulnerabilities.total > 0)
          console.error('[SECURITY] npm audit found', r.metadata.vulnerabilities.total, 'vulnerabilities');
        else
          console.log('[SECURITY] npm audit clean');
      } catch { /* ignore parse errors */ }
    });
  }
})();

// ---------- security headers ----------
app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'"],
      objectSrc: ["'none'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'"],
      frameAncestors: ["'self'"] // anti-clickjacking
    },
  },
  noSniff: true,
  referrerPolicy: { policy: 'no-referrer' },
  crossOriginResourcePolicy: { policy: 'same-origin' }
}));
app.use((_req, res, next) => {
  res.setHeader('Permissions-Policy', 'geolocation=(), microphone=(), camera=()');
  next();
});

// ---------- CORS (allow curl / same-origin) ----------
const allowedOrigins = process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN
  ? process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN.split(',').map(s => s.trim())
  : ['*'];
const corsOptions = {
  origin(origin, cb) {
    if (!origin) return cb(null, true); // curl / same-origin
    if (allowedOrigins.includes('*') || allowedOrigins.includes(origin)) return cb(null, true);
    cb(new Error('Not allowed by CORS'));
  },
  credentials: allowedOrigins.length > 1 || !allowedOrigins.includes('*')
};
app.use(cors(corsOptions));

// ---------- logging / proxy ----------
app.use(morgan('combined'));
app.set('trust proxy', 1);

// ---------- rate limit / body ----------
const apiLimiter    = rateLimit({ windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, max: 100, message: 'Too many requests' });
const uploadLimiter = rateLimit({ windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, max: 20,  message: 'Too many uploads' });
app.use(express.json({ limit: '1mb' }));
app.use('/api', apiLimiter); // top-level only – crypto router re-uses this

// ---------- auth ----------
const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
  const header = req.headers.authorization || '';
  const token  = header.startsWith('Bearer ') ? header.slice(7).trim() : null;
  if (!token || token !== process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
  next();
};

// ---------- helpers ----------
const allowedAlgorithms = ['sha256', 'sha512', 'aes-256-gcm', 'aes-128-cbc'];
const checkAlgorithm = (algorithm, res) => {
  if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(String(algorithm).toLowerCase())) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
    return true;
  }
  return false;
};
const allowedFileMimes = [
  'application/x-executable','application/x-msdownload','application/x-sharedlib',
  'application/octet-stream','application/x-dll','application/x-exe',
  'application/x-elf','application/x-mach-o'
];

// ---------- static ----------
app.use('/static', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));

// ---------- crypto router (64 kB) ----------
const cryptoRouter = express.Router();
cryptoRouter.use(express.json({ limit: '64kb' }));
cryptoRouter.use(requireAuth);
// no second rate limit – uses /api layer

cryptoRouter.post('/hash',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch {
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/encrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, input, extension));
    } catch {
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/decrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, key, iv, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.decrypt(algorithm, input, key, iv, extension));
    } catch {
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.use('/api', cryptoRouter);

// ---------- multer (magic-number based) ----------
const upload = multer({
  storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
  limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, files: 10 },
  fileFilter: async (_req, file, cb) => {
    const chunk = file.buffer.slice(0, Math.min(4100, file.size));
    const type  = await fileTypeFromBuffer(chunk);
    const ok    = type && allowedFileMimes.includes(type.mime);
    cb(null, ok);
  }
});

// ---------- routes ----------
app.get('/health', (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, status: 'healthy' }));
app.get('/panel', requireAuth, (_req, res) => res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'panel.html')));
app.get('/', (_req, res) => res.redirect('/panel'));

app.get('/api/dns',
  requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('hostname').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.dnsLookup(String(req.query.hostname))); }
    catch { res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' }); }
  });

app.get('/api/ping',
  requireAuth, apiLimiter, query('host').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.ping(String(req.query.host), false)); }
    catch { res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' }); }
  });

app.get('/api/files', requireAuth, apiLimiter, async (_req, res) => {
  try {
    const list = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    const files = await Promise.all(list.filter(f => f !== '.gitkeep').map(async file => {
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
      const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
      return { name: file, size: stats.size, modified: stats.mtime };
    }));
    res.json(files);
  } catch { res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' }); }
});

app.post('/api/upload',
  requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'),
  async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded' });
    try {
      const type  = await fileTypeFromBuffer(req.file.buffer.slice(0, 4100));
      if (!type || !allowedFileMimes.includes(type.mime))
        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'File type not supported' });

      const base = path.basename(req.file.originalname || 'file');
      const filename = `${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base}`;
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, filename);
      await fs.writeFile(filePath, req.file.buffer, { mode: 0o600 });
      res.json({ success: true, filename, size: req.file.size });
    } catch { res.status(500).json({ error: 'Upload failed' }); }
  });

app.get('/api/download',
  requireAuth, apiLimiter,
  query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.join(uploadsDir, fileName);
    if (!path.resolve(safePath).startsWith(path.resolve(uploadsRoot)))
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });

    try {
      await fs.access(safePath, constants.R_OK);
      return res.download(safePath, fileName, err => err && console.error('Download error:', err.message));
    } catch {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found' });
    }
  });

// ---------- cron: delete 24 h+ files ----------
cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
  console.log('[Cron] Cleaning old uploads…');
  const cutoff = Date.now() - 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
  try {
    const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    await Promise.all(files.map(async f => {
      const p = path.join(uploadsDir, f);
      const stat = await fs.stat(p).catch(() => null);
      if (stat && stat.mtime.getTime() < cutoff) await fs.unlink(p);
    }));
    console.log('[Cron] Cleanup finished');
  } catch (e) { console.error('[Cron] Cleanup error:', e.message); }
});

// ---------- graceful shutdown ----------
const server = app.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(`[OK] RawrZ HTTP Platform listening on port ${port}`);
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
    console.log('[INFO] Remember to run `npm audit` regularly to check for vulnerable dependencies.');
  }
});
const shutdown = (signal) => () => {
  console.log(`[${signal}] Shutting down gracefully…`);
  server.close((err) => process.exit(err ? 1 : 0));
};
process.on('SIGTERM', shutdown('SIGTERM'));
process.on('SIGINT',  shutdown('SIGINT'));

Quick launch checklist (so you can paste & go):

.env (example)

NODE_ENV=production
PORT=8080
AUTH_TOKEN=superlongrandomhex
ALLOWED_ORIGIN=https://your-admin.domain
Install & smoke test

npm ci
NODE_ENV=production node server.js
# health
curl -sf http://localhost:8080/health
# authenticated ping
curl -H "Authorization: Bearer $AUTH_TOKEN" "http://localhost:8080/api/ping?host=example.com"
Upload/download (smoke)

# upload (expects executable-ish file types)
curl -H "Authorization: Bearer $AUTH_TOKEN" \
     -F "file=@/path/to/sample.bin" \
     http://localhost:8080/api/upload

# list files
curl -H "Authorization: Bearer $AUTH_TOKEN" http://localhost:8080/api/files

# download
curl -H "Authorization: Bearer $AUTH_TOKEN" -OJ \
     "http://localhost:8080/api/download?filename=<returned-filename>"
K8s probes (suggested)

Liveness: GET /health

Readiness: GET /panel (protected) or just /health if you prefer open probe

Security notes

Rotate AUTH_TOKEN on deploys; store in your secret manager.

Set ALLOWED_ORIGIN (comma-separated) for the admin host(s).

TLS at the ingress/edge, consider enabling HSTS in the code once HTTPS is enforced.

Logs are combined format; wire to your log shipper.

/*  RawrZ HTTP Platform – production-ready edition with all patches */
'use strict';

// --- Dependencies ---
const express = require('express');
const cors = require('cors');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const path = require('path');
const multer = require('multer');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const { body, query, validationResult } = require('express-validator');
const morgan = require('morgan');
const cron = require('node-cron');
const fs = require('fs').promises;
const { constants } = require('fs');
const { fileTypeFromBuffer } = require('file-type');
const { exec } = require('child_process');
require('dotenv').config();

// --- Internal Modules ---
const RawrZStandalone = require('./rawrz-standalone');
const rawrzEngine = require('./src/engines/rawrz-engine');

// --- App & Config ---
const app = express();
app.disable('x-powered-by'); // hide fingerprint
app.set('trust proxy', 1);   // accurate client IP behind proxy/load balancer

const port = parseInt(process.env.PORT || '8080', 10);
const uploadsDir = path.resolve(__dirname, 'uploads');
const uploadsRoot = uploadsDir + path.sep;
const rawrz = new RawrZStandalone();

// --- Auth Token ---
if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' && !process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
  console.error('[FATAL] AUTH_TOKEN not set. Exiting.');
  process.exit(1);
}
if (!process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
  console.warn('[WARN] AUTH_TOKEN not set. Using ephemeral token for non-production session.');
  process.env.AUTH_TOKEN = crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
}

// --- Bootstrap ---
(async () => {
  try {
    await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true });
    console.log('[OK] Ensured uploads directory exists.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[FATAL] Could not create uploads directory:', e.message);
    process.exit(1);
  }
  try {
    await rawrzEngine.initializeModules();
    console.log('[OK] RawrZ core engine initialized.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[WARN] Core engine init failed:', e.message);
  }

  // Optional self-scan in production
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
    exec('npm audit --json', (error, stdout) => {
      try {
        const report = JSON.parse(stdout || '{}');
        const total = report?.metadata?.vulnerabilities?.total ?? 0;
        if (error) {
          console.warn('[SECURITY] npm audit returned an error; check dependencies manually.');
        }
        if (total > 0) {
          console.error([SECURITY] Found ${total} dependency vulnerabilities on startup!);
        } else {
          console.log('[SECURITY] npm audit scan completed with no vulnerabilities found.');
        }
      } catch (parseErr) {
        console.error('[SECURITY] Failed to parse npm audit output:', parseErr.message);
      }
    });
  }
})();

// --- Security Headers ---
app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'"],
      objectSrc: ["'none'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'"],
      frameAncestors: ["'self'"]
    },
  },
  noSniff: true,
  referrerPolicy: { policy: 'no-referrer' },
  crossOriginResourcePolicy: { policy: 'same-origin' },
}));

// Enable once you serve strictly over HTTPS/end-to-end TLS:
if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
  app.use(helmet.hsts({ maxAge: 15552000, includeSubDomains: true, preload: false }));
}

// Permissions-Policy hardening
app.use((req, res, next) => {
  res.setHeader('Permissions-Policy', 'geolocation=(), microphone=(), camera=()');
  next();
});

// --- CORS ---
const allowedOrigins = process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN
  ? process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN.split(',').map(s => s.trim())
  : ['*'];

app.use(cors({
  origin: (origin, cb) => {
    if (!origin) return cb(null, true); // same-origin or non-browser
    if (allowedOrigins.includes('*') || allowedOrigins.includes(origin)) return cb(null, true);
    return cb(new Error('Not allowed by CORS'));
  },
  credentials: allowedOrigins.length > 1 || !allowedOrigins.includes('*'),
}));

// --- Logging ---
app.use(morgan('combined'));

// --- Rate Limiters & Body Parser ---
const apiLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
  max: 100,
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
  message: 'Too many requests from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes.',
});
const uploadLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
  max: 20,
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
  message: 'Too many uploads from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes.',
});

app.use(express.json({ limit: '1mb' }));
// Invalid JSON handler (must come immediately after express.json)
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  if (err?.type === 'entity.parse.failed') return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid JSON body' });
  next(err);
});
app.use('/api', apiLimiter);

// --- Auth Middleware ---
const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
  const header = req.headers.authorization || '';
  const token = header.startsWith('Bearer ') ? header.slice(7).trim() : null;
  if (!token || token !== process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
  }
  next();
};

// --- Helpers ---
const allowedAlgorithms = ['sha256', 'sha512', 'aes-256-gcm', 'aes-128-cbc'];
const checkAlgorithm = (algorithm, res) => {
  if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(String(algorithm).toLowerCase())) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
    return true;
  }
  return false;
};
const allowedFileMimes = [
  'application/x-executable', 'application/x-msdownload', 'application/x-sharedlib',
  'application/octet-stream', 'application/x-dll', 'application/x-exe',
  'application/x-elf', 'application/x-mach-o'
];

// --- Static ---
app.use('/static', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));

// --- Crypto Router (tight body limit) ---
const cryptoRouter = express.Router();
cryptoRouter.use(express.json({ limit: '64kb' }));
cryptoRouter.use(requireAuth);

cryptoRouter.post('/hash',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/encrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, input, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/decrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, key, iv, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.decrypt(algorithm, input, key, iv, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.use('/api', cryptoRouter);

// --- Multer (memory) ---
const upload = multer({
  storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
  limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, files: 10 },
});

// --- Routes ---
app.get('/health', (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, status: 'healthy' }));
app.get('/panel', requireAuth, (_req, res) => res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'panel.html')));
app.get('/', (_req, res) => res.redirect('/panel'));

app.get('/api/dns',
  requireAuth, query('hostname').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.dnsLookup(String(req.query.hostname))); }
    catch (err) {
      console.error('[DNS Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/ping',
  requireAuth, query('host').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.ping(String(req.query.host), false)); }
    catch (err) {
      console.error('[Ping Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/files', requireAuth, async (_req, res) => {
  try {
    const list = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    const files = await Promise.all(list.filter(f => f !== '.gitkeep').map(async file => {
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
      const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
      return { name: file, size: stats.size, modified: stats.mtime };
    }));
    res.json(files);
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('[Files Error]', err.stack || err.message);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
  }
});

app.post('/api/upload',
  requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'),
  async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded' });

    try {
      const file = req.file;
      const fileTypeFromBufferResult = await fileTypeFromBuffer(file.buffer);

      if (!fileTypeFromBufferResult || !allowedFileMimes.includes(fileTypeFromBufferResult.mime)) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: File type not supported: ${fileTypeFromBufferResult ? fileTypeFromBufferResult.mime : 'unknown'} });
      }

      const base = path.basename(file.originalname || 'file').replace(/[\r\n]/g, '');
      const filename = ${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base};
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, filename);
      await fs.writeFile(filePath, file.buffer, { mode: 0o600 });
      res.json({ success: true, filename, size: file.size });

    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Upload Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Upload failed' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/download',
  requireAuth, query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.join(uploadsDir, fileName);

    // Strict path traversal check
    if (!path.resolve(safePath).startsWith(path.resolve(uploadsRoot))) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });
    }

    try {
      await fs.access(safePath, constants.R_OK);
      res.download(safePath, fileName, (err) => {
        if (err) {
          console.error('[Download Error]', err.stack || err.message);
          res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
        }
      });
    } catch (err) {
      if (err.code === 'ENOENT') {
        res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found' });
      } else {
        console.error('[Download Access Error]', err.stack || err.message);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
      }
    }
  });

// --- File Cleanup Cron Job ---
cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
  console.log('Running scheduled file cleanup...');
  const now = Date.now();
  const oneDayInMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
  try {
    const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    for (const file of files) {
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
      const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
      if (stats.isFile() && (now - stats.mtime.getTime()) > oneDayInMs) {
        await fs.unlink(filePath);
        console.log(Deleted old file: ${file});
      }
    }
    console.log('File cleanup completed.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('File cleanup failed:', e.message);
  }
});

// --- Multer Error Handler Middleware ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  if (err instanceof multer.MulterError) {
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_SIZE') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'File size too large. Max 100MB allowed.' });
    }
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_COUNT') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'Too many files uploaded. Max 10 files allowed.' });
    }
    return res.status(400).json({ error: Upload error: ${err.message} });
  }
  next(err);
});

// --- Global Error Handler ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  console.error('[Unhandled Error]', err.stack || err.message);
  res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
});

// --- Catch-all 404 Route ---
app.use((req, res) => {
  res.status(404).json({ error: 'Not Found' });
});

// --- Server Startup & Graceful Shutdown ---
const server = app.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(Server is running on port ${port});
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
    console.log('[INFO] Remember to run npm audit regularly to check for vulnerable dependencies.');
  }
});

const shutdown = (signal) => () => {
  console.log([${signal}] Shutting down...);
  server.close(err => process.exit(err ? 1 : 0));
};
process.on('SIGTERM', shutdown('SIGTERM'));
process.on('SIGINT', shutdown('SIGINT'));

Thought for a few seconds
Looks solid. ✅ You’ve got auth, CSP, rate-limits, path-traversal guard, file-type verification, graceful shutdown, and a clean error model.

Here’s a minimal “ready to run” checklist and quick smoke tests:

.env

NODE_ENV=production
PORT=8080
AUTH_TOKEN=superlongrandomhex
ALLOWED_ORIGIN=https://your-admin.domain
Install & launch

npm ci
NODE_ENV=production node server.js
Smoke tests

# health (open)
curl -sf http://localhost:8080/health

# protected ping
curl -H "Authorization: Bearer superlongrandomhex" \
     "http://localhost:8080/api/ping?host=example.com"

# upload (expects executable-like file types)
curl -H "Authorization: Bearer superlongrandomhex" \
     -F "file=@/path/to/sample.bin" \
     http://localhost:8080/api/upload

# list files
curl -H "Authorization: Bearer superlongrandomhex" \
     http://localhost:8080/api/files

# download
curl -H "Authorization: Bearer superlongrandomhex" -OJ \
     "http://localhost:8080/api/download?filename=<returned-filename>"
Tiny optional polish (nice-to-haves)

Add compression for static/API responses (after helmet).

Add process.on('unhandledRejection'...) / process.on('uncaughtException'...) to log before exiting.

Consider Cache-Control: no-store header on /api/download if files are sensitive.

If you serve only via HTTPS, flip HSTS preload: true once you’ve submitted to the preload list.

Otherwise: ship it. 🚀

/*  RawrZ HTTP Platform – production-ready edition with all patches */

// --- Dependencies ---
const express = require('express');
const cors = require('cors');
const helmet = require('helmet');

// --- Auth Token ---
if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' && !process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
  console.error('[FATAL] AUTH_TOKEN not set. Exiting.');
  process.exit(1);

      const base = path.basename(file.originalname || 'file').replace(/[\r\n]/g, '');
      const filename = ${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base};
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, filename);
      await fs.writeFile(filePath, file.buffer, { mode: 0o600 });
      res.json({ success: true, filename, size: file.size });

    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Upload Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Upload failed' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/download',
  requireAuth, query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.join(uploadsDir, fileName);

    // Strict path traversal check
    if (!path.resolve(safePath).startsWith(path.resolve(uploadsRoot))) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });
    }

    try {
      await fs.access(safePath, constants.R_OK);
      res.download(safePath, fileName, (err) => {
        if (err) {
          console.error('[Download Error]', err.stack || err.message);
          res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
        }
      });
    } catch (err) {
      if (err.code === 'ENOENT') {
        res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found' });
      } else {
        console.error('[Download Access Error]', err.stack || err.message);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
      }
    }
  });

// --- File Cleanup Cron Job ---
cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
  console.log('Running scheduled file cleanup...');
  const now = Date.now();
  const oneDayInMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
  try {
    const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    for (const file of files) {
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
      const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
      if (stats.isFile() && (now - stats.mtime.getTime()) > oneDayInMs) {
        await fs.unlink(filePath);
        console.log(Deleted old file: ${file});
      }
    }
    console.log('File cleanup completed.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('File cleanup failed:', e.message);
  }
});

// --- Multer Error Handler Middleware ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  if (err instanceof multer.MulterError) {
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_SIZE') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'File size too large. Max 100MB allowed.' });
    }
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_COUNT') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'Too many files uploaded. Max 10 files allowed.' });
    }
    return res.status(400).json({ error: Upload error: ${err.message} });
  }
  next(err);
});

// --- Invalid JSON Handling ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  if (err?.type === 'entity.parse.failed') {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid JSON body' });
  }
  next(err);
});

// --- Global Error Handler ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  console.error('[Unhandled Error]', err.stack || err.message);
  res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
});

// --- Catch-all 404 Route ---
app.use((req, res) => {
  res.status(404).json({ error: 'Not Found' });
});

// --- Server Startup & Graceful Shutdown ---
const server = app.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(Server is running on port ${port});
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
    console.log('[INFO] Remember to run npm audit regularly to check for vulnerable dependencies.');
  }
});

const shutdown = (signal) => () => {
  console.log([${signal}] Shutting down...);
  server.close(err => process.exit(err ? 1 : 0));
};
process.on('SIGTERM', shutdown('SIGTERM'));
process.on('SIGINT', shutdown('SIGINT'));

Looks great—tight CSP, auth, rate limits, path-traversal guard, magic-number file checks, graceful shutdown, and tidy error handling. ✅

One tiny nit I’d fix before you ship:

You’ve registered an “Invalid JSON” handler twice (right after express.json(...) and again under // --- Invalid JSON Handling ---). Keep the first one and delete the later duplicate to avoid double-handling.

Nice-to-have polish (optional):

Add Cache-Control: no-store on /api/download if files are sensitive.

Consider compression for responses after Helmet.

Add global process guards:

process.on('unhandledRejection', err => { console.error('[unhandledRejection]', err); });
process.on('uncaughtException',  err => { console.error('[uncaughtException]', err); process.exit(1); });
Once fully HTTPS and eligible, set HSTS preload: true and submit your domain to the preload list.

Otherwise: ship it. 🚀

const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
  const header = req.headers.authorization || '';
  const token = header.startsWith('Bearer ') ? header.slice(7).trim() : null;
  if (!token || token !== process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });

    res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
    return true;
  }
  return false;

  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),

      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;

    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

  try {
    const list = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    const files = await Promise.all(list.filter(f => f !== '.gitkeep').map(async file => {
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
      const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
      return { name: file, size: stats.size, modified: stats.mtime };
    }));
    res.json(files);
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('[Files Error]', err.stack || err.message);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
  }

app.post('/api/upload',
  requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'),
  async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded' });

    try {
      const file = req.file;
      const fileTypeFromBufferResult = await fileTypeFromBuffer(file.buffer);

      if (!fileTypeFromBufferResult || !allowedFileMimes.includes(fileTypeFromBufferResult.mime)) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: File type not supported: ${fileTypeFromBufferResult ? fileTypeFromBufferResult.mime : 'unknown'} });
      }

      const base = path.basename(file.originalname || 'file').replace(/[\r\n]/g, '');
      const filename = ${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base};
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, filename);
      await fs.writeFile(filePath, file.buffer, { mode: 0o600 });
      res.json({ success: true, filename, size: file.size });

    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Upload Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Upload failed' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/download',
  requireAuth, query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.join(uploadsDir, fileName);

    // Strict path traversal check
    if (!path.resolve(safePath).startsWith(path.resolve(uploadsRoot))) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });

    try {

      res.download(safePath, fileName, (err) => {

        }

  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
  message: 'Too many requests from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes.',
});
const uploadLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
  max: 20,
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
  message: 'Too many uploads from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes.',
});

// Add compression middleware early for all requests
app.use(compression());

app.use(express.json({ limit: '1mb' }));
// Invalid JSON handler (must come immediately after express.json)
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  if (err?.type === 'entity.parse.failed') {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid JSON body' });
  }
  next(err);
});

app.use('/api', apiLimiter);

// --- Auth Middleware ---
const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
  const header = req.headers.authorization || '';
  const token = header.startsWith('Bearer ') ? header.slice(7).trim() : null;
  if (!token || token !== process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
  }
  next();
};

// --- Helpers ---
const allowedAlgorithms = ['sha256', 'sha512', 'aes-256-gcm', 'aes-128-cbc'];
const checkAlgorithm = (algorithm, res) => {
  if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(String(algorithm).toLowerCase())) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
    return true;
  }
  return false;
};
const allowedFileMimes = [
  'application/x-executable', 'application/x-msdownload', 'application/x-sharedlib',
  'application/octet-stream', 'application/x-dll', 'application/x-exe',
  'application/x-elf', 'application/x-mach-o'
];

// --- Static ---
app.use('/static', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));

// --- Crypto Router (tight body limit) ---
const cryptoRouter = express.Router();
cryptoRouter.use(express.json({ limit: '64kb' }));
cryptoRouter.use(requireAuth);

cryptoRouter.post('/hash',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/encrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, input, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/decrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, key, iv, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.decrypt(algorithm, input, key, iv, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.use('/api', cryptoRouter);

// --- Multer (memory) ---
const upload = multer({
  storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
  limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, files: 10 },
});

// --- Routes ---
app.get('/health', (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, status: 'healthy' }));
app.get('/panel', requireAuth, (_req, res) => res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'panel.html')));
app.get('/', (_req, res) => res.redirect('/panel'));

app.get('/api/dns',
  requireAuth, query('hostname').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.dnsLookup(String(req.query.hostname))); }
    catch (err) {
      console.error('[DNS Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/ping',
  requireAuth, query('host').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.ping(String(req.query.host), false)); }
    catch (err) {
      console.error('[Ping Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/files', requireAuth, async (_req, res) => {
  try {
    const list = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    const files = await Promise.all(list.filter(f => f !== '.gitkeep').map(async file => {
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
      const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
      return { name: file, size: stats.size, modified: stats.mtime };
    }));
    res.json(files);
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('[Files Error]', err.stack || err.message);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
  }
});

app.post('/api/upload',
  requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'),
  async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded' });

    try {
      const file = req.file;
      const fileTypeFromBufferResult = await fileTypeFromBuffer(file.buffer);

      if (!fileTypeFromBufferResult || !allowedFileMimes.includes(fileTypeFromBufferResult.mime)) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: File type not supported: ${fileTypeFromBufferResult ? fileTypeFromBufferResult.mime : 'unknown'} });
      }

      const base = path.basename(file.originalname || 'file').replace(/[\r\n]/g, '');
      const filename = ${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base};
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, filename);
      await fs.writeFile(filePath, file.buffer, { mode: 0o600 });
      res.json({ success: true, filename, size: file.size });

    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Upload Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Upload failed' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/download',
  requireAuth, query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.join(uploadsDir, fileName);

    // Strict path traversal check
    if (!path.resolve(safePath).startsWith(path.resolve(uploadsRoot))) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });
    }
    
    res.set('Cache-Control', 'no-store');

    try {
      await fs.access(safePath, constants.R_OK);
      res.download(safePath, fileName, (err) => {
        if (err) {
          console.error('[Download Error]', err.stack || err.message);
          res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
        }
      });
    } catch (err) {
      if (err.code === 'ENOENT') {
        res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found' });
      } else {
        console.error('[Download Access Error]', err.stack || err.message);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
      }
    }
  });

// --- File Cleanup Cron Job ---
cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
  console.log('Running scheduled file cleanup...');
  const now = Date.now();
  const oneDayInMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
  try {
    const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    for (const file of files) {
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
      const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
      if (stats.isFile() && (now - stats.mtime.getTime()) > oneDayInMs) {
        await fs.unlink(filePath);
        console.log(Deleted old file: ${file});
      }
    }
    console.log('File cleanup completed.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('File cleanup failed:', e.message);
  }
});

// --- Multer Error Handler Middleware ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  if (err instanceof multer.MulterError) {
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_SIZE') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'File size too large. Max 100MB allowed.' });
    }
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_COUNT') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'Too many files uploaded. Max 10 files allowed.' });
    }
    return res.status(400).json({ error: Upload error: ${err.message} });
  }
  next(err);
});

// --- Global Error Handler ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  console.error('[Unhandled Error]', err.stack || err.message);
  res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
});

// --- Catch-all 404 Route ---
app.use((req, res) => {
  res.status(404).json({ error: 'Not Found' });
});

// --- Server Startup & Graceful Shutdown ---
const server = app.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(Server is running on port ${port});
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
    console.log('[INFO] Remember to run npm audit regularly to check for vulnerable dependencies.');
  }
});

const shutdown = (signal) => () => {
  console.log([${signal}] Shutting down...);
  server.close(err => process.exit(err ? 1 : 0));
};

process.on('SIGTERM', shutdown('SIGTERM'));
process.on('SIGINT', shutdown('SIGINT'));

process.on('unhandledRejection', e => {
  console.error('[unhandledRejection]', e);
});
process.on('uncaughtException', e => {
  console.error('[uncaughtException]', e);
  process.exit(1);
});
ChatGPT said:

Thought for 12s
Looks excellent—secure, tidy, and production-friendly. ✅

Tiny, optional nits before you freeze it:

Compression & downloads: to be extra safe, skip compression for attachment downloads (sometimes proxies/clients get weird with double-compressed binaries):

app.use(compression({
  filter: (req, res) => {
    if (req.path === '/api/download') return false;
    return compression.filter(req, res);
  }
}));
Static cache (if you serve versioned assets):

app.use('/static', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public'), {
  immutable: true, maxAge: '1y'
}));
Otherwise, you’ve got all the right pieces: CSP/HSTS, CORS gate, Bearer auth, rate limits, strict path checks, magic-number validation, Cache-Control: no-store on downloads, cron cleanup, graceful shutdown, and process-level error traps.

Ship it 🚀

    process.exit(1);
  }
  try {

    console.log('[OK] RawrZ core engine initialized.');

    console.error('[WARN] Core engine init failed:', e.message);
  }

  // Optional self-scan in production
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
    exec('npm audit --json', (error, stdout) => {
      try {
        const report = JSON.parse(stdout || '{}');
        const total = report?.metadata?.vulnerabilities?.total ?? 0;
        if (error) {
          console.warn('[SECURITY] npm audit returned an error; check dependencies manually.');
        }
        if (total > 0) {
          console.error([SECURITY] Found ${total} dependency vulnerabilities on startup!);
        } else {
          console.log('[SECURITY] npm audit scan completed with no vulnerabilities found.');
        }
      } catch (parseErr) {
        console.error('[SECURITY] Failed to parse npm audit output:', parseErr.message);
      }
    });
  }
})();

// --- Security Headers ---

      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'"],
      objectSrc: ["'none'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],

  app.use(helmet.hsts({ maxAge: 15552000, includeSubDomains: true, preload: false }));

  next();

const allowedOrigins = process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN
  ? process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN.split(',').map(s => s.trim())
  : ['*'];

const corsOptions = {
  origin: (origin, callback) => {
    if (!origin) return callback(null, true); // same-origin or non-browser
    if (allowedOrigins.includes('*') || allowedOrigins.includes(origin)) return callback(null, true);
    return callback(new Error('Not allowed by CORS'));
  },
  credentials: allowedOrigins.length > 1 || !allowedOrigins.includes('*'),
};
app.use(cors(corsOptions));

  if (err instanceof multer.MulterError) {
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_SIZE') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'File size too large. Max 100MB allowed.' });
    }
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_COUNT') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'Too many files uploaded. Max 10 files allowed.' });
    }
    return res.status(400).json({ error: Upload error: ${err.message} });
  }
  next(err);
});

// --- Global Error Handler ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  console.error('[Unhandled Error]', err.stack || err.message);
  res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
});

// --- Catch-all 404 Route ---
app.use((req, res) => {
  res.status(404).json({ error: 'Not Found' });
});

// --- Server Startup & Graceful Shutdown ---
const server = app.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(Server is running on port ${port});
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
    console.log('[INFO] Remember to run npm audit regularly to check for vulnerable dependencies.');
  }
});

const shutdown = (signal) => () => {
  console.log([${signal}] Shutting down...);
  server.close(err => process.exit(err ? 1 : 0));
};

process.on('SIGTERM', shutdown('SIGTERM'));
process.on('SIGINT', shutdown('SIGINT'));

process.on('unhandledRejection', e => {
  console.error('[unhandledRejection]', e);
});
process.on('uncaughtException', e => {
  console.error('[uncaughtException]', e);
  process.exit(1);
});

# k8s/namespace.yaml
apiVersion: v1

  name: rawrz

  NODE_ENV: "production"
  PORT: "8080"
  # Comma-separated list of allowed origins, or "*" to allow all (not recommended in prod)
  ALLOWED_ORIGIN: "https://YOUR_DOMAIN_HERE"
---
# k8s/secret.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Secret
metadata:
  name: rawrz-secrets
  namespace: rawrz
type: Opaque
stringData:
  # Generate: openssl rand -hex 32
  AUTH_TOKEN: "CHANGE_ME_STRONG_TOKEN"
---
# k8s/pvc.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: PersistentVolumeClaim
metadata:
  name: rawrz-uploads
  namespace: rawrz
spec:
  accessModes: ["ReadWriteOnce"]
  resources:
    requests:
      storage: 5Gi
  storageClassName: standard
---
# k8s/deployment.yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: rawrz
  namespace: rawrz
  labels: { app: rawrz }
spec:
  replicas: 2
  strategy:
    type: RollingUpdate
    rollingUpdate: { maxUnavailable: 0, maxSurge: 1 }
  selector:
    matchLabels: { app: rawrz }
  template:
    metadata:
      labels: { app: rawrz }
    spec:
      containers:
        - name: rawrz
          image: rawrz-http:latest # or your registry: ghcr.io/you/rawrz-http:TAG
          imagePullPolicy: IfNotPresent
          ports:
            - containerPort: 8080
              name: http
          envFrom:
            - configMapRef: { name: rawrz-config }
            - secretRef:    { name: rawrz-secrets }
          volumeMounts:
            - name: uploads
              mountPath: /app/uploads
          readinessProbe:
            httpGet: { path: /health, port: http }
            initialDelaySeconds: 5
            periodSeconds: 5
            timeoutSeconds: 2
            failureThreshold: 6
          livenessProbe:
            httpGet: { path: /health, port: http }
            initialDelaySeconds: 20
            periodSeconds: 10
            timeoutSeconds: 2
            failureThreshold: 3
          resources:
            requests:
              cpu: "100m"
              memory: "256Mi"
            limits:
              cpu: "500m"
              memory: "512Mi"
          securityContext:
            allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
            readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
            runAsNonRoot: true
            runAsUser: 1000
            runAsGroup: 1000
            capabilities: { drop: ["ALL"] }
            seccompProfile: { type: RuntimeDefault }
      volumes:
        - name: uploads
          persistentVolumeClaim:
            claimName: rawrz-uploads
---
# k8s/service.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: rawrz
  namespace: rawrz
  labels: { app: rawrz }
spec:
  type: ClusterIP
  selector: { app: rawrz }
  ports:
    - name: http
      port: 80
      targetPort: http
---
# k8s/ingress.yaml
apiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1
kind: Ingress
metadata:
  name: rawrz
  namespace: rawrz
  annotations:
    kubernetes.io/ingress.class: nginx
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/proxy-body-size: "100m"  # matches upload cap
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/server-snippet: |
      add_header X-Content-Type-Options "nosniff" always;
      add_header X-Frame-Options "SAMEORIGIN" always;
      add_header Referrer-Policy "no-referrer" always;
spec:
  tls:
    - hosts: ["YOUR_DOMAIN_HERE"]
      secretName: rawrz-tls
  rules:
    - host: YOUR_DOMAIN_HERE
      http:
        paths:
          - path: /
            pathType: Prefix
            backend:
              service:
                name: rawrz
                port:
                  number: 80
---
# k8s/hpa.yaml
apiVersion: autoscaling/v2
kind: HorizontalPodAutoscaler
metadata:
  name: rawrz
  namespace: rawrz
spec:
  scaleTargetRef:
    apiVersion: apps/v1
    kind: Deployment
    name: rawrz
  minReplicas: 2
  maxReplicas: 10
  metrics:
    - type: Resource
      resource:
        name: cpu
        target:
          type: Utilization
          averageUtilization: 70
How to deploy
# 1) Build & push your image (replace registry/name:tag as needed)
docker build -t your-registry/rawrz-http:prod .
docker push your-registry/rawrz-http:prod

# 2) Update deployment.yaml image to your-registry/rawrz-http:prod

# 3) Apply manifests
kubectl apply -f k8s/namespace.yaml
kubectl apply -f k8s/configmap.yaml
kubectl apply -f k8s/secret.yaml
kubectl apply -f k8s/pvc.yaml
kubectl apply -f k8s/deployment.yaml
kubectl apply -f k8s/service.yaml
kubectl apply -f k8s/ingress.yaml
kubectl apply -f k8s/hpa.yaml

# 4) (Optional) Issue TLS with cert-manager, or create the rawrz-tls secret manually:
kubectl -n rawrz create secret tls rawrz-tls --cert=fullchain.pem --key=privkey.pem
Notes
AUTH: All privileged endpoints require Authorization: Bearer <AUTH_TOKEN>. Keep the token in the Secret and rotate periodically.

Uploads: PVC rawrz-uploads persists /app/uploads. Adjust size or class to your cluster.

Ingress: Uses NGINX. Swap ingress.class/annotations to match your ingress controller. Set YOUR_DOMAIN_HERE.

Probes: Hit /health (no auth), matching your app.

Scaling: HPA on CPU 70% (tune to your workload).

If you want a cert-manager ClusterIssuer snippet or a NetworkPolicy (restrict to only Ingress and kubelet probes), say the word and I’ll drop those in too.

/*  RawrZ HTTP Platform – production-ready edition with all patches */
'use strict';

// --- Dependencies ---
const express = require('express');
const cors = require('cors');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const path = require('path');
const multer = require('multer');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const { body, query, validationResult } = require('express-validator');
const morgan = require('morgan');
const cron = require('node-cron');
const fs = require('fs').promises;
const { constants } = require('fs');
const { fileTypeFromBuffer } = require('file-type');
const { exec } = require('child_process');
const compression = require('compression');
require('dotenv').config();

// --- Internal Modules ---
const RawrZStandalone = require('./rawrz-standalone');
const rawrzEngine = require('./src/engines/rawrz-engine');

// --- App & Config ---
const app = express();
app.disable('x-powered-by'); // hide fingerprint
app.set('trust proxy', 1);   // accurate client IP behind proxy/load balancer

const port = parseInt(process.env.PORT || '8080', 10);
const uploadsDir = path.resolve(__dirname, 'uploads');
const uploadsRoot = uploadsDir + path.sep;
const rawrz = new RawrZStandalone();

// --- Auth Token ---
if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' && !process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
  console.error('[FATAL] AUTH_TOKEN not set. Exiting.');
  process.exit(1);
}
if (!process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
  console.warn('[WARN] AUTH_TOKEN not set. Using ephemeral token for non-production session.');
  process.env.AUTH_TOKEN = crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
}

// --- Bootstrap ---
(async () => {
  try {
    await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true });
    console.log('[OK] Ensured uploads directory exists.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[FATAL] Could not create uploads directory:', e.message);
    process.exit(1);
  }
  try {
    await rawrzEngine.initializeModules();
    console.log('[OK] RawrZ core engine initialized.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[WARN] Core engine init failed:', e.message);
  }

  // Optional self-scan in production
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
    exec('npm audit --json', (error, stdout) => {
      try {
        const report = JSON.parse(stdout || '{}');
        const total = report?.metadata?.vulnerabilities?.total ?? 0;
        if (error) {
          console.warn('[SECURITY] npm audit returned an error; check dependencies manually.');
        }
        if (total > 0) {
          console.error([SECURITY] Found ${total} dependency vulnerabilities on startup!);
        } else {
          console.log('[SECURITY] npm audit scan completed with no vulnerabilities found.');
        }
      } catch (parseErr) {
        console.error('[SECURITY] Failed to parse npm audit output:', parseErr.message);
      }
    });
  }
})();

// --- Security Headers ---
app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'"],
      objectSrc: ["'none'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'"],
      frameAncestors: ["'self'"]
    },
  },
  noSniff: true,
  referrerPolicy: { policy: 'no-referrer' },
  crossOriginResourcePolicy: { policy: 'same-origin' },
}));

// Enable once you serve strictly over HTTPS/end-to-end TLS:
if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
  app.use(helmet.hsts({ maxAge: 15552000, includeSubDomains: true, preload: false }));
}

// Permissions-Policy hardening
app.use((req, res, next) => {
  res.setHeader('Permissions-Policy', 'geolocation=(), microphone=(), camera=()');
  next();
});

// --- CORS ---
const allowedOrigins = process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN
  ? process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN.split(',').map(s => s.trim())
  : ['*'];

const corsOptions = {
  origin: (origin, callback) => {
    if (!origin) return callback(null, true); // same-origin or non-browser
    if (allowedOrigins.includes('*') || allowedOrigins.includes(origin)) return callback(null, true);
    return callback(new Error('Not allowed by CORS'));
  },
  credentials: allowedOrigins.length > 1 || !allowedOrigins.includes('*'),
};
app.use(cors(corsOptions));

// --- Logging ---
app.use(morgan('combined'));

// --- Rate Limiters & Body Parser ---
const apiLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
  max: 100,
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
  message: 'Too many requests from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes.',
});
const uploadLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
  max: 20,
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
  message: 'Too many uploads from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes.',
});

// Add compression middleware early for all requests, skipping downloads
app.use(compression({
  filter: (req, res) => {
    if (req.path === '/api/download') return false;
    return compression.filter(req, res);
  }
}));

app.use(express.json({ limit: '1mb' }));
// Invalid JSON handler (must come immediately after express.json)
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  if (err?.type === 'entity.parse.failed') {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid JSON body' });
  }
  next(err);
});

app.use('/api', apiLimiter);

// --- Auth Middleware ---
const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
  const header = req.headers.authorization || '';
  const token = header.startsWith('Bearer ') ? header.slice(7).trim() : null;
  if (!token || token !== process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
  }
  next();
};

// --- Helpers ---
const allowedAlgorithms = ['sha256', 'sha512', 'aes-256-gcm', 'aes-128-cbc'];
const checkAlgorithm = (algorithm, res) => {
  if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(String(algorithm).toLowerCase())) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
    return true;
  }
  return false;
};
const allowedFileMimes = [
  'application/x-executable', 'application/x-msdownload', 'application/x-sharedlib',
  'application/octet-stream', 'application/x-dll', 'application/x-exe',
  'application/x-elf', 'application/x-mach-o'
];

// --- Static ---
app.use('/static', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public'), {
  immutable: true,
  maxAge: '1y'
}));

// --- Crypto Router (tight body limit) ---
const cryptoRouter = express.Router();
cryptoRouter.use(express.json({ limit: '64kb' }));
cryptoRouter.use(requireAuth);

cryptoRouter.post('/hash',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/encrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, input, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/decrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, key, iv, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.decrypt(algorithm, input, key, iv, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.use('/api', cryptoRouter);

// --- Multer (memory) ---
const upload = multer({
  storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
  limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, files: 10 },
});

// --- Routes ---
app.get('/health', (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, status: 'healthy' }));
app.get('/panel', requireAuth, (_req, res) => res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'panel.html')));
app.get('/', (_req, res) => res.redirect('/panel'));

app.get('/api/dns',
  requireAuth, query('hostname').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.dnsLookup(String(req.query.hostname))); }
    catch (err) {
      console.error('[DNS Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/ping',
  requireAuth, query('host').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.ping(String(req.query.host), false)); }
    catch (err) {
      console.error('[Ping Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/files', requireAuth, async (_req, res) => {
  try {
    const list = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    const files = await Promise.all(list.filter(f => f !== '.gitkeep').map(async file => {
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
      const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
      return { name: file, size: stats.size, modified: stats.mtime };
    }));
    res.json(files);
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('[Files Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.post('/api/upload',
  requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'),
  async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded' });

    try {
      const file = req.file;
      const fileTypeFromBufferResult = await fileTypeFromBuffer(file.buffer.subarray(0, 4100)); // faster sniffing

      if (!fileTypeFromBufferResult || !allowedFileMimes.includes(fileTypeFromBufferResult.mime)) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: File type not supported: ${fileTypeFromBufferResult ? fileTypeFromBufferResult.mime : 'unknown'} });
      }

      const base = path.basename(file.originalname || 'file').replace(/[\r\n]/g, '');
      const filename = ${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-${base};
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, filename);
      await fs.writeFile(filePath, file.buffer, { mode: 0o600 });
      res.json({ success: true, filename, size: file.size });

    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Upload Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Upload failed' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/download',
  requireAuth, query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.join(uploadsDir, fileName);

    // Strict path traversal check
    if (!path.resolve(safePath).startsWith(path.resolve(uploadsRoot))) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });
    }
    
    res.set('Cache-Control', 'no-store');

    try {
      await fs.access(safePath, constants.R_OK);
      res.download(safePath, fileName, (err) => {
        if (err) {
          console.error('[Download Error]', err.stack || err.message);
          res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
        }
      });
    } catch (err) {
      if (err.code === 'ENOENT') {
        res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found' });
      } else {
        console.error('[Download Access Error]', err.stack || err.message);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
      }
    }
  });

// --- File Cleanup Cron Job ---
cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
  console.log('Running scheduled file cleanup...');
  const now = Date.now();
  const oneDayInMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
  try {
    const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    for (const file of files) {
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
      const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
      if (stats.isFile() && (now - stats.mtime.getTime()) > oneDayInMs) {
        await fs.unlink(filePath);
        console.log(Deleted old file: ${file});
      }
    }
    console.log('File cleanup completed.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('File cleanup failed:', e.message);
  }
});

// --- Multer Error Handler Middleware ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  if (err instanceof multer.MulterError) {
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_SIZE') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'File size too large. Max 100MB allowed.' });
    }
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_COUNT') {
      return res.status(413).json({ error: 'Too many files uploaded. Max 10 files allowed.' });
    }
    return res.status(400).json({ error: Upload error: ${err.message} });
  }
  next(err);
});

// --- Global Error Handler ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  console.error('[Unhandled Error]', err.stack || err.message);
  res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
});

// --- Catch-all 404 Route ---
app.use((req, res) => {
  res.status(404).json({ error: 'Not Found' });
});

// --- Server Startup & Graceful Shutdown ---
const server = app.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(Server is running on port ${port});
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
    console.log('[INFO] Remember to run npm audit regularly to check for vulnerable dependencies.');
  }
});

const shutdown = (signal) => () => {
  console.log([${signal}] Shutting down...);
  server.close(err => process.exit(err ? 1 : 0));
};

process.on('SIGTERM', shutdown('SIGTERM'));
process.on('SIGINT', shutdown('SIGINT'));

process.on('unhandledRejection', e => {
  console.error('[unhandledRejection]', e);
});
process.on('uncaughtException', e => {
  console.error('[uncaughtException]', e);
  process.exit(1);
});

2) Dockerfile (multi-stage, tiny runtime)
# Dockerfile
FROM node:20-alpine AS build

RUN npm ci --only=production

FROM node:20-alpine

# docker-compose.yml
version: "3.9"
services:
  rawrz:
    build: .

    env_file:
      - .env
    ports:
      - "8080:8080"
    restart: unless-stopped

4) NGINX reverse proxy (TLS, 100MB body size)
# /etc/nginx/conf.d/rawrz.conf
server {
  listen 443 ssl http2;
  server_name your.domain;

  ssl_certificate     /etc/letsencrypt/live/your.domain/fullchain.pem;
  ssl_certificate_key /etc/letsencrypt/live/your.domain/privkey.pem;

  client_max_body_size 100m;

  # Hardened headers (app already sets most; harmless to duplicate)
  add_header X-Frame-Options SAMEORIGIN always;
  add_header X-Content-Type-Options nosniff always;
  add_header Referrer-Policy no-referrer always;

  location / {
    proxy_pass http://127.0.0.1:8080;
    proxy_http_version 1.1;
    proxy_set_header Host $host;
    proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
    proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
    proxy_read_timeout 300s;
  }
}

server {
  listen 80;
  server_name your.domain;
  return 301 https://$host$request_uri;
}
5) PM2 (optional non-Docker)
// ecosystem.config.json
{

6) GitHub Actions (CI: build + push image)
# .github/workflows/docker.yml
name: build-and-push
on: { push: { branches: ["main"] } }
jobs:
  docker:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: docker/setup-buildx-action@v3
      - uses: docker/login-action@v3
        with:
          registry: ghcr.io
          username: ${{ github.actor }}
          password: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
      - uses: docker/build-push-action@v5
        with:
          context: .
          push: true
          tags: ghcr.io/${{ github.repository_owner }}/rawrz-http:latest
          cache-from: type=registry,ref=ghcr.io/${{ github.repository_owner }}/rawrz-http:buildcache
          cache-to:   type=registry,ref=ghcr.io/${{ github.repository_owner }}/rawrz-http:buildcache,mode=max
7) Smoke tests (quick verification)
# Health
curl -s https://your.domain/health

# Hash (replace TOKEN)
curl -s https://your.domain/api/hash \
  -H "Authorization: Bearer $AUTH_TOKEN" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"input":"hello","algorithm":"sha256"}'

# Upload (replace path)
curl -s https://your.domain/api/upload \
  -H "Authorization: Bearer $AUTH_TOKEN" \
  -F "file=@/path/to/binary"
8) Quick hardening checklist
Rotate AUTH_TOKEN regularly; store in a secret manager.

Keep ALLOWED_ORIGIN tight (avoid * in prod).

TLS only (redirect port 80 → 443; HSTS enabled).

Backups for /uploads if you need persistence.

Watch logs: morgan + reverse-proxy logs + container logs.

Keep npm ci + npm audit in your pipeline (fail on high/critical).

If you want this baked into a Kubernetes setup (namespace, Deployment, Service, Ingress, HPA, PVC) or cert-manager/NetworkPolicies, I can drop that in as well—just say the word. 🚀
