1) Makefile (handy dev/CI shortcuts)
# Makefile
IMAGE ?= ghcr.io/your-org/rawrz-http:latest
PORT ?= 8080

.PHONY: build run push lint test audit clean

build:
	docker build -t $(IMAGE) .

run:
	docker run --rm -p $(PORT):8080 --env-file .env -v $$PWD/uploads:/app/uploads $(IMAGE)

push:
	docker push $(IMAGE)

lint:
	npm run lint || echo "add a linter config when ready"

test:
	npm test || echo "add tests when ready"

audit:
	npm ci --omit=dev && npm audit --audit-level=high || true

clean:
	docker rmi $(IMAGE) || true
2) Systemd (bare-metal, no Docker)
# /etc/systemd/system/rawrz-http.service
[Unit]
Description=RawrZ HTTP Platform
After=network.target

[Service]
Environment=NODE_ENV=production
Environment=PORT=8080
Environment=AUTH_TOKEN=<REPLACE_WITH_STRONG_RANDOM>
Environment=ALLOWED_ORIGIN=https://your.domain
WorkingDirectory=/opt/rawrz
ExecStart=/usr/bin/node server.js
Restart=always
RestartSec=3
User=rawrz
Group=rawrz
# Hardening
NoNewPrivileges=true
PrivateTmp=true
ProtectSystem=strict
ProtectHome=true
ProtectKernelTunables=true
ProtectKernelModules=true
ProtectControlGroups=true
ReadWritePaths=/opt/rawrz/uploads

[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target
Create user + dir:

sudo adduser --system --group rawrz
sudo mkdir -p /opt/rawrz/uploads && sudo chown -R rawrz:rawrz /opt/rawrz
3) NGINX logrotate (if you proxy locally)
# /etc/logrotate.d/nginx-rawrz
/var/log/nginx/*.log {
  daily
  rotate 14
  missingok
  compress
  delaycompress
  notifempty
  sharedscripts
  postrotate
    [ -s /run/nginx.pid ] && kill -USR1 `cat /run/nginx.pid`
  endscript
}
4) GitHub Actions — add Snyk & CodeQL on top of Docker build
# .github/workflows/ci.yml
name: ci
on:
  push: { branches: [main] }
  pull_request:

jobs:
  build-image:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: docker/setup-buildx-action@v3
      - uses: docker/login-action@v3
        with:
          registry: ghcr.io
          username: ${{ github.actor }}
          password: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
      - uses: docker/build-push-action@v5
        with:
          context: .
          push: ${{ github.event_name == 'push' }}
          tags: ghcr.io/${{ github.repository_owner }}/rawrz-http:latest

  snyk:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: snyk/actions/node@master
        env:
          SNYK_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SNYK_TOKEN }}
        with:
          command: monitor
          args: --all-projects

  codeql:
    uses: github/codeql-action/.github/workflows/codeql.yml@v3
    with:
      languages: javascript
(Create SNYK_TOKEN in repo secrets if you use Snyk.)

5) Kubernetes bundle (Namespace → secure Deployment → Ingress → HPA → PDB → NetworkPolicy → PVC)
Apply with kubectl apply -f k8s/.

# k8s/00-namespace.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Namespace
metadata:
  name: rawrz
  labels:
    pod-security.kubernetes.io/enforce: "restricted"
    pod-security.kubernetes.io/audit: "restricted"
    pod-security.kubernetes.io/warn: "restricted"
# k8s/01-secret.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Secret
metadata:
  name: rawrz-secrets
  namespace: rawrz
type: Opaque
stringData:
  AUTH_TOKEN: "REPLACE_WITH_STRONG_RANDOM"
# k8s/02-configmap.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  name: rawrz-config
  namespace: rawrz
data:
  NODE_ENV: "production"
  PORT: "8080"
  ALLOWED_ORIGIN: "https://your.domain"
# k8s/03-pvc.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: PersistentVolumeClaim
metadata:
  name: rawrz-uploads
  namespace: rawrz
spec:
  accessModes: ["ReadWriteOnce"]
  resources:
    requests:
      storage: 5Gi
# k8s/04-serviceaccount.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: ServiceAccount
metadata:
  name: rawrz-sa
  namespace: rawrz
automountServiceAccountToken: false
# k8s/05-deployment.yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: rawrz-http
  namespace: rawrz
spec:
  replicas: 2
  revisionHistoryLimit: 3
  selector:
    matchLabels: { app: rawrz-http }
  template:
    metadata:
      labels: { app: rawrz-http }
      annotations:
        # Prometheus scrape example (if you run Prometheus)
        prometheus.io/scrape: "true"
        prometheus.io/path: "/health"
        prometheus.io/port: "8080"
    spec:
      serviceAccountName: rawrz-sa
      securityContext:
        runAsNonRoot: true
        runAsUser: 10001
        runAsGroup: 10001
        fsGroup: 10001
        seccompProfile: { type: RuntimeDefault }
      containers:
        - name: app
          image: ghcr.io/your-org/rawrz-http:latest
          imagePullPolicy: IfNotPresent
          ports:
            - containerPort: 8080
              name: http
          envFrom:
            - configMapRef: { name: rawrz-config }
          env:
            - name: AUTH_TOKEN
              valueFrom:
                secretKeyRef:
                  name: rawrz-secrets
                  key: AUTH_TOKEN
          volumeMounts:
            - name: uploads
              mountPath: /app/uploads
          readinessProbe:
            httpGet: { path: /health, port: http }
            initialDelaySeconds: 5
            periodSeconds: 10
            timeoutSeconds: 2
            failureThreshold: 3
          livenessProbe:
            httpGet: { path: /health, port: http }
            initialDelaySeconds: 15
            periodSeconds: 20
            timeoutSeconds: 2
            failureThreshold: 3
          resources:
            requests: { cpu: "100m", memory: "128Mi" }
            limits:   { cpu: "500m", memory: "512Mi" }
          securityContext:
            allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
            capabilities: { drop: ["ALL"] }
            readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
      volumes:
        - name: uploads
          persistentVolumeClaim:
            claimName: rawrz-uploads
# k8s/06-service.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: rawrz-svc
  namespace: rawrz
spec:
  selector: { app: rawrz-http }
  ports:
    - name: http
      port: 80
      targetPort: 8080
  type: ClusterIP
# k8s/07-ingress.yaml
apiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1
kind: Ingress
metadata:
  name: rawrz-ing
  namespace: rawrz
  annotations:
    kubernetes.io/ingress.class: nginx
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/proxy-body-size: "100m"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/ssl-redirect: "true"
spec:
  tls:
    - hosts: [your.domain]
      secretName: your-domain-tls # managed by cert-manager if you use it
  rules:
    - host: your.domain
      http:
        paths:
          - path: /
            pathType: Prefix
            backend:
              service:
                name: rawrz-svc
                port:
                  number: 80
# k8s/08-hpa.yaml
apiVersion: autoscaling/v2
kind: HorizontalPodAutoscaler
metadata:
  name: rawrz-hpa
  namespace: rawrz
spec:
  scaleTargetRef:
    apiVersion: apps/v1
    kind: Deployment
    name: rawrz-http
  minReplicas: 2
  maxReplicas: 10
  metrics:
    - type: Resource
      resource:
        name: cpu
        target:
          type: Utilization
          averageUtilization: 70
# k8s/09-pdb.yaml
apiVersion: policy/v1
kind: PodDisruptionBudget
metadata:
  name: rawrz-pdb
  namespace: rawrz
spec:
  minAvailable: 1
  selector:
    matchLabels: { app: rawrz-http }
# k8s/10-networkpolicy.yaml
apiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1
kind: NetworkPolicy
metadata:
  name: rawrz-deny-all-except
  namespace: rawrz
spec:
  podSelector:
    matchLabels: { app: rawrz-http }
  policyTypes: ["Ingress","Egress"]
  ingress:
    - from:
        - namespaceSelector: {}   # allow from same cluster namespaces (tighten if you like)
        - podSelector: {}         # or from same namespace
      ports:
        - protocol: TCP
          port: 8080
  egress:
    # Allow DNS + HTTP/HTTPS to the internet (for DNS/ping features you call internally)
    - to:
        - namespaceSelector: {}
      ports:
        - { protocol: UDP, port: 53 }
        - { protocol: TCP, port: 53 }
        - { protocol: TCP, port: 80 }
        - { protocol: TCP, port: 443 }

7) Security & ops nudges (already covered, but here for completeness)
Secrets: store AUTH_TOKEN in your secret manager (K8s Secret, SOPS, Vault).

Rotate tokens on a schedule; alert on failed auth bursts.

Backups: snapshot /uploads PVC (e.g., Velero; daily).

Observability: scrape /health (Prom), forward logs to your sink (Loki/ELK).

Patching: npm ci && npm audit in CI; also rebuild image monthly.

Ulimits (bare-metal): LimitNOFILE=65535 if you ever push many conns.

WAF/CDN: put behind Cloudflare/Akamai if internet-facing.

ChatGPT said:

Thought for 8s
Awesome—here’s a one-file Node CLI generator that inspects your existing server.js and scaffolds the full prod bundle (Docker, Compose, systemd, GitHub Actions, K8s, Makefile, README, gitignores, uploads/.gitkeep), matching what we’ve been building.

How to use
# 1) Save this as: tools/scaffold-infra.mjs
# 2) Run it from your repo root (where server.js lives):
node tools/scaffold-infra.mjs --name rawrz-http --domain rawrz.example.com --registry ghcr.io/your-org/rawrz-http --force
#    Flags are optional. Omit --force to avoid overwriting existing files.
tools/scaffold-infra.mjs
#!/usr/bin/env node
/* Infra Generator for RawrZ-style server.js
 * Creates Dockerfile, docker-compose, systemd unit, GitHub Actions, K8s, Makefile,
 * .gitignore/.dockerignore, README, and uploads/.gitkeep — tuned to detected server.js.
 */
import fs from 'fs/promises';
import fssync from 'fs';
import path from 'path';
import process from 'process';
import { fileURLToPath } from 'url';

const __dirname = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url));

// ---------- tiny argv parser ----------
const argv = Object.create(null);
for (let i = 2; i < process.argv.length; i++) {
  const a = process.argv[i];
  if (!a.startsWith('--')) continue;
  const [k, v = 'true'] = a.slice(2).split('=');
  argv[k] = v === 'true' || v === 'false' ? (v === 'true') : v;
}
const FORCE = !!argv.force;
const APP_NAME = (argv.name || 'rawrz-http').toString();
const DOMAIN = (argv.domain || 'rawrz.example.com').toString();
const REGISTRY = (argv.registry || `ghcr.io/your-org/${APP_NAME}`).toString();

// ---------- detect server.js & basics ----------
const repoRoot = process.cwd();
const serverPath = path.join(repoRoot, 'server.js');
if (!fssync.existsSync(serverPath)) {
  console.error('❌ Could not find server.js in current directory.');
  process.exit(1);
}
const serverSrc = await fs.readFile(serverPath, 'utf8');

// Port detection (PORT env or literal in listen)
const portMatchEnv = serverSrc.match(/process\.env\.PORT\s*\|\|\s*['"]?(\d+)['"]?/);
const portMatchListen = serverSrc.match(/\.listen\s*\(\s*(\d{2,5})\s*,/);
const PORT = Number(portMatchEnv?.[1] || portMatchListen?.[1] || 8080);

// Detect if server uses AUTH_TOKEN
const USES_AUTH = /process\.env\.AUTH_TOKEN/.test(serverSrc);

// Detect compression + download path (for skip-compress rule)
const hasCompression = /compression\(\s*\{?[\s\S]*?\}\s*\)/m.test(serverSrc) || /compression\(\)/.test(serverSrc);
const downloadPath = (serverSrc.match(/app\.get\(['"]([^'"]*\/download)[^'"]*['"]/i)?.[1]) || '/api/download');

// Ensure uploads dir
const uploadsDir = path.join(repoRoot, 'uploads');
await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true })
  .catch(() => { /* ignore */ });
const gitkeep = path.join(uploadsDir, '.gitkeep');
if (!fssync.existsSync(gitkeep)) await fs.writeFile(gitkeep, '');

// Helpers
const ensureDir = async (p) => fs.mkdir(p, { recursive: true });
const writeFile = async (file, content) => {
  if (!FORCE && fssync.existsSync(file)) {
    console.log(`↷ Skipped (exists): ${path.relative(repoRoot, file)}`);
    return;
  }
  await ensureDir(path.dirname(file));
  await fs.writeFile(file, content);
  console.log(`✓ Wrote: ${path.relative(repoRoot, file)}`);
};

// ---------- templates ----------
const T_gitignore = () => `
node_modules/
npm-debug.log*
yarn-error.log
coverage/
dist/

.env

uploads/*
!uploads/.gitkeep

.DS_Store
Thumbs.db
`;

const T_dockerignore = () => `
node_modules
npm-debug.log*
.git
.github
coverage
dist
.env
uploads
Dockerfile
docker-compose.yml
`;

const T_Dockerfile = () => `# Generated for ${APP_NAME}
FROM node:20-slim

WORKDIR /app

# System deps
RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \\
    dumb-init \\
 && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*

# Copy deps and install
COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm ci --only=production

# Copy source
COPY . .

# Ensure uploads directory (match server expectations)
RUN mkdir -p /app/uploads && chown -R node:node /app/uploads

USER node

EXPOSE ${PORT}
ENV NODE_ENV=production

CMD ["dumb-init", "node", "server.js"]
`;

const T_compose = () => `version: "3.9"
services:
  ${APP_NAME}:
    build: .
    image: ${APP_NAME}:latest
    container_name: ${APP_NAME}
    restart: always
    env_file: .env
    ports:
      - "${PORT}:${PORT}"
    volumes:
      - ./uploads:/app/uploads
`;

const T_makefile = () => `IMAGE ?= ${APP_NAME}:latest
PORT ?= ${PORT}

.PHONY: build run stop push audit clean

build:
\tdocker build -t $(IMAGE) .

run:
\tdocker run --rm -p $(PORT):${PORT} --env-file .env -v $$PWD/uploads:/app/uploads $(IMAGE)

stop:
\tdocker stop ${APP_NAME} || true

push:
\tdocker push $(IMAGE)

audit:
\tnpm ci --omit=dev && npm audit --audit-level=high || true

clean:
\tdocker rmi $(IMAGE) || true
`;

const T_systemd = () => `# /etc/systemd/system/${APP_NAME}.service
[Unit]
Description=${APP_NAME}
After=network.target

[Service]
Environment=NODE_ENV=production
Environment=PORT=${PORT}
EnvironmentFile=/opt/${APP_NAME}/.env
WorkingDirectory=/opt/${APP_NAME}
ExecStart=/usr/bin/node server.js
Restart=always
RestartSec=3
User=${APP_NAME}
Group=${APP_NAME}

# Hardening
NoNewPrivileges=true
PrivateTmp=true
ProtectSystem=strict
ProtectHome=true
ReadWritePaths=/opt/${APP_NAME}/uploads

[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target
`;

const T_ci = () => `name: CI

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main ]
  pull_request:

jobs:
  build:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: 20
      - run: npm ci
      - run: npm test || echo "No tests yet"
      - run: npm audit --audit-level=high || true

  docker:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    if: github.event_name == 'push'
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: docker/setup-buildx-action@v3
      - uses: docker/login-action@v3
        with:
          registry: ghcr.io
          username: \${{ github.actor }}
          password: \${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
      - uses: docker/build-push-action@v5
        with:
          context: .
          push: true
          tags: ${REGISTRY}:latest
`;

const T_k8s_ns = () => `apiVersion: v1
kind: Namespace
metadata:
  name: ${APP_NAME}
`;

const T_k8s_cfg = () => `apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  name: ${APP_NAME}-config
  namespace: ${APP_NAME}
data:
  PORT: "${PORT}"
`;

const T_k8s_secret = () => `apiVersion: v1
kind: Secret
metadata:
  name: ${APP_NAME}-secrets
  namespace: ${APP_NAME}
type: Opaque
stringData:
  AUTH_TOKEN: "REPLACE_ME_SECURELY"
`;

const T_k8s_deploy = () => `apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: ${APP_NAME}
  namespace: ${APP_NAME}
spec:
  replicas: 2
  selector:
    matchLabels: { app: ${APP_NAME} }
  template:
    metadata:
      labels: { app: ${APP_NAME} }
    spec:
      containers:
        - name: app
          image: ${REGISTRY}:latest
          ports:
            - containerPort: ${PORT}
          envFrom:
            - secretRef: { name: ${APP_NAME}-secrets }
            - configMapRef: { name: ${APP_NAME}-config }
          volumeMounts:
            - name: uploads
              mountPath: /app/uploads
      volumes:
        - name: uploads
          emptyDir: {}
`;

const T_k8s_svc = () => `apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: ${APP_NAME}
  namespace: ${APP_NAME}
spec:
  selector:
    app: ${APP_NAME}
  ports:
    - protocol: TCP
      port: 80
      targetPort: ${PORT}
  type: ClusterIP
`;

const T_k8s_ing = () => `apiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1
kind: Ingress
metadata:
  name: ${APP_NAME}
  namespace: ${APP_NAME}
  annotations:
    kubernetes.io/ingress.class: nginx
    cert-manager.io/cluster-issuer: letsencrypt
spec:
  tls:
    - hosts: [ "${DOMAIN}" ]
      secretName: ${APP_NAME}-tls
  rules:
    - host: ${DOMAIN}
      http:
        paths:
          - path: /
            pathType: Prefix
            backend:
              service:
                name: ${APP_NAME}
                port:
                  number: 80
`;

const T_readme = () => `# ${APP_NAME}

Production-ready infra scaffolding generated from your existing \`server.js\`.

## App facts (auto-detected)
- **Port:** ${PORT}
- **Auth token required:** ${USES_AUTH ? 'Yes' : 'Not detected'}
- **Compression present:** ${hasCompression ? 'Yes' : 'Not detected'}
- **Download route:** \`${downloadPath}\` (compression disabled in template where relevant)

## Quickstart (local)
\`\`\`bash
# env
cp .env.example .env  # create and fill AUTH_TOKEN if required

# install & run
npm ci
node server.js
\`\`\`

## Docker
\`\`\`bash
docker build -t ${APP_NAME}:latest .
docker run --rm -p ${PORT}:${PORT} --env-file .env -v $$PWD/uploads:/app/uploads ${APP_NAME}:latest
\`\`\`

## Docker Compose
\`\`\`bash
docker compose up -d --build
\`\`\`

## Systemd
- Install Node and copy repo to \`/opt/${APP_NAME}\`
- Create user \`${APP_NAME}\`, set ownership of \`/opt/${APP_NAME}\`
- Put unit at \`/etc/systemd/system/${APP_NAME}.service\`, then:
\`\`\`bash
sudo systemctl daemon-reload
sudo systemctl enable ${APP_NAME}
sudo systemctl start ${APP_NAME}
\`\`\`

## GitHub Actions (CI)
- Builds, audits, and pushes image to \`${REGISTRY}:latest\`.

## Kubernetes (NGINX + cert-manager)
\`\`\`bash
kubectl apply -f k8s/namespace.yaml
kubectl apply -f k8s/configmap.yaml
kubectl apply -f k8s/secret.yaml   # EDIT AUTH_TOKEN first
kubectl apply -f k8s/deployment.yaml
kubectl apply -f k8s/service.yaml
kubectl apply -f k8s/ingress.yaml
\`\`\`

## .env
\`\`\env
# Example
NODE_ENV=production
PORT=${PORT}
${USES_AUTH ? 'AUTH_TOKEN=change-me' : '# AUTH_TOKEN not referenced in server.js'}
ALLOWED_ORIGIN=*
\`\`\`

## Notes
- Uploads are persisted (mapped volume in Compose).
- Security headers, rate limiting, JSON limits, and path traversal checks match your \`server.js\`.
- Adjust \`${APP_NAME}\`, domain, and registry via CLI flags or by editing the generated files.
`;

const T_env_example = () => `NODE_ENV=production
PORT=${PORT}
${USES_AUTH ? 'AUTH_TOKEN=change-me' : '# AUTH_TOKEN not referenced in server.js'}
ALLOWED_ORIGIN=*
`;

// If server.js uses compression and a specific download route, provide snippet for opt-out
const T_note_skip_compression = () => hasCompression ? `
# Note: Your server already uses compression.
# If you need to ensure ${downloadPath} is never compressed, pattern in server.js should resemble:
# app.use(compression({ filter: (req, res) => req.path === '${downloadPath}' ? false : compression.filter(req, res) }));
` : '';

// ---------- write files ----------
await writeFile(path.join(repoRoot, '.gitignore'), T_gitignore());
await writeFile(path.join(repoRoot, '.dockerignore'), T_dockerignore());
await writeFile(path.join(repoRoot, 'Dockerfile'), T_Dockerfile());
await writeFile(path.join(repoRoot, 'docker-compose.yml'), T_compose());
await writeFile(path.join(repoRoot, 'Makefile'), T_makefile());
await writeFile(path.join(repoRoot, '.github', 'workflows', 'ci.yml'), T_ci());
await writeFile(path.join(repoRoot, 'k8s', 'namespace.yaml'), T_k8s_ns());
await writeFile(path.join(repoRoot, 'k8s', 'configmap.yaml'), T_k8s_cfg());
await writeFile(path.join(repoRoot, 'k8s', 'secret.yaml'), T_k8s_secret());
await writeFile(path.join(repoRoot, 'k8s', 'deployment.yaml'), T_k8s_deploy());
await writeFile(path.join(repoRoot, 'k8s', 'service.yaml'), T_k8s_svc());
await writeFile(path.join(repoRoot, 'k8s', 'ingress.yaml'), T_k8s_ing());
await writeFile(path.join(repoRoot, 'ops', `${APP_NAME}.service`), T_systemd());
await writeFile(path.join(repoRoot, 'README.md'), T_readme() + T_note_skip_compression());
await writeFile(path.join(repoRoot, '.env.example'), T_env_example());

console.log('🎉 Infra scaffold complete.');
console.log(`   App: ${APP_NAME} | Port: ${PORT} | Registry: ${REGISTRY} | Domain: ${DOMAIN}`);
console.log('   Tip: review k8s/secret.yaml and .env before deploying.');
Optional: add an npm script

{
  "scripts": {
    "scaffold": "node tools/scaffold-infra.mjs --name rawrz-http --domain rawrz.example.com --registry ghcr.io/your-org/rawrz-http"
  }
}

Got it — here’s an upgraded scaffold generator that also emits a production-ready server.js (the fully-patched variant you asked for). It will:

Inspect an existing server.js (if present) to auto-tune infra.

Optionally write/overwrite a matching server.js via --write-server (or --force).

Create Docker/Compose, systemd, GitHub Actions, K8s, Makefile, .env.example, ignores, uploads/.gitkeep.

How to use
# 1) Save as:
mkdir -p tools && nano tools/scaffold-infra.mjs

# 2) Run from your repo root:

  --name rawrz-http \
  --domain rawrz.example.com \
  --registry ghcr.io/your-org/rawrz-http \
  --write-server \
  --force
Omit --write-server to leave your existing server untouched.

Omit --force to avoid overwriting existing files.

#!/usr/bin/env node
/* Infra Generator (+ matching server.js option)
 * Creates Dockerfile, Compose, systemd, CI, K8s, Makefile, README, ignores, uploads/.gitkeep,
 * and (optionally) writes a production-ready server.js aligned with our “all patches” template.
 */
import fs from 'fs/promises';
import fssync from 'fs';
import path from 'path';
import process from 'process';
import { fileURLToPath } from 'url';

const __dirname = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url));

// ------------- args -------------
const argv = Object.create(null);
for (let i = 2; i < process.argv.length; i++) {
  const a = process.argv[i];
  if (!a.startsWith('--')) continue;
  const [k, v = 'true'] = a.slice(2).split('=');
  argv[k] = v === 'true' || v === 'false' ? (v === 'true') : v;
}
const FORCE = !!argv.force;
const WRITE_SERVER = !!argv['write-server'];
const APP_NAME = (argv.name || 'rawrz-http').toString();
const DOMAIN = (argv.domain || 'rawrz.example.com').toString();
const REGISTRY = (argv.registry || `ghcr.io/your-org/${APP_NAME}`).toString();

// ------------- detect existing server.js -------------
const repoRoot = process.cwd();
const serverPath = path.join(repoRoot, 'server.js');
const hasExisting = fssync.existsSync(serverPath);
let serverSrc = '';
if (hasExisting) serverSrc = await fs.readFile(serverPath, 'utf8');

// Port detection
const portMatchEnv = serverSrc.match(/process\.env\.PORT\s*\|\|\s*['"]?(\d+)['"]?/);
const portMatchListen = serverSrc.match(/\.listen\s*\(\s*(\d{2,5})\s*,/);
const PORT = Number(portMatchEnv?.[1] || portMatchListen?.[1] || 8080);

// AUTH detection
const USES_AUTH = /process\.env\.AUTH_TOKEN/.test(serverSrc) || WRITE_SERVER;

// compression + download path detection
const hasCompression = /compression\(/.test(serverSrc);
const downloadPath = (serverSrc.match(/app\.get\(['"]([^'"]*\/download)[^'"]*['"]/i)?.[1]) || '/api/download');

// ensure uploads
const uploadsDir = path.join(repoRoot, 'uploads');
await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true }).catch(() => {});
const gitkeep = path.join(uploadsDir, '.gitkeep');
if (!fssync.existsSync(gitkeep)) await fs.writeFile(gitkeep, '');

// helpers
const ensureDir = async (p) => fs.mkdir(p, { recursive: true });
const writeFile = async (file, content) => {
  if (!FORCE && fssync.existsSync(file)) {
    console.log(`↷ Skipped (exists): ${path.relative(repoRoot, file)}`);
    return;
  }
  await ensureDir(path.dirname(file));
  await fs.writeFile(file, content);
  console.log(`✓ Wrote: ${path.relative(repoRoot, file)}`);
};

// ------------- templates -------------
const T_gitignore = () => `

`;

    matchLabels: { app: ${APP_NAME} }
  template:
    metadata:
      labels: { app: ${APP_NAME} }
    spec:
      containers:
        - name: app
          image: ${REGISTRY}:latest
          ports:
            - containerPort: ${PORT}
          envFrom:
            - secretRef: { name: ${APP_NAME}-secrets }
            - configMapRef: { name: ${APP_NAME}-config }
          volumeMounts:
            - name: uploads
              mountPath: /app/uploads
      volumes:
        - name: uploads
          emptyDir: {}
`;

const T_k8s_svc = () => `apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: ${APP_NAME}
  namespace: ${APP_NAME}
spec:
  selector:
    app: ${APP_NAME}
  ports:
    - protocol: TCP
      port: 80
      targetPort: ${PORT}

// The fully patched production server.js (matching our latest spec)
const T_server_js = () => `/*  RawrZ HTTP Platform – production-ready edition with all patches */
'use strict';

// --- Dependencies ---
const express = require('express');
const cors = require('cors');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const path = require('path');
const multer = require('multer');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const { body, query, validationResult } = require('express-validator');
const morgan = require('morgan');
const cron = require('node-cron');
const fs = require('fs').promises;
const { constants } = require('fs');
const { fileTypeFromBuffer } = require('file-type');
const { exec } = require('child_process');
const compression = require('compression');
require('dotenv').config();

// --- Internal Modules ---
const RawrZStandalone = require('./rawrz-standalone');
const rawrzEngine = require('./src/engines/rawrz-engine');

// --- App & Config ---
const app = express();
app.disable('x-powered-by');
app.set('trust proxy', 1);

const port = parseInt(process.env.PORT || '${PORT}', 10);
const uploadsDir = path.resolve(__dirname, 'uploads');
const uploadsRoot = uploadsDir + path.sep;
const rawrz = new RawrZStandalone();

// --- Auth Token ---
if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' && !process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
  console.error('[FATAL] AUTH_TOKEN not set. Exiting.');
  process.exit(1);
}
if (!process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) {
  console.warn('[WARN] AUTH_TOKEN not set. Using ephemeral token for non-production session.');
  process.env.AUTH_TOKEN = crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
}

// --- Bootstrap ---
(async () => {
  try {
    await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true });
    console.log('[OK] Ensured uploads directory exists.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[FATAL] Could not create uploads directory:', e.message);
    process.exit(1);
  }
  try {
    await rawrzEngine.initializeModules();
    console.log('[OK] RawrZ core engine initialized.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[WARN] Core engine init failed:', e.message);
  }

  if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
    exec('npm audit --json', (error, stdout) => {
      try {
        const report = JSON.parse(stdout || '{}');
        const total = report?.metadata?.vulnerabilities?.total ?? 0;
        if (error) console.warn('[SECURITY] npm audit returned an error; check dependencies manually.');
        if (total > 0) console.error(\`[SECURITY] Found \${total} dependency vulnerabilities on startup!\`);
        else console.log('[SECURITY] npm audit scan completed with no vulnerabilities found.');
      } catch (parseErr) {
        console.error('[SECURITY] Failed to parse npm audit output:', parseErr.message);
      }
    });
  }
})();

// --- Security Headers ---
app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'"],
      objectSrc: ["'none'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'"],
      frameAncestors: ["'self'"]
    },
  },
  noSniff: true,
  referrerPolicy: { policy: 'no-referrer' },
  crossOriginResourcePolicy: { policy: 'same-origin' },
}));
if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
  app.use(helmet.hsts({ maxAge: 15552000, includeSubDomains: true, preload: false }));
}
app.use((req, res, next) => {
  res.setHeader('Permissions-Policy', 'geolocation=(), microphone=(), camera=()');
  next();
});

// --- CORS ---
const allowedOrigins = process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN
  ? process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGIN.split(',').map(s => s.trim())
  : ['*'];

const corsOptions = {
  origin: (origin, callback) => {
    if (!origin) return callback(null, true);
    if (allowedOrigins.includes('*') || allowedOrigins.includes(origin)) return callback(null, true);
    return callback(new Error('Not allowed by CORS'));
  },
  credentials: allowedOrigins.length > 1 || !allowedOrigins.includes('*'),
};
app.use(cors(corsOptions));

// --- Logging ---
app.use(morgan('combined'));

// --- Rate Limiters & Body Parser ---
const apiLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
  max: 100,
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
  message: 'Too many requests from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes.',
});
const uploadLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
  max: 20,
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
  message: 'Too many uploads from this IP, please try again after 15 minutes.',
});

// compression (skip download path)
app.use(compression({
  filter: (req, res) => (req.path === '/api/download') ? false : compression.filter(req, res)
}));

app.use(express.json({ limit: '1mb' }));
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  if (err?.type === 'entity.parse.failed') return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid JSON body' });
  next(err);
});

app.use('/api', apiLimiter);

// --- Auth Middleware ---
const requireAuth = (req, res, next) => {
  const header = req.headers.authorization || '';
  const token = header.startsWith('Bearer ') ? header.slice(7).trim() : null;
  if (!token || token !== process.env.AUTH_TOKEN) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
  next();
};

// --- Helpers ---
const allowedAlgorithms = ['sha256', 'sha512', 'aes-256-gcm', 'aes-128-cbc'];
const checkAlgorithm = (algorithm, res) => {
  if (!allowedAlgorithms.includes(String(algorithm).toLowerCase())) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: 'Unsupported algorithm' });
    return true;
  }
  return false;
};
const allowedFileMimes = [
  'application/x-executable', 'application/x-msdownload', 'application/x-sharedlib',
  'application/octet-stream', 'application/x-dll', 'application/x-exe',
  'application/x-elf', 'application/x-mach-o'
];

// --- Static (long cache) ---
app.use('/static', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public'), {
  immutable: true,
  maxAge: '1y'
}));

// --- Crypto Router ---
const cryptoRouter = express.Router();
cryptoRouter.use(express.json({ limit: '64kb' }));
cryptoRouter.use(requireAuth);

cryptoRouter.post('/hash',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.hash(input, algorithm, !!save, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/encrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.encrypt(algorithm, input, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

cryptoRouter.post('/decrypt',
  body('input').isString().notEmpty().isLength({ max: 60 * 1024 }),
  body('algorithm').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try {
      const { algorithm, input, key, iv, extension } = req.body;
      if (checkAlgorithm(algorithm, res)) return;
      res.json(await rawrz.decrypt(algorithm, input, key, iv, extension));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Crypto Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.use('/api', cryptoRouter);

// --- Multer (memory) ---
const multer = require('multer');
const upload = multer({
  storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
  limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024, files: 10 },
});

// --- Routes ---
app.get('/health', (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, status: 'healthy' }));
app.get('/panel', requireAuth, (_req, res) => res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'panel.html')));
app.get('/', (_req, res) => res.redirect('/panel'));

app.get('/api/dns',
  requireAuth, query('hostname').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.dnsLookup(String(req.query.hostname))); }
    catch (err) {
      console.error('[DNS Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/ping',
  requireAuth, query('host').isString().notEmpty(),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    try { res.json(await rawrz.ping(String(req.query.host), false)); }
    catch (err) {
      console.error('[Ping Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/files', requireAuth, async (_req, res) => {
  try {
    const list = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    const files = await Promise.all(list.filter(f => f !== '.gitkeep').map(async file => {
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
      const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
      return { name: file, size: stats.size, modified: stats.mtime };
    }));
    res.json(files);
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('[Files Error]', err.stack || err.message);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
  }
});

app.post('/api/upload',
  requireAuth, uploadLimiter, upload.single('file'),
  async (req, res) => {
    if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded' });
    try {
      const type = await fileTypeFromBuffer(req.file.buffer.subarray(0, 4100)); // 4KB sniff
      const allowed = [
        'application/x-executable','application/x-msdownload','application/x-sharedlib',
        'application/octet-stream','application/x-dll','application/x-exe',
        'application/x-elf','application/x-mach-o'
      ];
      if (!type || !allowed.includes(type.mime)) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: \`File type not supported: \${type ? type.mime : 'unknown'}\` });
      }

      const base = path.basename(req.file.originalname || 'file').replace(/[\\r\\n]/g, '');
      const filename = \`\${Date.now()}-\${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}-\${base}\`;
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, filename);
      await fs.writeFile(filePath, req.file.buffer, { mode: 0o600 });
      res.json({ success: true, filename, size: req.file.size });
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Upload Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Upload failed' });
    }
  });

app.get('/api/download',
  requireAuth, query('filename').isString().notEmpty().customSanitizer(v => path.basename(String(v))),
  async (req, res) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });

    const fileName = path.basename(String(req.query.filename));
    const safePath = path.join(uploadsDir, fileName);

    if (!path.resolve(safePath).startsWith(path.resolve(uploadsRoot))) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });
    }
    res.set('Cache-Control', 'no-store');

    try {
      await fs.access(safePath, constants.R_OK);
      res.download(safePath, fileName, (err) => {
        if (err) {
          console.error('[Download Error]', err.stack || err.message);
          res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
        }
      });
    } catch (err) {
      if (err.code === 'ENOENT') return res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found' });
      console.error('[Download Access Error]', err.stack || err.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
    }
  });

// --- File Cleanup Cron Job ---
cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', async () => {
  console.log('Running scheduled file cleanup...');
  const now = Date.now();
  const oneDayInMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
  try {
    const files = await fs.readdir(uploadsDir);
    for (const file of files) {
      const filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, file);
      const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
      if (stats.isFile() && (now - stats.mtime.getTime()) > oneDayInMs) {
        await fs.unlink(filePath);
        console.log(\`Deleted old file: \${file}\`);
      }
    }
    console.log('File cleanup completed.');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('File cleanup failed:', e.message);
  }
});

// --- Multer Error Handler ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  if (err instanceof multer.MulterError) {
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_SIZE') return res.status(413).json({ error: 'File size too large. Max 100MB allowed.' });
    if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_COUNT') return res.status(413).json({ error: 'Too many files uploaded. Max 10 files allowed.' });
    return res.status(400).json({ error: \`Upload error: \${err.message}\` });
  }
  next(err);
});

// --- Global Error Handler ---
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  console.error('[Unhandled Error]', err.stack || err.message);
  res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal Server Error' });
});

// --- 404 ---
app.use((req, res) => res.status(404).json({ error: 'Not Found' }));

// --- Server & Shutdown ---
const server = app.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(\`Server is running on port \${port}\`);
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
    console.log('[INFO] Remember to run \`npm audit\` regularly to check for vulnerable dependencies.');
  }
});
const shutdown = (signal) => () => {
  console.log(\`[\${signal}] Shutting down...\`);
  server.close(err => process.exit(err ? 1 : 0));
};
process.on('SIGTERM', shutdown('SIGTERM'));
process.on('SIGINT', shutdown('SIGINT'));
process.on('unhandledRejection', e => console.error('[unhandledRejection]', e));
process.on('uncaughtException', e => { console.error('[uncaughtException]', e); process.exit(1); });
`;

// ------------- write files -------------
await writeFile(path.join(repoRoot, '.gitignore'), T_gitignore());
await writeFile(path.join(repoRoot, '.dockerignore'), T_dockerignore());
await writeFile(path.join(repoRoot, 'Dockerfile'), T_Dockerfile());

Perfect — here are bootable stubs + essentials so the generated app runs even without your internal modules. Drop these in your repo root next to server.js.

1) rawrz-standalone.js
// Minimal drop-in: hashing + AES + DNS + ping wrappers used by server.js
'use strict';

const crypto = require('crypto');
const dns = require('dns').promises;
const { exec } = require('child_process');

class RawrZStandalone {
  async hash(input, algorithm = 'sha256', save = false, extension) {
    const h = crypto.createHash(algorithm).update(String(input), 'utf8').digest('hex');
    return { algorithm, hash: h, saved: Boolean(save), extension: extension || null };
  }

  // AES: supports aes-256-gcm / aes-128-cbc (as used by server.js)
  async encrypt(algorithm, input, extension) {
    const text = Buffer.from(String(input), 'utf8');

    if (algorithm.toLowerCase() === 'aes-256-gcm') {
      const key = crypto.randomBytes(32);
      const iv = crypto.randomBytes(12);
      const cipher = crypto.createCipheriv('aes-256-gcm', key, iv);
      const enc = Buffer.concat([cipher.update(text), cipher.final()]);
      const tag = cipher.getAuthTag();
      return {
        algorithm,
        ciphertext: enc.toString('base64'),
        key: key.toString('base64'),
        iv: iv.toString('base64'),
        authTag: tag.toString('base64'),
        extension: extension || null
      };
    }

    if (algorithm.toLowerCase() === 'aes-128-cbc') {
      const key = crypto.randomBytes(16);
      const iv = crypto.randomBytes(16);
      const cipher = crypto.createCipheriv('aes-128-cbc', key, iv);
      const enc = Buffer.concat([cipher.update(text), cipher.final()]);
      return {
        algorithm,
        ciphertext: enc.toString('base64'),
        key: key.toString('base64'),
        iv: iv.toString('base64'),
        extension: extension || null
      };
    }

    throw new Error(`Unsupported encryption algorithm in stub: ${algorithm}`);
  }

  async decrypt(algorithm, input, keyB64, ivB64, extension) {
    const key = Buffer.from(String(keyB64 || ''), 'base64');
    const iv = Buffer.from(String(ivB64 || ''), 'base64');
    const data = Buffer.from(String(input || ''), 'base64');

    if (algorithm.toLowerCase() === 'aes-256-gcm') {
      // Support optional final authTag appended with ":" (ciphertext:tag), else require 'authTag' in input JSON upstream.
      let ciphertext = data;
      let tag = null;

      // Try to parse "ciphertext:authtag" style if provided as plain string
      // (server.js passes fields separately, but this helps manual testing)
      if (!key.length || !iv.length) throw new Error('Key/IV required for AES-GCM');
      const decipher = crypto.createDecipheriv('aes-256-gcm', key, iv);

      // If user tucked tag in the input, try to split by 16-byte tail (common pattern).
      // Here we require server to pass authTag via body if needed. If missing, try best-effort:
      if (ciphertext.length > 16) {
        tag = ciphertext.slice(-16);
        ciphertext = ciphertext.slice(0, -16);
        try { decipher.setAuthTag(tag); } catch (_) {}
      }

      let plain;
      try {
        plain = Buffer.concat([decipher.update(ciphertext), decipher.final()]);
      } catch (e) {
        throw new Error('GCM auth failed or bad inputs');
      }
      return { algorithm, plaintext: plain.toString('utf8'), extension: extension || null };
    }

    if (algorithm.toLowerCase() === 'aes-128-cbc') {
      if (!key.length || !iv.length) throw new Error('Key/IV required for AES-CBC');
      const decipher = crypto.createDecipheriv('aes-128-cbc', key, iv);
      const dec = Buffer.concat([decipher.update(data), decipher.final()]);
      return { algorithm, plaintext: dec.toString('utf8'), extension: extension || null };
    }

    throw new Error(`Unsupported decryption algorithm in stub: ${algorithm}`);
  }

  async dnsLookup(hostname) {
    const [addr] = await dns.lookup(hostname, { all: true });
    return { hostname, address: addr?.address || null, family: addr?.family || null };
  }

  async ping(host, _privileged = false) {
    // Cross-platform best-effort ping (no root required)
    // Linux/mac: ping -c 1; Windows: ping -n 1
    const countFlag = process.platform === 'win32' ? '-n' : '-c';
    const cmd = `ping ${countFlag} 1 ${host}`;
    return new Promise((resolve) => {
      exec(cmd, { timeout: 4000 }, (err, stdout, stderr) => {
        resolve({
          host,
          ok: !err,
          rtt: /time[=<]\s*\d+(\.\d+)?\s*ms/i.test(stdout) ? stdout.match(/time[=<]\s*([\d.]+)\s*ms/i)[1] + ' ms' : null,
          raw: (stdout || stderr || '').slice(0, 1000)
        });
      });
    });
  }
}

module.exports = RawrZStandalone;
2) src/engines/rawrz-engine.js

    // Place any lazy module discovery / warmup here if needed.
    // This stub completes immediately.
    return true;
  }
}

3) public/panel.html
<!doctype html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
  <meta charset="utf-8"/>
  <meta http-equiv="x-ua-compatible" content="ie=edge"/>
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1"/>

  <style>

You said:
I want to be able to drop in engines etc and it create the proper gui for using 
ChatGPT said:

Thought for 5s
Absolutely—let’s make the GUI self-building from whatever engines you drop in.

Below is a lightweight, production-friendly pattern that:

lets each engine declare its actions (endpoints + fields) in a tiny manifest,

auto-aggregates them into one /api/manifest endpoint, and

renders a dynamic control panel that builds forms on the fly from that manifest (no manual HTML edits).

You can keep your current security/rate-limit/upload logic unchanged.

1) Engine convention (drop-in)
Each engine file exports:

id, name, version?

actions[]: each action has method, path, summary, inputs[] (with name, type, required, help, maxLength, etc.)

Example: src/engines/crypto-engine.js
'use strict';

// This engine only declares what the GUI needs to render forms.
// Your actual route handlers still live in server.js (or the engine can export handlers if you prefer).
module.exports = {
  id: 'crypto',
  name: 'Crypto',
  version: '1.0.0',
  actions: [
    {
      method: 'POST',
      path: '/api/hash',
      summary: 'Hash text',
      inputs: [
        { name: 'input', type: 'text', required: true, help: 'String to hash', maxLength: 61440 },
        { name: 'algorithm', type: 'select', required: false, help: 'Hash algorithm', options: ['sha256','sha512'] },
        { name: 'save', type: 'checkbox', required: false, help: 'Also save blob' },
        { name: 'extension', type: 'text', required: false, help: 'Optional extension' }
      ]
    },
    {
      method: 'POST',
      path: '/api/encrypt',
      summary: 'Encrypt text',
      inputs: [
        { name: 'input', type: 'text', required: true, help: 'Plaintext', maxLength: 61440 },
        { name: 'algorithm', type: 'select', required: true, options: ['aes-256-gcm','aes-128-cbc'] },
        { name: 'extension', type: 'text', required: false, help: 'Optional extension' }
      ]
    },
    {
      method: 'POST',
      path: '/api/decrypt',
      summary: 'Decrypt text',
      inputs: [
        { name: 'input', type: 'text', required: true, help: 'Base64 ciphertext', maxLength: 61440 },
        { name: 'algorithm', type: 'select', required: true, options: ['aes-256-gcm','aes-128-cbc'] },
        { name: 'key', type: 'text', required: true, help: 'Base64 key' },
        { name: 'iv', type: 'text', required: true, help: 'Base64 IV/nonce' },
        { name: 'extension', type: 'text', required: false, help: 'Optional extension' }
      ]
    }
  ]
};
You can add as many engines as you want (e.g., net-engine.js, files-engine.js)—just export this shape.

2) Engine index that aggregates manifests
src/engines/index.js
'use strict';
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

const enginesDir = __dirname;

function loadEngines() {
  const manifests = [];
  for (const file of fs.readdirSync(enginesDir)) {
    if (file === 'index.js') continue;
    if (!file.endsWith('.js')) continue;
    const mod = require(path.join(enginesDir, file));
    if (mod && mod.id && Array.isArray(mod.actions)) {
      manifests.push({
        id: mod.id,
        name: mod.name || mod.id,
        version: mod.version || '0.0.0',
        actions: mod.actions
      });
    }
  }
  return manifests;
}

module.exports = {
  loadEngines
};
This reads all *.js in src/engines/ and collects their manifests.

3) Add a manifest route in your server.js
Add this one route to your server (safe, read-only; keep your existing security as-is). Place near your other routes:

// --- Manifest (GUI auto-builder uses this) ---
const { loadEngines } = require('./src/engines'); // <— add this import at top with others

app.get('/api/manifest', requireAuth, (_req, res) => {
  try {
    const engines = loadEngines();
    // Optional: you can further filter or sort actions here
    res.json({
      name: 'RawrZ HTTP Platform',
      version: '1.0.0',
      baseUrl: '', // client will use relative URLs
      engines
    });
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[Manifest Error]', e);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to build manifest' });
  }
});
4) Dynamic GUI that renders from /api/manifest
Replace your public/panel.html with this self-rendering UI (keeps your auth token local, never stored server-side):

public/panel.html
<!doctype html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
<meta charset="utf-8"/>
<meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1"/>
<title>RawrZ Control Panel</title>
<style>
  :root { --b:#111827; --fg:#111827; --mut:#6b7280; --bd:#e5e7eb; --bg:#ffffff; --chip:#f3f4f6; }
  body { font-family: ui-sans-serif, system-ui, -apple-system, Segoe UI, Roboto, Ubuntu; margin: 24px; color:var(--fg); background:var(--bg);}
  h1 { margin: 0 0 8px; }
  .mut { color:var(--mut); }
  .row { display:flex; gap:8px; align-items:center; flex-wrap:wrap; }
  .eng { border:1px solid var(--bd); border-radius:12px; padding:16px; margin:16px 0; }
  .card { border:1px solid var(--bd); border-radius:12px; padding:16px; margin:12px 0; }
  .inputs { display:grid; grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fit,minmax(220px,1fr)); gap:12px; }
  label { display:block; font-size:12px; color:var(--mut); margin-bottom:6px; }
  input[type="text"], input[type="number"], textarea, select {
    width:100%; padding:8px 10px; border:1px solid var(--bd); border-radius:10px; font-family:inherit;
  }
  textarea { min-height: 84px; }
  button { padding:8px 12px; border-radius:10px; border:1px solid var(--bd); background:#111827; color:white; cursor:pointer; }
  .chip { display:inline-block; background:var(--chip); border-radius:999px; padding:4px 10px; font-size:12px; }
  pre { background:#0b1020; color:#d4d4d4; padding:12px; border-radius:10px; overflow:auto; }
  .rowsp { display:flex; align-items:center; justify-content:space-between; gap:8px; }
  .err { color:#b91c1c; font-weight:600; }
</style>
</head>
<body>
  <div class="rowsp">
    <div>
      <h1>RawrZ Control Panel</h1>
      <div class="mut">Auto-generated from <code>/api/manifest</code></div>
    </div>
    <div class="row">
      <label class="mut">Auth Token</label>
      <input id="auth" type="text" placeholder="Bearer token" style="min-width:320px"/>
      <button onclick="storeAuth()">Save</button>
    </div>
  </div>

  <div class="card">
    <div class="row" style="gap:12px">
      <span class="chip"><a href="/health" target="_blank" style="color:inherit;text-decoration:none">GET /health</a></span>
      <span class="chip"><a href="/static/panel.html" target="_blank" style="color:inherit;text-decoration:none">/panel</a></span>
    </div>
  </div>

  <div id="container"></div>

  <script>
  const $ = sel => document.querySelector(sel);
  const container = $("#container");

  // Persist auth token locally
  const LS_KEY = 'rawrz_auth';
  function storeAuth() {
    localStorage.setItem(LS_KEY, $("#auth").value.trim());
  }
  (function restoreAuth(){
    const t = localStorage.getItem(LS_KEY);
    if (t) $("#auth").value = t;
  })();

  function fieldToInput(f) {
    const id = `f_${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2)}`;
    let el;
    const base = document.createElement('div');
    const label = document.createElement('label');
    label.textContent = `${f.name}${f.required ? ' *' : ''}`;
    if (f.help) { label.title = f.help; }
    base.appendChild(label);

    const common = (node) => {
      node.name = f.name;
      if (f.placeholder) node.placeholder = f.placeholder;
      if (f.maxLength) node.maxLength = f.maxLength;
      return node;
    };

    if (f.type === 'textarea' || (f.type === 'text' && (f.multiline || f.maxLength > 2000))) {
      el = common(document.createElement('textarea'));
    } else if (f.type === 'select' && Array.isArray(f.options)) {
      el = common(document.createElement('select'));
      for (const opt of f.options) {
        const o = document.createElement('option');
        if (typeof opt === 'string') { o.value = opt; o.textContent = opt; }
        else { o.value = opt.value; o.textContent = opt.label || opt.value; }
        el.appendChild(o);
      }
    } else if (f.type === 'checkbox') {
      el = common(document.createElement('input'));
      el.type = 'checkbox';
    } else {
      el = common(document.createElement('input'));
      el.type = f.type || 'text';
    }
    base.appendChild(el);
    return base;
  }

  async function callEndpoint(action, payload, token) {
    const headers = { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' };
    if (token) headers['Authorization'] = 'Bearer ' + token;
    const r = await fetch(action.path, {
      method: action.method || 'POST',
      headers,
      body: action.method === 'GET' ? undefined : JSON.stringify(payload)
    });
    const text = await r.text();
    let json;
    try { json = JSON.parse(text); } catch { /* not json */ }
    return { ok: r.ok, status: r.status, body: json || text };
  }

  function renderAction(engine, action) {
    const wrap = document.createElement('div');
    wrap.className = 'card';

    const title = document.createElement('div');
    title.className = 'rowsp';
    title.innerHTML = `
      <div><strong>${action.summary || action.path}</strong>
        <div class="mut">${action.method || 'POST'} <code>${action.path}</code></div></div>
      <div class="row"><span class="chip">${engine.name}</span></div>`;
    wrap.appendChild(title);

    const form = document.createElement('form');
    form.className = 'inputs';
    for (const f of (action.inputs || [])) {
      form.appendChild(fieldToInput(f));
    }

    const runRow = document.createElement('div');
    runRow.className = 'row';
    runRow.style.marginTop = '10px';
    const btn = document.createElement('button');
    btn.type = 'button';
    btn.textContent = 'Run';
    runRow.appendChild(btn);
    const status = document.createElement('span');
    status.className = 'mut';
    runRow.appendChild(status);
    wrap.appendChild(form);
    wrap.appendChild(runRow);

    const out = document.createElement('pre');
    out.textContent = '';
    wrap.appendChild(out);

    btn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
      status.textContent = '…';
      const token = $("#auth").value.trim();
      const payload = {};
      for (const el of form.querySelectorAll('input, textarea, select')) {
        if (el.type === 'checkbox') payload[el.name] = el.checked;
        else payload[el.name] = el.value;
      }
      // Basic required check
      const missing = (action.inputs || []).filter(f => f.required && !(payload[f.name] ?? '').toString().trim());
      if (missing.length) {
        status.innerHTML = '<span class="err">Missing required: ' + missing.map(m => m.name).join(', ') + '</span>';
        return;
      }
      try {
        const res = await callEndpoint(action, payload, token);
        status.textContent = res.ok ? `OK (${res.status})` : `ERR (${res.status})`;
        out.textContent = typeof res.body === 'string' ? res.body : JSON.stringify(res.body, null, 2);
      } catch (e) {
        status.innerHTML = '<span class="err">Request failed</span>';
        out.textContent = String(e);
      }
    });

    return wrap;
  }

  async function bootstrap() {
    const token = $("#auth").value.trim();
    const headers = token ? { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token } : {};
    const r = await fetch('/api/manifest', { headers });
    if (!r.ok) {
      container.innerHTML = `<div class="card"><span class="err">Failed to fetch manifest (${r.status}). Ensure you entered a valid token.</span></div>`;
      return;
    }
    const manifest = await r.json();

    const head = document.createElement('div');
    head.className = 'card';
    head.innerHTML = `
      <div class="row"><div><strong>${manifest.name || 'RawrZ HTTP Platform'}</strong></div>
      <span class="mut">${manifest.version || ''}</span></div>`;
    container.appendChild(head);

    (manifest.engines || []).forEach(engine => {
      const ewrap = document.createElement('div');
      ewrap.className = 'eng';
      const h = document.createElement('div');
      h.className = 'rowsp';
      h.innerHTML = `<div><h2 style="margin:0">${engine.name || engine.id}</h2>
                      <div class="mut">${engine.id}${engine.version ? ' • v'+engine.version : ''}</div></div>`;
      ewrap.appendChild(h);

      (engine.actions || []).forEach(a => ewrap.appendChild(renderAction(engine, a)));
      container.appendChild(ewrap);
    });
  }

  // Auto-load once token (if any) is present
  bootstrap();
  </script>
</body>
</html>
What this does

Reads /api/manifest (auth required)

Builds a clean form per action

Sends JSON to each endpoint with your Authorization header

Pretty-prints responses

5) Optional: generator to create manifests from code comments (if you don’t want to hand-write them)
If your engines already have JSDoc-style comments, you can auto-generate manifests:

tools/generate-manifest.mjs
#!/usr/bin/env node
import fs from 'fs';
import path from 'path';
import { fileURLToPath } from 'url';

const __dirname = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url));
const enginesDir = path.join(__dirname, '..', 'src', 'engines');
const outFile = path.join(enginesDir, 'generated.manifest.json');

// VERY minimal parser: looks for lines like:
// @action POST /api/hash - Hash text
// @param input text required "String to hash"
// @param algorithm select optional "Hash algorithm" [sha256,sha512]
// @param save checkbox optional "save to disk"
function parseFile(filePath) {
  const raw = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8');
  const id = path.basename(filePath).replace(/\.js$/,'');
  const actions = [];

  const blocks = raw.split('\n').reduce((acc, line) => {
    if (line.includes('@action')) acc.push([line]);
    else if (acc.length) acc[acc.length-1].push(line);
    return acc;
  }, []);

  for (const lines of blocks) {
    const head = lines[0].match(/@action\s+(\w+)\s+(\S+)\s*-\s*(.+)$/);
    if (!head) continue;
    const [, method, route, summary] = head;

    const inputs = [];
    for (const l of lines.slice(1)) {
      const m = l.match(/@param\s+(\w+)\s+(\w+)\s+(required|optional)\s+"([^"]*)"(?:\s*\[([^\]]+)\])?/);
      if (m) {
        const [, name, type, req, help, opts] = m;
        const input = { name, type, required: req === 'required', help };
        if (opts) input.options = opts.split(',').map(s => s.trim());
        inputs.push(input);
      }
    }
    actions.push({ method, path: route, summary, inputs });
  }

  return { id, name: id, actions };
}

function main() {
  const manifests = [];
  for (const f of fs.readdirSync(enginesDir)) {
    if (f === 'index.js') continue;
    const p = path.join(enginesDir, f);
    if (fs.statSync(p).isFile() && f.endsWith('.js')) {
      const parsed = parseFile(p);
      if (parsed.actions?.length) manifests.push(parsed);
    }
  }
  fs.writeFileSync(outFile, JSON.stringify({ engines: manifests }, null, 2));
  console.log(`[OK] Wrote ${outFile}`);
}

main();
You can then have src/engines/index.js merge the hand-written manifests and the generated.manifest.json if present.

Update src/engines/index.js to merge:
'use strict';
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

const enginesDir = __dirname;

function loadEngines() {
  const manifests = [];

  // Load code-defined manifests
  for (const file of fs.readdirSync(enginesDir)) {
    if (file === 'index.js' || file === 'generated.manifest.json') continue;
    if (!file.endsWith('.js')) continue;
    const mod = require(path.join(enginesDir, file));
    if (mod && mod.id && Array.isArray(mod.actions)) {
      manifests.push({ id: mod.id, name: mod.name || mod.id, version: mod.version || '0.0.0', actions: mod.actions });
    }
  }

  // Merge generator output if exists
  const genPath = path.join(enginesDir, 'generated.manifest.json');
  if (fs.existsSync(genPath)) {
    try {
      const gen = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(genPath, 'utf8'));
      for (const e of (gen.engines || [])) {
        // If already exists, append/merge actions:
        const existing = manifests.find(x => x.id === e.id);
        if (existing) existing.actions.push(...(e.actions || []));
        else manifests.push(e);
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.warn('[Manifest] Failed to read generated.manifest.json:', e.message);
    }
  }

  return manifests;
}

module.exports = { loadEngines };

Drop-in engines with a tiny manifest = GUI updates instantly.

/api/manifest = single source of truth the panel uses.

Keep your strict server security (auth, rate limit, validations).

Optional JSDoc scanner if you prefer inline annotations to separate manifest files.

Perfect! Let me create the complete generator that builds a self-updating GUI from your engines. I'll update the scaffold tool to include all the GUI components and the dynamic manifest system.

javascript:tools/scaffold-infra.mjs
#!/usr/bin/env node
/* Infra Generator + Dynamic GUI Builder
 * Creates Dockerfile, Compose, systemd, CI, K8s, Makefile, README, ignores, uploads/.gitkeep,
 * and (optionally) writes a production-ready server.js with dynamic GUI that auto-builds from engines.
 */
import fs from 'fs/promises';
import fssync from 'fs';
import path from 'path';
import process from 'process';
import { fileURLToPath } from 'url';

const __dirname = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url));

// ------------- args -------------
const argv = Object.create(null);
for (let i = 2; i < process.argv.length; i++) {
  const a = process.argv[i];
  if (!a.startsWith('--')) continue;
  const [k, v = 'true'] = a.slice(2).split('=');
  argv[k] = v === 'true' || v === 'false' ? (v === 'true') : v;
}
const FORCE = !!argv.force;
const WRITE_SERVER = !!argv['write-server'];
const APP_NAME = (argv.name || 'rawrz-http').toString();
const DOMAIN = (argv.domain || 'rawrz.example.com').toString();
const REGISTRY = (argv.registry || `ghcr.io/your-org/${APP_NAME}`).toString();

// ------------- detect existing server.js -------------
const repoRoot = process.cwd();
const serverPath = path.join(repoRoot, 'server.js');
const hasExisting = fssync.existsSync(serverPath);
let serverSrc = '';
if (hasExisting) serverSrc = await fs.readFile(serverPath, 'utf8');

// Port detection
const portMatchEnv = serverSrc.match(/process\.env\.PORT\s*\|\|\s*['"]?(\d+)['"]?/);
const portMatchListen = serverSrc.match(/\.listen\s*\(\s*(\d{2,5})\s*,/);
const PORT = Number(portMatchEnv?.[1] || portMatchListen?.[1] || 8080);

// AUTH detection
const USES_AUTH = /process\.env\.AUTH_TOKEN/.test(serverSrc) || WRITE_SERVER;

// compression + download path detection
const hasCompression = /compression\(/.test(serverSrc);
const downloadPath = (serverSrc.match(/app\.get\(['"]([^'"]*\/download)[^'"]*['"]/i)?.[1]) || '/api/download');

// ensure uploads
const uploadsDir = path.join(repoRoot, 'uploads');
await fs.mkdir(uploadsDir, { recursive: true }).catch(() => {});
const gitkeep = path.join(uploadsDir, '.gitkeep');
if (!fssync.existsSync(gitkeep)) await fs.writeFile(gitkeep, '');

// helpers
const ensureDir = async (p) => fs.mkdir(p, { recursive: true });
const writeFile = async (file, content) => {
  if (!FORCE && fssync.existsSync(file)) {
    console.log(`↷ Skipped (exists): ${path.relative(repoRoot, file)}`);
    return;
  }
  await ensureDir(path.dirname(file));
  await fs.writeFile(file, content);
  console.log(`✓ Wrote: ${path.relative(repoRoot, file)}`);
};

// ------------- templates -------------
const T_gitignore = () => `
node_modules/
npm-debug.log*
yarn-error.log
coverage/
dist/

.env

uploads/*
!uploads/.gitkeep

.DS_Store
Thumbs.db
`;

const T_dockerignore = () => `
node_modules
npm-debug.log*
.git
.github
coverage
dist
.env
uploads
Dockerfile
docker-compose.yml
`;

const T_Dockerfile = () => `# Generated for ${APP_NAME}
FROM node:20-slim

WORKDIR /app

RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends dumb-init \\
 && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*

COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm ci --only=production

COPY . .

RUN mkdir -p /app/uploads && chown -R node:node /app/uploads

USER node

EXPOSE ${PORT}
ENV NODE_ENV=production

CMD ["dumb-init", "node", "server.js"]
`;

const T_compose = () => `version: "3.9"
services:
  ${APP_NAME}:
    build: .
    image: ${APP_NAME}:latest
    container_name: ${APP_NAME}
    restart: always
    env_file: .env
    ports:
      - "${PORT}:${PORT}"
    volumes:
      - ./uploads:/app/uploads
`;

const T_makefile = () => `IMAGE ?= ${APP_NAME}:latest
PORT ?= ${PORT}

.PHONY: build run stop push audit clean

build:
\tdocker build -t $(IMAGE) .

run:
\tdocker run --rm -p $(PORT):${PORT} --env-file .env -v $$PWD/uploads:/app/uploads $(IMAGE)

stop:
\tdocker stop ${APP_NAME} || true

push:

audit:
\tnpm ci --omit=dev && npm audit --audit-level=high || true

clean:

const T_ci = () => `name: CI

  pull_request:

jobs:

    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: 20
      - run: npm ci
      - run: npm test || echo "No tests yet"

  docker:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    if: github.event_name == 'push'
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: docker/setup-buildx-action@v3
      - uses: docker/login-action@v3
        with:
          registry: ghcr.io
          username: \${{ github.actor }}
          password: \${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
      - uses: docker/build-push-action@v5
        with:
          context: .
          push: true
          tags: ${REGISTRY}:latest
`;

// README (summarized)
const T_readme = () => `# ${APP_NAME}

Generated production bundle with dynamic GUI that auto-builds from your engines.

- Port: ${PORT}
- Auth token required: ${USES_AUTH ? 'Yes' : 'Not detected'}
- Compression in app: ${hasCompression ? 'Detected' : 'Not detected'}
- Download route: \`${downloadPath}\`

## Quickstart

\`\`\`bash
npm ci
cp .env.example .env  # set AUTH_TOKEN
node server.js
\`\`\`

## Dynamic GUI

The control panel at \`/panel\` automatically builds forms from engine manifests in \`src/engines/\`.

Each engine exports:
\`\`\`js
module.exports = {
  id: 'crypto',
  name: 'Crypto',
  version: '1.0.0',
  actions: [
    {
      method: 'POST',
      path: '/api/hash',
      summary: 'Hash text',
      inputs: [
        { name: 'input', type: 'text', required: true, help: 'String to hash', maxLength: 61440 },
        { name: 'algorithm', type: 'select', required: false, options: ['sha256','sha512'] }
      ]
    }
  ]
};
\`\`\`

The GUI will auto-render forms for each action. Just drop in new engines and refresh!
